### [50] [Origins of the UV continuum and Balmer emission lines in Little Red Dots: observational validation of dense gas envelope models enshrouding the AGN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.10573)
*Yoshihisa Asada,Kohei Inayoshi,Qinyue Fei,Seiji Fujimoto,Chris Willott*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (94/100) - 该论文聚焦于JWST观测的‘小红点’（LRDs）高红移活动星系核，核心研究UV连续谱与Hα发射线的起源，涉及稠密气体包层、星暴星系等主题，与用户兴趣画像中的JWST、稠密气体、恒星形成星系、星暴星系高度匹配。作者中包含用户核心作者seiji fujimoto和kohei inayoshi，且论文方法（JWST/NIRSpec光谱分析）与用户常用手段一致。论文主题与用户强引力透镜领域虽无直接重叠，但高红移星系物理、稠密气体、AGN演化等方向与用户兴趣高度相关，且用户明确要求优先考虑高红移星系动力学、多相气体等方向，因此给予高分。

TL;DR: 该研究通过JWST/NIRSpec数据分析了"小红点"（LRDs）的UV连续谱和窄/宽发射线起源，发现LRDs中的UV和Hα发射主要来自年轻大质量恒星而非活动星系核，支持LRDs是中心黑洞被稠密气体包层包裹的短寿命快速生长阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究新发现的"小红点"（LRDs）类活动星系核中UV连续谱和窄/宽发射线的起源，理解这些天体与普通AGN的差异及其在黑洞早期演化中的作用。

Method: 利用所有存档的JWST/NIRSpec数据，构建了28个红移5-7.2的光谱确认LRDs样本，要求具有宽Hα发射、蓝色UV颜色、V形连续谱和致密形态。同时定义了9个没有红色光学连续谱的蓝色致密宽线AGN作为对照样本（LBDs），分析UV与窄/宽Hα光度之间的相关性。

Result: 在LRDs中，窄和宽Hα分量都与UV连续谱紧密相关，光度比与年轻星暴星系一致；而LBDs中的UV到宽Hα比与本地未遮蔽AGN匹配，且与LRDs有统计差异。Lyα出现率和强度在两类天体中没有差异，与正常恒星形成星系相当。

Conclusion: 结果支持LRDs中心黑洞被稠密不透明气体包层包裹的模型：UV连续谱以及窄甚至宽Hα发射主要由包层周围的年轻大质量恒星提供，而非AGN本身。随着包层消散，直接AGN辐射可能显现，LRDs可能转变为LBDs，标志着黑洞快速生长的短寿命阶段结束。

Abstract: We present a statistical study on the origins of the UV continuum and narrow/broad emission lines in little red dots (LRDs), a newly discovered class of active galactic nuclei (AGNs). Leveraging all archived JWST/NIRSpec data, we build a sample of 28 spectroscopically-confirmed LRDs at $5<z_{\rm spec}<7.2$, by requiring broad H$α$ emission, blue UV colors, V-shaped continua, and compact morphologies. We define a control sample of 9 blue, compact, broad-line AGNs without red optical continua (hereafter little blue dots; LBDs), and examine correlations between rest UV and the narrow/broad H$α$ luminosities in these populations. In LRDs, both narrow and broad H$α$ components are tightly correlated with the UV continuum, and the luminosity ratios are consistent with those in young starburst galaxies. In contrast, the UV to broad H$α$ ratios in LBDs closely match local unobscured AGNs and are statistically different from LRDs. The Ly$α$ occurrence rates and strengths do not differ between LRDs and LBDs and are comparable to normal star-forming galaxies. These results are consistent with a scenario where the central BH in LRDs is enshrouded by a dense opaque gas envelope -- in this model, the UV continuum as well as narrow and even broad H$α$ emissions are not powered by AGNs but predominantly by young massive stars surrounding the envelope, while the envelope radiates as a $\sim 5000$ K blackbody. As the envelope dissipates, direct AGN emission can emerge, potentially transforming LRDs into LBDs and marking the end of a short-lived phase of rapid black hole growth.

Abstract Translation:
我们对小红点（LRDs）中紫外连续谱和窄/宽发射线的起源进行了统计研究，LRDs是一类新发现的活跃星系核（AGNs）。利用所有存档的JWST/NIRSpec数据，我们构建了一个包含28个光谱证认的LRDs样本，红移范围为$5<z_{\rm spec}<7.2$，要求具有宽Hα发射、蓝色紫外颜色、V形连续谱和致密形态。我们定义了一个由9个蓝色、致密、宽发射线AGN组成的对照样本，这些AGN没有红色光学连续谱（以下简称小蓝点；LBDs），并研究了这些天体静止系紫外光度与窄/宽Hα光度之间的相关性。在LRDs中，窄和宽Hα分量均与紫外连续谱紧密相关，其光度比与年轻星暴星系中的一致。相比之下，LBDs中紫外与宽Hα的光度比与本地未遮蔽AGN的比值非常接近，并且在统计上与LRDs不同。Lyα出现率和强度在LRDs和LBDs之间没有差异，且与正常恒星形成星系相当。这些结果与中心黑洞被稠密不透明气体包层包裹的情景一致——在该模型中，紫外连续谱以及窄甚至宽Hα发射并非由AGN提供能量，而是主要由包层周围的年轻大质量恒星主导，而包层则表现为一个约5000 K的黑体辐射。随着包层消散，直接的AGN辐射可能显现，从而可能将LRDs转变为LBDs，标志着黑洞快速生长的短寿命阶段结束。

Conclusion Translation:
结果支持LRDs中心黑洞被稠密不透明气体包层包裹的模型：UV连续谱以及窄甚至宽Hα发射主要由包层周围的年轻大质量恒星提供，而非AGN本身。随着包层消散，直接AGN辐射可能显现，LRDs可能转变为LBDs，标志着黑洞快速生长的短寿命阶段结束。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.10573v4/figures/schematic_pics.png)

图1：文献中提出的LRDs的AGN+稠密气体包层模型（也称为BH*模型）示意图。(a) K. Inayoshi et al. ( 2025a ) 提出了一个模型，其中中心BH被厚气体包层包裹。由于其光学厚度，来自AGN吸积的辐射无法逃逸，包层被热化并作为黑体被观测到。在该模型中，所有紫外光、窄线和宽线均由包层周围的年轻大质量恒星提供能量，而静止光学连续谱则由热辐射解释。(b) 最初由R. P. Naidu et al. ( 2025 ) 提出的茧状包层模型在中心BH周围有一个分层茧。宽线起源于内层，由吸积盘照亮，并经过外层多次散射后泄漏出来。茧对紫外连续谱是光学厚的，LRDs中的紫外光和窄线需要由宿主星系发射。该模型中的静止光学连续谱要么源于茧对Balmer极限光子的吸收，要么源于被AGN吸积加热的茧的热辐射。(c) 当中心BH周围的稠密包层不是球对称且对极轴方向不是光学厚时（例如，X. Lin et al., 2025 ），所有紫外光、窄线和宽线都可以来自AGN吸积。这与标准AGN图像类似，但缺少尘埃环，取而代之的是一个非球对称包层，该包层在静止光学波段发射黑体热辐射。

<small>Figure 1: Schematic pictures of AGN+dense gas envelope models (also known as BH* models) for LRDs proposed in literature. (a) K. Inayoshi et al. ( 2025a ) proposed a model where the central BH is enshrouded by thick gas envelope. Since its optically thickness, no radiation from the AGN accretion can be escaped, and the envelope is thermalized and observed as a blackbody. In this model, all UV light, narrow lines, and broad lines are powered by young massive stars surrounding the envelope, and the rest optical continuum is explained by the thermal emission. (b) the cocoon envelope model originally proposed by R. P. Naidu et al. ( 2025 ) has a layered cocoon around the central BH. The broad lines are originated from the inner layer, which is illuminated by the accretion disk, and leak out after multiple scatterings through the outer layer. The cocoon is optically thick for UV continuum, and the UV light and narrow line in LRDs needs to be emitted from host galaxies. The rest optical continuum in this model originated either from the Balmer limit photon absorption by the cocoon or from the thermal emission of the cocoon heated by the AGN accretion. (c) when the dense envelope around the central BH is not spherical and is not optically thick towards the polar axis (e.g., X. Lin et al., 2025 ) , all UV light, narrow, and broad lines can be from the AGN accretion. This is similar to the standard AGN picture, but it lacks the dust torus and instead has a non-spherical envelope which emits blackbody thermal emission in the rest optical.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.10573v4/x1.png)

图2：本工作中的样本选择。(a) 我们从光谱证认的宽Hα发射体中选择具有V形连续谱的LRDs，红移范围为5 (M. V. Maseda et al., 2024 ) 。顶部面板展示了NIRSpec/棱镜光谱，底部面板显示了Lyα（左）和Hα（右）线轮廓。对于Lyα线，最佳拟合线轮廓以蓝色实线曲线显示，而仅连续谱拟合模型以虚线曲线显示。对于Hα线，显示了窄、未分辨分量拟合（橙色）和宽+窄分量拟合（蓝色）的最佳拟合线轮廓，并在下方子面板中给出了每种情况的噪声归一化残差。(c) 与面板(b)相同，但针对一个LBDs的示例，该示例取自RUBIES计划（A. de Graaff et al., 2025b ）的一部分。

<small>Figure 2: Sample selection in this work. (a) we select LRDs with V-shaped continua from spectroscopically-confirmed broad H \(\alpha\) line emitters at \(5 (M. V. Maseda et al., 2024 ) . The top panel presents the NIRSpec/Prism spectrum, and the bottom panel shows the Ly \(\alpha\) (left) and H \(\alpha\) (right) line profile. For the Ly \(\alpha\) line, the best-fit line profile is shown with the blue solid curve, while the continuum-only fit model is with the dashed curve. For the H \(\alpha\) line, the best-fit line profiles with narrow, unresolved component fit (orange) and broad+narrow components fit (blue) are shown, and the noise-normalized residual for each case is presented in the lower sub-panel. (c) same as panel (b) but for an example of the LBDs, taken as part of the RUBIES program (A. de Graaff et al., 2025b ) .</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2601.10573v4/x3.png)

图3：LRDs（顶部）和LBDs（底部）中静止系紫外光度与Hα线光度的关系。左侧和右侧分别显示宽分量和窄分量。绘图按Balmer跳变强度进行颜色编码，定义为\(f_{\nu,4230}/f_{\nu,3560}\)。作为参考，还显示了年轻星暴星系（黑色虚线）和典型1型AGN（红色实线）的紫外与Hα光度比。灰色阴影带显示了年轻恒星形成星系中恒星年龄和气体密度变化时光度比的范围。

<small>Figure 3: Rest UV versus H \(\alpha\) line luminosity in LRDs (top) and LBDs (bottom). Broad and narrow components are displayed on the left and right, respectively. Plots are color-coded by the Balmer break strength, defined as \(f_{\nu,4230}/f_{\nu,3560}\) . As a reference, the UV-to-H \(\alpha\) luminosity ratios for young starburst galaxies (black dotted line) and typical Type 1 AGNs (red solid line) are also shown. The gray shaded band shows the range of the luminosity ratio when the stellar age and gas density is varied for young star-forming galaxies.</small>

#### Figure 4
表1：紫外与Hα光度比† † 脚注文本：\(\star\) 引用样本中的中位数值。标准差作为不确定性引用。† † 脚注文本：\(\dagger\) 根据D. E. Vanden Berk et al. ( 2001 ) 的本地1型AGN汇编光谱测量。† † 脚注文本：\(\dagger\dagger\) 根据BPASS+Cloudy光电离建模估算。该比值在星云/恒星条件不同假设下的可能范围作为不确定性引用。

<small>Figure 6: The effect of different size-luminosity relation on the BH mass estimation. Plots are color-coded by the blackbody temperature ( \(T_{BB}\) ). It demonstrates that using the typical \(R_{BLR}\) - \(L\) relation can overestimate the BH mass by \(\sim 1\) dex due to the different \(R_{BLR}\) estimations.</small>

### [51] [Baryonic mass budgets in the central regions of the Bullet Cluster and their consistency with strong lensing in MOND](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19454)
*Dong Zhang,Hosein Haghi,Elena Asencio,Indranil Banik,Akram Hasani Zonoozi,Sangjun Cha,Boseong Young Cho,Hyungjin Joo,Pavel Kroupa,Anastasia Lazutkina,Eda Gjergo*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 论文直接涉及强引力透镜（strong lensing）和暗物质（dark matter），与用户的核心兴趣高度吻合。虽然MOND并非用户主要关注点，但论文通过强透镜约束重子质量分布，与用户对星系动力学和暗物质的研究方向紧密相关。

TL;DR: 子弹头星团的强引力透镜观测传统上被视为暗物质的强证据和对MOND理论的挑战。本文利用IGIMF理论重新估计了星团核心区的重子质量，发现MOND强透镜质量落在IGIMF模型预测范围内，表明在IGIMF框架下重子质量预算与MOND要求一致，但剩余物质的空间分布和动力学行为仍需验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 子弹头星团的强透镜观测一直被视为暗物质存在的关键证据，同时对MOND理论构成重大挑战。作者希望检验MOND是否能在修正的重子质量估计下解释观测结果。

Method: 利用IGIMF理论，通过恒星族合成模型分别采用恒定金属丰度和自增丰金属丰度，对子弹头星团三个最亮星系团星系（BCG）核心区域的重子质量进行重新估计，并与MOND强透镜质量进行比较。

Result: 三个核心区域的MOND强透镜质量均落在IGIMF模型预测的质量范围内，表明IGIMF框架下的重子质量预算与MOND要求一致。

Conclusion: IGIMF理论可能使MOND在子弹头星团核心区与观测一致，但需进一步验证剩余物质的空间分布和动力学行为。更广泛而言，无论MOND是否成立，结果意味着所需暗物质可能少于先前推断。

Abstract: Strong lensing observations of the Bullet Cluster have traditionally been regarded as strong evidence for dark matter and a major challenge to Milgromian dynamics (MOND). The offset between the lensing mass and the X-ray gas centroids implies a substantial amount of unseen mass near the brightest cluster galaxies (BCGs). However, the high metallicities observed in both the intracluster gas and the massive early-type member galaxies suggest a past stellar population dominated by massive stars, whose evolved remnants contribute additional baryonic mass. This effect is naturally incorporated in the integrated galaxy-wide initial mass function (IGIMF) theory, which predicts substantially larger baryonic masses than a canonical IMF. In this work, we re-estimate the baryonic masses of the three BCG-centred core regions of the Bullet Cluster and compare them with MOND strong-lensing masses. We derive IGIMF masses using stellar population synthesis models with constant and (self-) enriched metallicities, representing lower and upper mass limits, respectively. We find that the MOND strong-lensing masses of all three cores lie within the range predicted by the IGIMF models. These results suggest that the baryonic mass budget inferred under the IGIMF framework is consistent with MOND requirements in the core regions of the Bullet Cluster. However, the physical viability of this scenario also depends on the spatial distribution and dynamical behavior of the remnant population, which remain to be established. More generally, regardless of the validity of MOND, the results imply that less dark matter may be required than previously inferred.

Abstract Translation:
子弹头星团的强透镜观测传统上被视为暗物质存在的有力证据，也是对米尔格罗姆动力学（MOND）的重大挑战。透镜质量与X射线气体质心之间的偏移表明，在 brightest 星团星系（BCGs）附近存在大量不可见质量。然而，在星团内气体和大型早型成员星系中观测到的高金属丰度表明，过去恒星群体以大质量恒星为主，其演化后的残骸贡献了额外的重子质量。这一效应自然地包含在集成星系初始质量函数（IGIMF）理论中，该理论预测的重子质量比标准IMF显著更大。在本工作中，我们重新估计了子弹头星团三个以BCG为中心的核心区域的重子质量，并将其与MOND强透镜质量进行比较。我们使用恒星种群合成模型推导IGIMF质量，分别采用恒定金属丰度和（自）富集金属丰度，代表质量下限和上限。我们发现，所有三个核心的MOND强透镜质量均落在IGIMF模型预测的范围内。这些结果表明，在IGIMF框架下推断的重子质量预算与子弹头星团核心区域的MOND要求一致。然而，这一情景的物理可行性还取决于残骸种群的空间分布和动力学行为，这仍有待确定。更广泛而言，无论MOND是否成立，这些结果意味着所需暗物质可能少于先前推断。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有总结：IGIMF理论可能使MOND在子弹头星团核心区与观测一致，但需进一步验证剩余物质的空间分布和动力学行为。更广泛而言，无论MOND是否成立，结果意味着所需暗物质可能少于先前推断。

### [52] [Resolving the Multiphase Outflow, Shock Signatures, and PAHs in the AGN-Starburst Composite ULIRG F10565+2448 with JWST MIRI/MRS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.03016)
*Kylie Yui Dan,Jerome Seebeck,Sylvain Veilleux,David Rupke,Eduardo Gonzalez-Alfonso,Ismael Garcia-Bernete,Weizhe Liu,Dieter Lutz,Marcio Melendez,Miguel Pereira Santaella,Eckhard Sturm,Francesco Tombesi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 该论文研究超亮红外星系中的多相外流，使用JWST MIRI MRS数据，涉及分子气体、星暴和AGN反馈，与用户Zotero画像中的核心主题（starburst、molecular gas、JWST）高度匹配，且作者中包含用户核心作者Dieter Lutz。论文聚焦于星系级外流的气体运动学和物理性质，与用户对高红移星系动力学和气体研究的兴趣方向一致。

TL;DR: 利用JWST MIRI MRS观测了超亮红外星系F10565+2448，发现了未分辨的核区外流（电离和分子气体）以及分辨的kpc尺度暖分子外流，分析了PAH特征和激波诊断，支持该星系是AGN-星暴复合体的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了深入理解超亮红外星系中星系级外流的多相气体性质、能量来源（AGN vs 星暴）以及反馈机制对星系演化的影响。

Method: 使用JWST MIRI MRS积分场光谱数据，通过分析气体运动学（速度分布）、温度诊断（H₂转动温度）、[Fe II] 5.34 μm/Pfα激波诊断以及PAH特征（电离态和粒径）的径向分布来研究外流性质。

Result: 发现未分辨的暖电离气体外流速度达-520 km/s，暖分子外流速度-150 km/s；分辨的kpc尺度暖分子外流速度-280到-110 km/s，低于逃逸速度（≥300 km/s）；外流区温度（507 K）高于盘区（329 K）；PAH电离和粒径随半径先减后增。

Conclusion: F10565+2448是一个AGN-星暴复合体星系，其外流能量学需要同时由恒星形成和AGN活动驱动，且暖分子外流可能无法完全逃逸出星系势阱，更多表现为再循环或喷泉模式。

Abstract: We present new James Webb Space Telescope Mid-Infrared Instrument (MIRI) Medium-Resolution Spectrometer (MRS) observations of the nearby ultra-luminous infrared galaxy F10565+2448. These integral field spectroscopic data reveal an unresolved nuclear outflow in both warm-ionized and warm-molecular gas phases as well as a resolved blueshifted kpc-scale warm-molecular outflow. The unresolved warm-ionized outflow has a mean projected velocity up to $-520$ km/s, while the unresolved warm-molecular outflow is slower at $-150$ km/s. For the resolved warm-molecular outflow, the projected mean velocity ($-280 < v_{50} < -110$ km/s) is only slightly faster than the velocity of the disk ($-70 < v_{50} < 120$ km/s) and as such likely does not exceed the estimated escape velocity of $\gtrsim 300$ km/s. The warm-molecular outflow is slightly hotter ($507 \pm 25$K) than the disk ($329 \pm 5$K), and displays areas of higher temperature and lower column density that may indicate a shock front, which we explore using the [Fe II] 5.34 $μ$m/Pf$α$ shock diagnostic. Analysis of the polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbon features reveal trends of ionization and grain size that first decrease with radius up to 1 kpc before increasing up to 3 kpc. These results bolster the picture of F10565+2448 being an AGN-starburst composite where both star formation and AGN-powered phenomena are required to explain the outflow energetics.

Abstract Translation:
我们展示了新的詹姆斯·韦伯空间望远镜中红外仪器（MIRI）中分辨率光谱仪（MRS）对邻近超亮红外星系F10565+2448的观测数据。这些积分场光谱数据揭示了在暖电离和暖分子气体相中均存在未分辨的核外流，以及一个分辨的、蓝移的千秒差距尺度暖分子外流。未分辨的暖电离外流平均投影速度高达$-520$ km/s，而未分辨的暖分子外流较慢，为$-150$ km/s。对于分辨的暖分子外流，其投影平均速度（$-280 < v_{50} < -110$ km/s）仅略快于盘的速度（$-70 < v_{50} < 120$ km/s），因此可能未超过估计的逃逸速度（$\gtrsim 300$ km/s）。暖分子外流温度略高（$507 \pm 25$K），高于盘的温度（$329 \pm 5$K），并显示出较高温度和较低柱密度的区域，这可能指示激波前沿，我们利用[Fe II] 5.34 $μ$m/Pf$α$激波诊断进行了探索。对多环芳烃特征的分析揭示了电离度和晶粒尺寸的趋势，这些趋势先随半径增加至1 kpc而减小，然后增加至3 kpc。这些结果强化了F10565+2448是一个活动星系核-星暴复合体的图像，其中恒星形成和活动星系核驱动的现象都需要用来解释外流能量学。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，F10565+2448是一个AGN-星暴复合体星系，其外流能量学需要同时由恒星形成和AGN活动驱动，且暖分子外流可能无法完全逃逸出星系势阱，更多表现为再循环或喷泉模式。

( 2025 ) , emission lines, and the 6.1 \(\mu\) m optical depth feature from water ice. The fitted attenuation at 9.6 \(\mu\) m of the cool, warm, and hot dust components as well as the water ice are respectively \(\tau_{{cool}}\sim 5.19\) , \(\tau_{{warm}}\sim 1.45\) , \(\tau_{{hot}}\sim 0.00\) , and \(\tau_{{ice}}\sim 0.51\) . The pixel scale is 0.20 arcsec px -1 . The central circles represent the nuclear extracted spectrum ( \(\sim\) 0.75″) where colors are accurate to the nuclear line parameters (see Table 2 ). Left column: Maps of the line fluxes in erg s -1 cm -2 spaxel -1 . Middle column: Median velocities (v 50 ) in km s -1 . Right column: 80th-percentile line widths ( \(w_{80}\) ). Component 1 traces a low-velocity, nearly face-on disk. Component 2 reveals an asymmetric, blueshifted outflow with \(v_{50}\) of up to \(-\) 280 km s -1 .</small>

</details>


### [53] [Hamilton's Object Revisited: A challenging source redshift of a strong lensing configuration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19867)
*Jenny Wagner,Richard E. Griffiths,Emilio E. Falco*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 论文直接涉及强引力透镜系统（Hamilton天体），属于用户核心领域。虽然红移测量本身并非用户最关注的高红移星系动力学或气体性质，但该工作解决了透镜源的红移歧义，对后续透镜研究至关重要。用户画像中'lens'权重高，且论文涉及星系团尺度强透镜，与用户兴趣高度相关。

TL;DR: 通过重新分析光谱数据，确认Hamilton天体的红移为z=0.82，而非之前MOIRCS光谱暗示的z=3.201，解决了低分辨率光谱仪在红移测量上的模糊性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低分辨率光谱仪在测量z≈1和z≈3星系红移时存在困难，因为镁和铁的光谱线在不同红移下会与氢、硅、氧的谱线重叠。Hamilton天体作为引力透镜星系，其红移测量存在z=0.82和z=3.201两种矛盾结果，需要澄清。

Method: 重新分析Blue KCWI光谱数据，使用新的数据处理管道PypeIt，结合信号增强和Python程序进行谱线拟合。对三个多重像的光谱进行全面重新评估，包括外围的恒星形成区域。

Result: 重新分析确认红移为z=0.820±0.001（基于6个吸收特征）和z=0.821±0.002（基于4个发射特征）。而z=3.199±0.003的假设拟合效果较差，且与其他光谱不一致。MOIRCS光谱因观测覆盖不完整和波长校准问题而不可靠。

Conclusion: Hamilton天体的红移确定为z≈0.82，解决了红移测量的模糊性。需要新的MOIRCS观测来验证该天体是否具有已知星系团尺度强透镜中透镜团与源星系之间最小的角直径距离分离。

Abstract: Low-resolution spectrographs used to have difficulties to determine redshifts of galaxies at $z\approx1$ and $z\approx3$. Spectral emission and absorption lines of magnesium and iron redshifted to $z\approx1$ fall close to hydrogen, silicon, and oxygen lines at $z\approx3$. Here, we demonstrate that, even with modern, integrated field unit spectrographs, this task remains challenging. Hamilton's object, a blue star-forming galaxy, gravitationally lensed into three multiple images by the galaxy cluster SDSS J223010.47-081017.8 is such a case. Using the Blue Keck Cosmic Web Imager, its redshift was determined as $z=0.82$, while its MOIRCS spectrum hinted at $z=3.201$. To resolve the ambiguity, we completely re-analyse the Blue KCWI spectra of all three multiple images including the star-forming region in the outskirts. We employ a new data reduction pipeline, PypeIt, signal enhancement, and line fitting by Python-routines. The re-evaluation confirms the previous result based on 6 absorption features, $z=0.820 \pm 0.001$ and 4 emission features, $z=0.821 \pm 0.002$. The alternative $z=3.199\pm 0.003$, based on 6 absorption and 2 emission lines is a worse fit, also compared to other spectra. Moreover, we find the MOIRCS spectrum inconclusive: Observations cover two of three multiple images, with the slit for image C only covering its central bulge; furthermore the pixel-to-wavelength calibration requires a nightsky-emission-line calibration due to a missing calibration arc lamp. New MOIRCS observations are needed to verify that Hamilton's object has the smallest separation in angular diameter distance between lensing cluster and source galaxy among the known cluster-scale strong lenses.

Abstract Translation:
低分辨率光谱仪过去难以确定红移约为1和红移约为3的星系的红移。镁和铁的谱线发射和吸收线红移到红移约为1时，与红移约为3时的氢、硅和氧谱线接近。在此，我们证明，即使使用现代积分场单元光谱仪，这项任务仍然具有挑战性。Hamilton天体是一个蓝色恒星形成星系，被星系团SDSS J223010.47-081017.8引力透镜成三个多重像，就是这样一个案例。使用蓝Keck宇宙网成像仪，其红移被确定为z=0.82，而其MOIRCS光谱则暗示红移为z=3.201。为解决这一歧义，我们完全重新分析了所有三个多重像（包括外围恒星形成区域）的蓝KCWI光谱。我们采用了新的数据归约管线PypeIt、信号增强以及基于Python例程的谱线拟合。重新评估确认了先前基于6个吸收特征的结果，z=0.820 ± 0.001，以及4个发射特征，z=0.821 ± 0.002。替代方案z=3.199±0.003基于6个吸收线和2个发射线，拟合效果较差，与其他光谱相比也是如此。此外，我们发现MOIRCS光谱不具决定性：观测覆盖了三个多重像中的两个，而像C的狭缝仅覆盖其中心核球；此外，由于缺少校准弧灯，像素到波长的校准需要夜天发射线校准。需要新的MOIRCS观测来验证Hamilton天体是否具有已知星系团尺度强透镜中透镜团与源星系之间最小的角直径距离分离。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，Hamilton天体的红移确定为z≈0.82，解决了红移测量的模糊性。需要新的MOIRCS观测来验证该天体是否具有已知星系团尺度强透镜中透镜团与源星系之间最小的角直径距离分离。

### [54] [Revealing the nature of the starburst galaxies in the $z=2.4$ overdensity HATLAS J0849](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23608)
*Melanie Kaasinen,Francesca Rizzo,Francesco Valentino,Cecilia Bacchini,Jianhang Chen,Takafumi Tsukui,Aristeidis Amvrosiadis*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 该论文聚焦于z=2.41超密度区域中的星暴星系，利用高分辨率CO(4-3)、[C I]和尘埃连续谱观测研究冷气体形态与运动学，与用户对高红移星系动力学、多相气体及强引力透镜的兴趣高度吻合。论文作者中包含用户核心作者Jianhang Chen，且主题涉及星暴星系、冷气体、尘埃等用户高频关键词。论文方法（高分辨率干涉观测）和科学问题（星暴触发机制、盘星系旋转速度）与用户画像中的密集气体、大质量主序星系、宇宙正午等主题直接相关。

TL;DR: 研究发现在z=2.41超密度区域中，气体丰富的星暴星系中至少有42%是旋转主导的盘星系，这些星系已经处于与当今最大椭圆星系相当的质量环境中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了理解当今最大椭圆星系的起源，需要研究z≥2超密度区域中的星暴星系触发机制及其演化过程。

Method: 对z=2.41超密度区域HATLAS J084933.4+021443中的五个气体丰富星系进行高分辨率（0.15"）CO(4-3)、[C I] 1-0和尘埃连续谱观测，分析其冷气体形态和运动学特征。

Result: 发现两个旋转盘星系（W和C）都表现出非轴对称径向气体运动（与棒状结构一致）。W是旋转主导的盘星系，旋转速度约520 km/s，T很可能是晚期合并星系。超过42%的气体丰富星暴星系是旋转主导的盘星系，且旋转速度>400 km/s的盘星系几乎只存在于超密度区域。

Conclusion: 这些星系已经处于与当今最大椭圆星系相当的质量环境中，尽管星暴活动剧烈，但恒星反馈仍是主要的湍流驱动机制，流入气体通过有序流动有效传输，只有小部分动能转化为盘范围的湍流。

Abstract: Today's most massive ellipticals are proposed to originate from starbursting galaxies in $z\gtrsim2$ overdensities. To discern what triggers these starbursts, and their $z=0$ descendants, we performed a detailed case study of five gas-rich galaxies in the $z=2.41$ overdensity, HATLAS J084933.4+021443. Using 0.15" resolution CO(4-3), [C I] 1-0, and dust-continuum observations, we characterised their cold gas morphology and kinematics. We find two rotating discs, W and C, both exhibiting non-axisymmetric radial gas motions (consistent with bars). Of the two extreme starbursts, W is a lopsided, rotation-dominated disc with a rotation velocity of $\sim520$ km s$^{-1}$, whereas T is most likely a late-stage merger. Combined with recent studies, we find that $\gtrsim42\%$ of gas-rich, massive starbursts in overdensities are rotation-dominated discs, a fraction not yet systematically reproduced by galaxy evolution models. Beyond $z=1$, disc galaxies with rotation velocities of $>400$ km s$^{-1}$ reside almost exclusively in overdensities, consistent with early mass assembly in dense environments. By comparing to local early-type galaxies with cold gas discs, we confirm that these systems already reside in halos comparable to the most massive $z\sim0$ ellipticals at the centres of groups and clusters. Despite their extreme star-formation rates, these discs lie on the same $σ-$SFR locus as lower-SFR field galaxies, implying that stellar feedback remains the dominant turbulence driver. We postulate that this is because inflowing gas is effectively transported through ordered streaming, such that only a small fraction of kinetic energy feeds disc-wide turbulence.

Abstract Translation:
当今最巨大的椭圆星系被认为起源于红移z≳2的超密度区域中的星暴星系。为了探究触发这些星暴的原因及其在z=0时的后裔，我们对位于z=2.41超密度区域HATLAS J084933.4+021443中的五个富气体星系进行了详细的案例研究。利用0.15角秒分辨率的CO(4-3)、[C I] 1-0和尘埃连续谱观测，我们表征了它们的冷气体形态和运动学。我们发现两个旋转盘，W和C，均表现出非轴对称的径向气体运动（与棒结构一致）。在两个极端星暴中，W是一个不对称的、旋转主导的盘，旋转速度约为520 km/s，而T则很可能是一个晚期并合体。结合近期研究，我们发现超密度区域中超过42%的富气体大质量星暴是旋转主导的盘，这一比例尚未被星系演化模型系统性地重现。在z>1之外，旋转速度超过400 km/s的盘状星系几乎只存在于超密度区域中，这与早期质量在密集环境中聚集的图景一致。通过与拥有冷气体盘的本地早型星系比较，我们确认这些系统已经处于与群和团中心最巨大的z~0椭圆星系相当的质量环境中。尽管其恒星形成率极高，这些盘却位于与低恒星形成率场星系相同的σ-SFR关系上，这意味着恒星反馈仍然是主要的湍流驱动机制。我们推测这是因为流入气体通过有序流动被有效传输，只有一小部分动能转化为盘范围的湍流。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，这些星系已经处于与当今最大椭圆星系相当的质量环境中，尽管星暴活动剧烈，但恒星反馈仍是主要的湍流驱动机制，流入气体通过有序流动有效传输，只有小部分动能转化为盘范围的湍流。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
表1：HATLAS J084933.4+021443成员星系的属性

<small>Table 1: Properties of HATLAS J084933.4+021443 member galaxies</small>

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.23608v1/x1.png)

### [55] [The ALPINE-CRISTAL-JWST Survey: Gas-phase abundance gradients of main sequence star-forming galaxies and their kinematics at $4 < z < 6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13493)
*Lilian L. Lee,Natascha M. Förster Schreiber,Seiji Fujimoto,Andreas L. Faisst,Rodrigo Herrera-Camus,Reinhard Genzel,Linda J. Tacconi,Dieter Lutz,Alvio Renzini,Ryan Sanders,Emily Wisnioski,Stijn Wuyts,Eleonora Parlanti,Gareth Jones,Hannah Übler,Daizhong Liu,Jianhang Chen,Ric I. Davies,Giulia Tozzi,Andreas Burkert,Sedona H. Price,Manuel Aravena,Médéric Boquien,Matthieu Béthermin,Elisabete da Cunha,Rebecca L. Davies,Ilse De Looze,Miroslava Dessauges-Zavadsky,Andrea Ferrara,Deanne B. Fisher,Steven Gillman,Michele Ginolfi,Edo Ibar,Anton M. Koekemoer,Juan Molina,Thorsten Naab,Mónica Relaño,Dominik A. Riechers,David B. Sanders,Justin S. Spilker,Livia Vallini,Giovanni Zamorani,Ambra Nanni,Poulomi Dam,Tanio Diaz-Santos,Diego Gómez-Espinoza,Ali Hadi,Ryota Ikeda,Ana Posses,Michael Romano,Amiel Sternberg,Vicente Villanueva,Wuji Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 该论文与用户Zotero兴趣画像高度吻合：研究主题为高红移主序星系的金属丰度梯度与运动学性质，属于强引力透镜领域用户明确优先关注的高红移星系动力学/运动学方向；核心作者包括daizhong liu、jianhang chen、natascha m förster schreiber、reinhard genzel、hannah übler等用户高频作者；方法上使用JWST NIRSpec IFU和ALMA [CII]观测，与用户常用数据手段一致；论文聚焦于盘成熟度对金属丰度梯度的影响，与用户兴趣中的'cosmic noon'、'main-sequence galaxy'、'gas kinematics'等关键词直接匹配。

TL;DR: JWST观测显示4<z<6星系金属丰度梯度平均为正，与盘成熟度相关


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高红移星系金属丰度梯度与运动学性质的关系，探索盘成熟度对金属丰度分布的影响

Method: 使用JWST NIRSpec IFU观测20个4<z<6星系，通过强线法绘制氧丰度径向分布，结合ALMA [CII]观测的运动学数据，分析梯度与速度弥散、旋转速度的关系

Result: 金属丰度梯度平均为正（中值+0.039±0.010 dex/kpc），仅3个星系梯度>0.05 dex/kpc，无显著负梯度；发现V_rot/σ_0与梯度呈负相关，与σ_0无强关系

Conclusion: 金属丰度梯度与盘成熟度相关，V_rot/σ_0增加导致梯度变负，这与从高红移到低红移的宇宙演化趋势一致

Abstract: We present gas-phase radial metallicity profiles for 20 main-sequence galaxies at $4<z<6$, primarily based on JWST NIRSpec IFU observations obtained as part of the JWST-ALPINE-CRISTAL programme. Our study aims to connect the metallicity gradients of these galaxies with their kinematic properties from [CII]158$μ$m ALMA observations. We map the radial profiles of oxygen abundance using the strong-line method leveraging the rich set of rest-frame optical emission lines. Linear fits to the annular-binned radial profiles show that, on average, the metallicity gradients are slightly positive with a median of $+0.039 \pm 0.010{\rm dexkpc^{-1}}$. There are no substantial systematic offsets in gradients when using different line diagnostics. However, only three galaxies show a gradient $>0.05{\rm dexkpc^{-1}}$ at $1σ$, and none have a significant negative gradient. We investigate the correlation between the metallicity gradients and the intrinsic gas velocity dispersion $σ_0$, as well as the ratio $V_{\rm rot}/σ_0$ of the disks. Combining our sample with mass-matched literature samples at $3<z<7$, we find a negative shallow correlation between $V_{\rm rot}/σ_0$ and the metallicity gradients, but no strong relationships with $σ_0$. As $V_{\rm rot}/σ_0$ increases towards later cosmic times, the observed negative trend with $V_{\rm rot}/σ_0$ is consistent with the overall cosmic evolution of metallicity gradients from high to low redshifts. This suggests that disk maturity plays a crucial role in shaping the radial metallicity gradients. [Abridged abstract]

Abstract Translation:
我们展示了20个主序星系在$4<z<6$范围内的气体相位径向金属丰度分布，主要基于作为JWST-ALPINE-CRISTAL计划一部分的JWST NIRSpec IFU观测数据。本研究旨在将这些星系的金属丰度梯度与其来自[CII]158$\mu$m ALMA观测的运动学特性联系起来。我们利用丰富的静止光学发射线，通过强线方法绘制了氧丰度的径向分布图。对环状分箱径向分布的线性拟合显示，平均而言，金属丰度梯度略为正，中位数为$+0.039 \pm 0.010{\rm dexkpc^{-1}}$。使用不同的线诊断方法时，梯度没有显著的系统性偏移。然而，只有三个星系在$1\sigma$水平上显示出$>0.05{\rm dexkpc^{-1}}$的梯度，且没有一个星系具有显著的负梯度。我们研究了金属丰度梯度与固有气体速度弥散$\sigma_0$以及盘面旋转速度与速度弥散之比$V_{\rm rot}/\sigma_0$之间的相关性。将我们的样本与$3<z<7$范围内质量匹配的文献样本相结合，我们发现$V_{\rm rot}/\sigma_0$与金属丰度梯度之间存在微弱的负相关，但与$\sigma_0$没有强相关性。随着$V_{\rm rot}/\sigma_0$在更晚的宇宙时间增加，观测到的与$V_{\rm rot}/\sigma_0$的负相关趋势与金属丰度梯度从高红移到低红移的整体宇宙演化一致。这表明盘面成熟度在塑造径向金属丰度梯度中起着关键作用。[摘要删节]

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，金属丰度梯度与盘成熟度相关，V_rot/σ_0增加导致梯度变负，这与从高红移到低红移的宇宙演化趋势一致。

Right : Pixel-based metallicity profile. Each data point is coloured coded by its (absolute) acute azimuthal angle difference from the major axis. <small>Figure 3 : Distributions of metallicity gradients, \(\nabla_{r}\log({Z})\) as a function of the velocity dispersion, \(\sigma_{0}\) ( left ), and the ratio of rotational velocity to velocity dispersion, \(V_{rot}/\sigma_{0}\) ( right ), for the CRISTAL disk galaxies (green hexagons). However, comparing the overall distribution of the two populations at \(z\) \( Ma et al. 2017 (purple contour), FIRE2 at \(z\) \(=\) \(3\) from Sun et al. 2025 ( right , open purple pentagons), and TNG50 at \(z\) \(=\) \(3\) from Hemler et al. 2021 ( right , dashed orange line). While the simulations capture the slight positive and negative relationships between \(\nabla_{r}\log({Z})\) and \(\sigma_{0}\) and \(V_{rot}/\sigma_{0}\) , respectively, the normalisation and steepness of these relationships differ from the observations.</small>

### [56] [Mature but Still Growing: JWST Detection of the Earliest Intracluster Light at z ~ 2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03427)
*Hyungjin Joo,M. James Jee,Kyle Finner,Zachary P. Scofield,Sangjun Cha,Jinhyub Kim,Ranga-Ram Chary,Andreas Faisst,Bomee Lee*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 该论文研究z=1.98的星系团XLSSC 122中的星系内光（ICL），使用了JWST数据，并涉及强引力透镜质量分布与光分布的对比。虽然主题是星系团ICL而非直接的星系-星系强引力透镜，但强引力透镜分析是论文核心方法之一，且用户画像中'jwst'、'lensing'、'strong lensing'权重高，因此给予高分。

TL;DR: JWST观测发现红移z=1.98的星系团XLSSC 122中已存在显著的星系内光（ICL），表明大质量晕中星系内恒星的积聚在宇宙早期（约100亿年前）已在进行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究宇宙早期（红移z≈2）星系团中星系内光（ICL）的形成和演化，了解大质量晕中恒星积聚的时间尺度，探索ICL作为星系团动力学活动指示器的潜力。

Method: 使用JWST深度成像数据，结合HST数据，通过多分量PSF卷积Sersic模型将表面亮度分布分解为三个成分：BCG核心、BCG包层和ICL成分；采用小波基模型量化ICL的南向过量；比较BCG+ICL光分布与强引力透镜质量分布。

Result: 在红移z=1.98的星系团中稳健检测到延伸数百kpc的弥散发射；ICL比例约17%，表明星系内恒星积聚在z≈2时已显著进行；ICL比例在5000Å处达到峰值，与动力学活跃星系团特征一致；检测到ICL南向过量，支持系统处于动力学活跃状态；BCG+ICL光分布与强透镜质量分布在100kpc内形态一致。

Conclusion: 星系内光是早期形成且具有动力学信息的大质量晕成分，其积聚在宇宙早期（红移z≈2）已显著进行，ICL可作为星系团动力学活动的有效示踪物。

Abstract: We present a JWST analysis of intracluster light (ICL) in XLSSC 122 at z = 1.98, currently the most distant known strong lensing galaxy cluster with an evolved member population. Using deep JWST imaging complemented by HST data and careful control of systematics, we robustly detect diffuse emission extending to several hundred kpc from the brightest cluster galaxy (BCG) down to about 29 mag arcsec^-2. Multi component PSF convolved Sersic modeling separates the surface brightness profiles into three components: a BCG core, a BCG envelope, and an ICL component, with stable Sersic indices across wavelengths. Nearly flat color profiles indicate minimal radial variation in the stellar populations of the BCG envelope and the ICL. The median ICL fraction measured across seven bands is about 17 percent, demonstrating that the buildup of intracluster stars in massive halos was already well underway by z about 2. The ICL fraction peaks near 5000 Angstrom in the rest frame, resembling the behavior observed in dynamically active clusters. We also detect a southern excess of ICL relative to the best fit Sersic model and quantify it using wavelet based modeling, providing additional support that this system is dynamically active. The BCG + ICL light distribution and strong lensing mass map show strong morphological agreement within about 100 kpc. These findings establish the ICL as an early forming and dynamically informative component of massive halos.

Abstract Translation:
我们展示了JWST对红移z=1.98的XLSSC 122星系团内光（ICL）的分析，这是目前已知最遥远的强透镜星系团，拥有演化的成员星系群。利用深JWST成像，辅以HST数据和对系统误差的仔细控制，我们稳健地探测到从最亮团星系（BCG）延伸至数百千秒差距的弥散发射，表面亮度低至约29星等每平方角秒。多分量PSF卷积Sérsic模型将表面亮度轮廓分解为三个分量：BCG核、BCG包层和ICL分量，其Sérsic指数在不同波段间保持稳定。近乎平坦的颜色轮廓表明BCG包层和ICL的恒星种群在径向上变化极小。在七个波段中测得的ICL中值比例约为17%，表明在大质量晕中，团内恒星的积聚在红移z≈2时已显著进行。ICL比例在静止系约5000埃处达到峰值，与动力学活跃星系团中观测到的行为相似。我们还探测到相对于最佳拟合Sérsic模型的南部ICL过量，并通过基于小波的建模进行量化，进一步支持该系统处于动力学活跃状态。BCG+ICL的光分布与强透镜质量图在约100千秒差距内显示出强烈的形态一致性。这些发现确立了ICL作为大质量晕中早期形成且具有动力学信息的分量。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，星系内光是早期形成且具有动力学信息的大质量晕成分，其积聚在宇宙早期（红移z≈2）已显著进行，ICL可作为星系团动力学活动的有效示踪物。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.03427v1/x1.png)

图1：多波段表面亮度轮廓与模型分解。顶行显示HST观测（F814W、F105W和F140W），底行显示JWST/NIRCam观测（F090W、F200W、F277W和F356W）。黑色数据点表示椭圆环内观测到的中值表面亮度，误差棒包含流量不确定度和系统天空误差（\(\sigma_{sky}\)）的平方和。水平点划线表示各波段的极限表面亮度（\(\mu_{lim}\)）。红色实线表示与望远镜PSF卷积后的最佳拟合多分量Sérsic模型。该模型分解为三个不同的恒星分量：BCG核（蓝色点线）、BCG包层（橙色点划线）和弥散ICL（绿色虚线）。最后的分量（绿色虚线）用于本工作中的ICL分析。下方子图显示观测数据与总模型之间的残差（\(\Delta\mu\)）。

<small>Figure 1: Multiband SB Profiles and Model Decomposition. The top row displays HST observations (F814W, F105W, and F140W), while the bottom row presents JWST/NIRCam observations (F090W, F200W, F277W, and F356W). Black data points represent the observed median SB within elliptical bins, with error bars accounting for the quadrature sum of flux uncertainties and systematic sky error ( \(\sigma_{sky}\) ). Horizontal dot-dashed lines indicate the limiting SB ( \(\mu_{lim}\) ) for each respective band. The red solid line denotes the best-fit multi-component Sérsic model convolved with the telescope PSF. The model is decomposed into three distinct stellar components: the BCG core (blue dotted line), the BCG envelope (orange dot-dashed line), and the diffuse ICL (green dashed line). The last components (green dashed line) are utilized for the ICL analysis in this work. Lower subpanels show the residuals ( \(\Delta\mu\) ) between the observed data and the total model.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.03427v1/02_color_profiles.png)

图2：由六个相邻滤光片对导出的BCG+ICL径向颜色轮廓。阴影区域表示68%置信区间，包含统计流量不确定度和系统天空背景误差（\(\sigma_{sky}\)）。内部灰色区域（\(\lesssim 1\) kpc）表示HST和JWST之间PSF宽度的差异可能引起人为颜色梯度。在此尺度之外，颜色轮廓在误差范围内保持非常平坦，表明BCG包层和ICL中的恒星种群在空间上均匀。一个显著的例外是F814W \(-\) F090W轮廓，在\(3\lesssim SMA \lesssim 10\) kpc处表现出变化，可能指示中心星系内的径向差异，如尘埃消光（见正文）。

<small>Figure 2: Radial color profiles of the BCG+ICL derived from six adjacent filter pairs. Shaded regions represent the 68% confidence interval, incorporating both statistical flux uncertainties and systematic sky background errors ( \(\sigma_{sky}\) ). The inner gray region ( \(\lesssim 1\) kpc) indicates the area where differences in PSF widths between HST and JWST may induce artificial color gradients. Beyond this scale, the color profiles remain remarkably flat within the error margins, suggesting a spatially uniform stellar population across the BCG envelope and ICL. A notable exception is the F814W \(-\) F090W profile, which exhibits variation at \(3\lesssimSMA\lesssim 10\) kpc, potentially indicating radial differences such as dust attenuation within the central galaxy (see text).</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.03427v1/x2.png)

图3：ICL比例（\(f_{ICL}\)）随静止系波长的变化。红色十字表示XLSSC 122（\(z=1.98\)）在七个观测波段上的测量值。作为比较，粉色（天蓝色）点表示由Jiménez-Teja等人（2018, 2021）；de Oliveira等人（2022）；Jiménez-Teja等人（2025）；de Oliveira等人（2025）测量的动力学活跃（松弛）星系团中的\(f_{ICL}\)。XLSSC 122的\(f_{ICL}\)值在4800 Å附近呈现特征性的局部最大值，这一模式与动力学活跃或并合系统中的趋势非常相似。

<small>Figure 3: ICL fraction ( \(f_{ICL}\) ) as a function of rest-frame wavelength. The red crosses represent the measurements for XLSSC 122 ( \(z=1.98\) ) across the seven observed bands. For comparison, pink (sky blue) points indicate \(f_{ICL}\) in dynamically active (relaxed) clusters measured by Jiménez-Teja et al. ( 2018 , 2021 ); de Oliveira et al. ( 2022 ); Jiménez-Teja et al. ( 2025 ); de Oliveira et al. ( 2025 ) . The \(f_{ICL}\) values for XLSSC 122 exhibit a characteristic local maximum near 4800 Å , a pattern that closely resembles the trends found in dynamically active or merging systems.</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.03427v1/x3.png)

图4：XLSSC 122中非Sérsic弥散发射的定位。左列显示减去最佳拟合二维Sérsic ICL（弥散）分量后的JWST/NIRCam图像（F200W、F277W和F356W），揭示了南部显著的残差信号。中列显示由基于小波的算法DAWIS检测到的这一额外弥散分量的孤立模型。右列显示减去全局Sérsic和局部DAWIS模型后的最终残差图。这一南部特征代表了从BCG延伸约100千秒差距的显著弥散发射过量。其与成员星系超密度的空间对齐以及独立的多波段不对称性（X射线、射电和SZ）强烈表明，其起源于星系团内正在进行的或最近的动力学相互作用导致的潮汐剥离恒星。

<small>Figure 4: Localization of non-Sérsic diffuse emission in XLSSC 122. The left column presents JWST/NIRCam images (F200W, F277W, and F356W) following the subtraction of the best-fit 2D Sérsic ICL (diffuse) component, revealing a prominent residual signal to the south. The middle column displays the isolated model of this additional diffuse component as detected by the wavelet-based algorithm DAWIS . The right column shows the final residual maps after subtracting both the global Sérsic and local DAWIS models. This southern feature represents a significant excess of diffuse emission extending approximately 100 kpc from the BCG. Its spatial alignment with the overdensity of member galaxies and independent multi-wavelength asymmetries (X-ray, radio, and SZ) strongly suggests an origin in tidally stripped stars resulting from ongoing or recent dynamical interactions within the cluster.</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.03427v1/05_comparison_with_SL.png)

图5：XLSSC 122中质量分布与弥散恒星光的比较。左上：质光比（\(\kappa/\mu\)）的径向轮廓由SL质量图和F356W表面亮度轮廓导出。该比值在\(r\sim 100\) kpc内遵循线性关系（\(\kappa/\mu\propto r\)），这是SL模型约束最稳健的区域。右：展示了SL质量分布（红色等高线）与平滑后的BCG+ICL+成员星系恒星光分布（蓝色等高线和灰度）之间的二维比较。左下：橙色曲线展示了光与质量等高线之间的OC，绿色曲线展示了MHD。这两个指标一致表明，在\(r\sim 180\) kpc内，质量与弥散光分量之间的整体形态相似性保持较高。在\(r\sim 60\) kpc之外相似性的轻微下降归因于南部ICL过量的存在以及SL约束的缺乏。

<small>Figure 5: Comparison between the mass distribution and diffuse stellar light in XLSSC 122. Top left: The radial profile of the mass-to-light ratio ( \(\kappa/\mu\) ) is derived from the SL mass map and the F356W SB profile. The ratio follows a linear relation ( \(\kappa/\mu\propto r\) ) up to \(r\sim 100\) kpc, the regime where the SL model constraints are most robust. Right: A two-dimensional comparison between the SL mass distribution (red contours) and the smoothed stellar light distribution of the combined BCG + ICL + member galaxies (blue contours and gray scales) is presented. Bottom left: The orange curve illustrates the OC between the light and mass contours, while the green curve displays the MHD. Both metrics consistently indicate that the overall morphological similarity between mass and diffuse light components remains high up to \(r\sim 180\) kpc. The slight decrease in similarly beyond \(r\sim 60\) kpc is attributed to the presence of the southern ICL excess and the lack of the SL constraints.</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.03427v1/x4.png)

图6：1/f噪声建模示例。面板(a)显示原始图像。面板(b)和(c)展示了使用附录A.1中描述的算法建模的1/f噪声和去噪后的图像。面板(d)和(e)显示了JWST流水线算法（clean_flicker_noise）的输出。面板(f)展示了两种算法之间的差异。我们的算法有效避免了明亮源附近的过度校正，并更好地保留了弥散发射。

<small>Figure 6: Example of modeling the 1/f noise. Panel (a) shows the original image. Panels (b) and (c) present the modeled 1/f noise and the denoised image obtained with our algorithm described in Appendix A.1 . Panels (d) and (e) show the output of the JWST pipeline algorithm ( clean_flicker_noise ). Panel (f) illustrates the difference between the two algorithms. Our algorithm effectively avoids over-correction near bright sources and better preserves diffuse emission.</small>

### [57] [The ionised interstellar medium of DSFGs revealed by JWST/NIRSpec and ALMA: Super-solar metallicity, low ionisation parameters and, typical electron densities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.18558)
*Steven Gillman,Kei Ito,Francesco Valentino,Gabe Brammer,Pablo Araya Araya,Georgios Magdis,Ugnė Dudzevičiūtė,Aswin P. Vijayan,Minju Lee,Bitten Gullberg,Daniel Ceverino,Andreas L. Faisst,Seiji Fujimoto,Thomas R. Greve,Rashmi Gottumukkala,Chandana Hegde,Michaela Hirschmann,Shuowen Jin,Christian Kragh Jespersen,Takumi Kakimoto,Mariko Kubo,Peter Laursen,Masato Onodera,Antonio Pensabene,Francesca Rizzo,John R. Weaver,Po-Feng Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 该论文利用JWST/NIRSpec和ALMA研究高红移尘埃遮蔽恒星形成星系(DSFGs)的星际介质，包括金属丰度、电子密度和电离参数，与用户对高红移星系动力学、多相气体和强引力透镜的兴趣高度吻合。论文作者中包含用户核心作者列表中的Seiji Fujimoto、Andreas L. Faisst、Michaela Hirschmann和Aswin P. Vijayan，且主题涉及JWST、ALMA、星际介质和尘埃，与用户Zotero库中的高频关键词匹配。

TL;DR: JWST/NIRSpec观测48个高红移ALMA星系，发现这些远红外明亮星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，偏离了标准尘埃-金属平衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高红移、尘埃遮蔽的恒星形成星系的性质，特别是它们的金属丰度、电子密度和电离参数，以了解这些系统的星际介质特征和演化状态。

Method: 使用JWST/NIRSpec获取近红外光谱(2-4μm)，结合ALMA探测，对48个高红移(z=2.53)星系进行多波段SED分析，测量金属丰度([NII]/Hα)、电子密度([SII]双线比)和电离参数([OII]/Hβ)。

Result: 样本中位恒星质量log(M*/M⊙)=10.8±0.1，尘埃质量log(Md/M⊙)=8.7±0.1；金属丰度12+log(O/H)=8.71±0.02，最明亮的FIR星系偏离基本金属丰度关系0.15±0.03dex；电子密度log(ne/cm³)=2.53±0.07；电离参数log(U)=-2.84±0.06；40%星系显示AGN活动迹象。

Conclusion: 远红外明亮星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，偏离了在较少尘埃遮蔽星系中观察到的标准尘埃和金属产生平衡，突显了JWST和ALMA协同研究的重要性。

Abstract: We present a detailed study of near-infrared (2-4$\rm μ$m) JWST/NIRSpec spectra of 48 high-redshift ($z=2.53^{+1.32}_{-0.70}$) galaxies detected with ALMA at $>3σ$. From a multi-wavelength SED analysis we establish the sample has a a median stellar mass of $\rm\log_{10}(M_\ast/M_\odot)=10.8\pm0.1$ and dust mass of $\rm\log_{10}(M_{\rm d}/M_\odot)=8.7\pm0.1$, covering a broad range of far-infrared luminosity $\rm (\log_{10}(L_{FIR}/L_\odot)=10.9-12.7)$. The majority of sources show no signs of AGN activity, with 40% having either X-ray counterparts $(\rm L_{Xc}>10^{42}erg/s)$, elevated optical line ratios, or broad (FWHM>800 km/s) H$α$ profiles, although we note this is a lower limit due to the stochastic placement of NIRSpec slits. We establish the sample has a median gas-phase metallicity of $12+\log({\rm O/H})=8.71\pm0.02$, as derived from the [NII]/H$α$ ratio, with the most FIR-luminous galaxies ($\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)>12$) falling $0.15\pm0.03$dex above the fundamental metallicity relation. From the [SII] emission-line doublet ratio, we measure a median electron density of $\log_{10}(n_{\rm e}/{\rm cm}^{-3})=2.53\pm0.07$ consistent with less-massive, star-forming, galaxies at the same epoch. For nine galaxies with [OII] and H$β$ detections (median $\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)=11.81\pm0.15$), we derive a median observed (dust-uncorrected) ionisation parameter of $\rm\log_{10}(U)=-2.84\pm0.06$. Our results indicate that luminous far-infrared galaxies are massive, chemically evolved systems that appear to deviate from the standard dust and metal production equilibrium observed in less obscured galaxies. This study demonstrates the synergy of JWST and ALMA in unveiling the nature of DSFGs, and highlights the need for a NIRSpec survey of uniformly selected, massive, dust-obscured, galaxies to fully characterise their interstellar medium.

Abstract Translation:
我们详细研究了48个高红移（$z=2.53^{+1.32}_{-0.70}$）且被ALMA以$>3σ$探测到的星系的近红外（2-4$\rm μ$m）JWST/NIRSpec光谱。通过多波段SED分析，我们确定该样本的中值恒星质量为$\rm\log_{10}(M_\ast/M_\odot)=10.8\pm0.1$，尘埃质量为$\rm\log_{10}(M_{\rm d}/M_\odot)=8.7\pm0.1$，覆盖了广泛的远红外光度范围$\rm (\log_{10}(L_{FIR}/L_\odot)=10.9-12.7)$。大多数源没有显示出活动星系核（AGN）活动的迹象，40%的源具有X射线对应体$(\rm L_{Xc}>10^{42}erg/s)$、增强的光学谱线比或宽的（FWHM>800 km/s）H$α$轮廓，尽管我们注意到由于NIRSpec狭缝的随机放置，这是一个下限。我们确定样本的中值气体相位金属丰度为$12+\log({\rm O/H})=8.71\pm0.02$，这是根据[NII]/H$α$比值推导出的，其中远红外光度最高的星系（$\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)>12$）比基本金属丰度关系高出$0.15\pm0.03$dex。根据[SII]发射线双线比值，我们测量到中值电子密度为$\log_{10}(n_{\rm e}/{\rm cm}^{-3})=2.53\pm0.07$，与同一时期质量较小的恒星形成星系一致。对于九个探测到[OII]和H$β$的星系（中值$\rm\log_{10}(L_{\rm FIR}/L_\odot)=11.81\pm0.15$），我们推导出中值观测（未经尘埃校正）电离参数为$\rm\log_{10}(U)=-2.84\pm0.06$。我们的结果表明，明亮的远红外星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，似乎偏离了在较少尘埃遮蔽星系中观察到的标准尘埃和金属产生平衡。这项研究展示了JWST和ALMA在揭示DSFGs性质方面的协同作用，并强调需要对均匀选择的、大质量的、尘埃遮蔽的星系进行NIRSpec巡天，以全面表征其星际介质。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，远红外明亮星系是质量大、化学演化成熟的系统，偏离了在较少尘埃遮蔽星系中观察到的标准尘埃和金属产生平衡，突显了JWST和ALMA协同研究的重要性。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/x1.png)

图1：最终48个ALMA – NIRSpec星系的JWST/NIRCam假彩色图像，按远红外光度（L FIR ）降序排列。对于每个源，我们展示了标记有DJA-ID、光谱红移、远红外光度、ALMA峰值流量中心（紫色星形）和一个抖动位置的NIRSpec MSA狭缝（白色方框）的4 \(\aas@@fstack{\prime\prime}\) 0 \(\,\times\,\) 4 \(\aas@@fstack{\prime\prime}\) 0 剪切图。对于每个源，我们选择对应于静止系2 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\)（R，近红外）、0.7 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\)（G，光学）和0.3 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\)（B，紫外）的NIRCam滤光片。被识别为AGN（见第4.2节）的源被高亮显示，其中\(\dagger\)表示宽发射线，\(\ddagger\)表示X射线对应体，\(*\)表示增强的光学谱线比。

<small>Figure 1 : JWST/NIRCam false colour images for the final sample of 48 ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies ranked in descending far-infrared luminosity (L FIR ). For each source we show the 4 \(\aas@@fstack{\prime\prime}\) 0 \(\,\times\,\) 4 \(\aas@@fstack{\prime\prime}\) 0 cutout as labelled with the DJA-ID, spectroscopic redshift, far-infrared luminosity, ALMA peak flux centroid (purple star) and NIRSpec MSA slits (white boxes) for one dither position. For each source we select the NIRCam filter that corresponds to rest-frame 2 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\) (R, near-infrared), 0.7 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\) (G, optical) and 0.3 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\) (B, ultra-violet). Sources identified as AGN (see Sec. 4.2 ) are highlighted, where \(\dagger\) indicates broad emission lines, \(\ddagger\) indicates an X-ray counterpart and \(*\) highlights elevated optical-line ratios.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/x2.png)

图2：mercurius远红外修正黑体建模的三个示例。对于每个源，展示了测光数据（黑点；上限显示为箭头）、最佳拟合黑体曲线（紫色虚线）和1 \(\sigma\) 不确定度（紫色阴影区域）。我们在每个面板中报告最佳拟合参数，以及NIRSpec（和ALMA）源ID、红移和CMB温度。被识别为AGN（见第4.2节）的源被高亮显示，其中\(\dagger\)表示宽发射线，\(\ddagger\)表示X射线对应体，\(*\)表示增强的光学谱线比。完整样本的SED和MCMC角点图见第6节。

<small>Figure 2 : Three examples of the mercurius far-infrared modified blackbody modelling. For each source show the photometry (black points; upper limits shown as arrows) and best-fit blackbody curve (purple-dashed line) and 1 \(\sigma\) uncertainty (purple shaded region). We report the best-fit parameter in each panel, as well as NIRSpec (and ALMA) source ID, redshift and CMB temperature. Sources identified as AGN (see Sec. 4.2 ) are highlighted, where \(\dagger\) indicates broad emission lines, \(\ddagger\) indicates an X-ray counterpart and \(*\) highlights elevated optical-line ratios. The SEDs, and MCMC corner plots, of the full sample are given in Section 6 .</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/x5.png)

图3：样本中四个星系在不同远红外光度范围内的JWST/NIRSpec光谱。对于每个源，我们展示了静止系0.36 – 0.54 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\)（突出显示[O iii ]/H \(\beta\) 复合体）和0.65 – 0.74 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\)（突出显示[N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) 复合体）的NIRSpec光谱（及1 \(\sigma\) 不确定度），并标记了探测到的（\(>\) 3 \(\sigma\) ）发射线。我们还标明了每个源的NIRSpec-ID、bagpipes推导的恒星质量、观测到的[N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) 比值、光谱红移以及ALMA-ID、ALMA流量密度和远红外光度。被识别为AGN（见第4.2节）的源被高亮显示，其中\(\dagger\)表示宽发射线，\(\ddagger\)表示X射线对应体，\(*\)表示增强的光学谱线比。

<small>Figure 3 : JWST/NIRSpec spectra for four galaxies in the sample across a range of far-infrared luminosity. For each source we show the NIRSpec spectra (and 1 \(\sigma\) uncertainty) from rest-frame 0.36 – 0.54 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\) highlighting the [O iii ]/H \(\beta\) complex and 0.65 – 0.74 \(\text{\,}{\SIUnitSymbolMicro m}\) highlighting the [N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) complex, with detected ( \(>\) 3 \(\sigma\) ) emission lines labelled. We further indicate the NIRSpec-ID, bagpipes derived stellar mass, observed [N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) ratio, spectroscopic redshift as well as ALMA-ID, ALMA flux density and far-infrared luminosity of each source. Sources identified as AGN (see Sec. 4.2 ) are highlighted, where \(\dagger\) indicates broad emission lines, \(\ddagger\) indicates an X-ray counterpart and \(*\) highlights elevated optical-line ratios.</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/x8.png)

图5：观测到的（未经尘埃校正）[O iii ]/H \(\beta\) 作为[N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) （左）和[S ii ]/H \(\alpha\) （右）的函数。信噪比 \( ii ]/H \(\alpha\) 和[S ii ]/H \(\alpha\) 的分布由灰色直方图显示。我们展示了来自斯隆数字巡天（SDSS；Brinchmann et al., 2004）的典型恒星形成星系在\(z\) \(\sim\) 0（红色密度）的比较样本，以及来自CEERS（Shapley et al., 2023）和AURORA巡天（Shapley et al., 2025）的红移匹配的恒星形成星系样本。黑色实线显示了\(z\) = 0时恒星形成活动与AGN之间的划分（Kauffmann et al., 2003），而来自（Kewley et al., 2013）在\(z\) = 2和\(z\) = 3的理论分界线分别由蓝色和红色虚线给出。黑色箭头表示使用Calzetti et al.（2000）尘埃定律进行A V = 5尘埃校正的影响。大多数ALMA – NIRSpec星系与同一时期的典型SFG一致，趋向于更低的[O iii ]/H \(\beta\) 谱线比，只有三个星系显示出类似AGN的光学谱线诊断特征。

<small>Figure 5 : Observed (dust-uncorrected) [O iii ]/H \(\beta\) as function of [N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) (left) and [S ii ]/H \(\alpha\) (right). Sources with S/N \( ii ]/H \(\alpha\) and [S ii ]/H \(\alpha\) for the full sample is shown by the grey histograms. We show comparison samples of typical star-forming galaxies at \(z\) \(\sim\) 0 (red density) from the Sloan Digital Sky Survey (SDSS; Brinchmann et al., 2004 ) , as well as a redshift matched sample of star-forming galaxies from the CEERS (Shapley et al., 2023 ) and AURORA Surveys Shapley et al. ( 2025 ) . The black solid curve shows the division between star-formation acticity and AGN (Kauffmann et al., 2003 ) at \(z\) = 0 whilst the theoretical demarcation at \(z\) = 2 and \(z\) = 3 from (Kewley et al., 2013 ) is given by the blue- and red-dashed lines respectively. The black arrow indicates the impact of A V = 5 dust correction using a Calzetti et al. ( 2000 ) dust law. The majority of ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies are consistent with typical SFGs at the same epoch, pushing to lower [O iii ]/H \(\beta\) line ratios, with only three galaxies showing AGN-like optical line diagnostics.</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/x9.png)

图6：使用Bian et al.（2018）强线校准从[N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) 指数推导出的气体相位金属丰度，作为ALMA – NIRSpec星系恒星质量的函数。信噪比 \( ii ] 6584 \(\lambda\) 发射线的源显示为上限。水平虚线表示太阳金属丰度（Asplund, 2005，12+log(O/H)= 8.66）。我们展示了来自SDSS（Curti et al., 2020）在\(z\) \(\sim\) 0（灰线）、MOSDEF巡天（Sanders et al., 2021）在\(z\) \(\sim\) 2.3（绿实线）和\(z\) \(\sim\) 3.3（红实线）的典型恒星形成星系比较样本，以及来自CEERS（Shapley et al., 2023）和AURORA巡天（Shapley et al., 2025）的红移匹配星系样本。我们进一步比较了来自KAOSS在\(z\) \(\sim\) 1 – 3（Birkin, 2022；Birkin et al., 2024b）的DSFGs高红移观测、来自Hogan et al.（2021）在\(z\) \(\sim\) 2.25的赫歇尔选择源，以及来自L-Galaxies模拟（Araya-Araya et al., 2025a）的远红外明亮（\(S_{870\mu m}\) \(>\) 1mJy）在\(z\) = 1 – 5的星系（蓝色密度）。ALMA – NIRSpec星系的气体相位金属丰度高于同一时期的观测比较样本，但与L-Galaxies的预测相当。

<small>Figure 6 : Gas-phase metallicity, as derived from the [N ii ]/H \(\alpha\) index using the Bian et al. ( 2018 ) strong-line calibrations, as a function of stellar mass for the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies. Sources with S/N \( ii ] 6584 \(\lambda\) emission-line are shown as limits. The horizontal dashed line indicates solar metallicity (Asplund, 2005 , 12+log(O/H)= 8.66) . We show comparison samples of typical star-forming galaxies at \(z\) \(\sim\) 0 from SDSS (Curti et al., 2020 ) (grey line), the MOSDEF Survey (Sanders et al., 2021 ) at \(z\) \(\sim\) 2.3 (green solid line) and \(z\) \(\sim\) 3.3 (red solid line), and a redshift matched sample of galaxies from the CEERS (Shapley et al., 2023 ) and AURORA Surveys Shapley et al. ( 2025 ) . We further compare to high-redshift observations of DSFGs from KAOSS at \(z\) \(\sim\) 1 – 3 (Birkin, 2022 ; Birkin et al., 2024b ) and Herschel selected sources from Hogan et al. ( 2021 ) at \(z\) \(\sim\) 2.25, as well as far-infrared bright ( \(S_{870\mu m}\) \(>\) 1mJy) at \(z\) = 1 – 5 galaxies (blue density) from the L-Galaxies simulation (Araya-Araya et al., 2025a ) . The ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies have higher gas-phase metallicity than the observational comparison samples at the same epoch, but comparable to predications from L-Galaxies.</small>

#### Figure 8
![Figure 8](https://arxiv.org/html/x12.png)

图8：左图：ALMA – NIRSpec样本的[S ii ]双线发射线比值作为光谱红移的函数，按比恒星形成率（sSFR）着色。信噪比 \( ii ] 发射线的源显示为上限。我们展示了来自CEERS巡天（Shapley et al., 2023）（圆圈）和AURORA巡天（Shapley et al., 2025）（三角形）的典型恒星形成星系比较样本。我们还标明了[S ii ]谱线比对电子密度的敏感区域（黑色虚线）（Kewley et al., 2019b）。ALMA – NIRSpec样本的[S ii ]双线发射线比值略低于来自CEERS和AURORA的质量较低的SFG样本，且与sSFR没有明显依赖关系。右图：使用mappings v5.1光电离代码（Kewley et al., 2019b）推导的[S ii ]电子密度作为光谱红移的函数，ALMA – NIRSpec星系按尘埃质量着色。灰色实线表示来自Abdurro’uf et al.（2024）的恒星形成星系典型演化（\(n_{e}\) \(\propto\) (1+z) 1.2）。ALMA – NIRSpec星系的电子密度与典型恒星形成星系一致，与比恒星形成率或远红外光度没有强相关性。

<small>Figure 8 : Left: [S ii ] doublet emission-line ratio as function of spectroscopic redshift for the ALMA – NIRSpec sample coloured by specific star-formation rate (sSFR). Sources with S/N \( ii ] emission-lines are shown as limits. We show comparison samples of typical star-forming galaxies from the CEERS Survey Shapley et al. ( 2023 ) (circles) and AURORA survey Shapley et al. ( 2025 ) (triangles). We further indicate the sensitivity region (black dashed lines) of the [S ii ] line ratio to the electron density (Kewley et al., 2019b ) . The ALMA – NIRSpec sample exhibits slightly lower [S ii ] doublet emission-line ratios to the lower mass SFGs samples from CEERS and AURORA, with no clear dependence on sSFR. Right: The [S ii ] derived electron density, using the mappings v5.1 photoionisation code (Kewley et al., 2019b ) , as a function of spectroscopic redshift, with the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies coloured by dust mass. The grey solid line indicates the typical evolution of star-forming galaxies ( \(n_{e}\) \(\propto\) (1+z) 1.2 ) from Abdurro’uf et al. ( 2024 ) . The electron density of the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies are consistent with typical star-forming galaxies, with no strong correlations with specific star-formation rate or far-infrared luminosity.</small>

#### Figure 9
![Figure 9](https://arxiv.org/html/x13.png)

图9：从O 32强线比推导出的电离参数（\(U\)）作为H \(\alpha\) 恒星形成率面密度的函数。对于ALMA – NIRSpec星系，这代表观测值（未经尘埃校正），而对于CEERS样本，我们显示的是本征值（经尘埃校正）。我们按[S ii ]推导的电子密度对星系着色，并显示来自Reddy et al.（2023）对CEERS巡天的参数拟合，形式为log \({}_{10}(U)\) = (0.378 \(\pm\) 0.021) \(\times\) log 10 (sSFR) \(-\) (2.655 \(\pm\) 0.011)。黑色箭头表示A V = 1的尘埃消光影响。ALMA – NIRSpec星系的观测值（未经尘埃校正）与经尘埃校正的CEERS星系一致，尽管统计数量较少。

<small>Figure 9 : Ionisation parameter ( \(U\) ), as derived from the O 32 strong-line ratio, as a function of H \(\alpha\) star-formation rate surface density. For the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies this represents the observed (dust-uncorrected) values whilst for the CEERS sample we show the intrsinc (dust-corrected) values. We colour the galaxies by [S ii ] derived electron density and show the parametric fit from Reddy et al. ( 2023 ) for the CEERS survey of the form log \({}_{10}(U)\) = (0.378 \(\pm\) 0.021) \(\times\) log 10 (sSFR) \(-\) (2.655 \(\pm\) 0.011). The black arrow indicates the impact of dust attenuation with A V = 1. The observed (dust-uncorrected) values of the ALMA – NIRSpec galaxies are consistent with dust-corrected CEERS galaxies, although with low number statistics.</small>

表1：48个远红外探测到的NIRSpec源的源属性，按红外光度降序排列，如图1所示。对于每个源，我们列出NIRSpec ID（第1列，C1）、ALMA ID（AS2UDS (A2-) 或 A3COSMOS (A3-) 或 ECOGAL (EG-)）（C3）、J2000 赤经（C5）、J2000 赤纬（C6）、NIRSpec光谱红移（C7）、ALMA主波束校正流量（C8）、ALMA波段、ALMA – NIRSpec间距（C10）。NIRSpec ID以JWST项目缩写（DD = DeepDive, RB = Rubies, JD = JADES, GR = George Rieke, GT = GTO, BA = BlueJay）后跟DJA目标ID（objid）给出。DJA光谱文件名包含在表格的在线版本中。没有ALMA ID的源来自相应ALMA档案程序的盲探测星表。被识别为AGN（见第4.2节）的源被高亮显示，其中\(\dagger\)表示宽发射线，\(\ddagger\)表示X射线对应体，\(*\)表示增强的光学谱线比。

(C6), NIRSpec spectroscopic redshift (C7), ALMA primary beam corrected flux (C8), ALMA Band, ALMA – NIRSpec separation (C10). The NIRSpec ID is given as JWST program acronym (DD = DeepDive, RB = Rubies, JD = JADES, GR = George Rieke, GT = GTO, BA = BlueJay) followed by the DJA object-id ( objid ). DJA spectra file names are included in the online version of the table. Sources with no ALMA ID originate from the blind detection catalogue of the respective ALMA archival program. ### [58] [Searching for Galaxy Cluster-Scale Strong lenses from the DESI Legacy Imaging Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.11054)
*Zhejian Zhang,Nan Li,Shude Mao,Hu Zou,Zizhao He,Mingxiang Fu,Shenzhe Cui*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (92/100) - 该论文聚焦于星系团尺度强引力透镜搜索，与用户的核心兴趣领域（强引力透镜、暗物质）高度吻合。虽然用户更关注星系-星系强透镜，但星系团透镜是强透镜的重要分支，且论文使用了深度学习方法和DESI巡天数据，与用户兴趣中的‘lens’、‘dark matter’、‘gravitational lensing: strong’等关键词匹配。论文不涉及用户明确要求降权的领域（如恒星物理、纯宇宙学等）。

TL;DR: 使用深度学习从DESI巡天数据中识别星系团引力透镜，通过迭代训练和人工筛选发现了485个高置信度候选体，其中247个是新发现的


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星系团尺度强引力透镜系统稀少但价值重大，可用于研究暗物质、暗能量及遥远宇宙。大规模巡天提供了扩展透镜样本的机会

Method: 采用基于ResNet-18的深度学习模型，使用模拟透镜图像作为正样本，观测非透镜图像作为负样本进行训练。通过迭代操作增加完整性，将发现的真阳性样本加入训练集多次训练。最后进行人工检查，按强透镜弧的显著性分为A、B、C等级

Result: 从540,432个星系团候选体中发现了485个高置信度引力透镜候选体，质量范围10^13.67-14.97 M⊙，红移范围0.04-0.89。排除先前研究已发现的，得到247个新发现候选体（16个A级、90个B级、141个C级）

Conclusion: 成功建立了星系团引力透镜候选体目录并公开，鼓励后续观测确认并深入研究这些系统

Abstract: Galaxy cluster-scale strong gravitational lensing systems are rare yet valuable tools for investigating the properties of dark matter and dark energy, as well as providing the opportunity to study the distant universe at flux levels and spatial resolutions that would otherwise be unavailable. Large-scale imaging surveys present unprecedented opportunities to expand the sample of cluster lenses. In this study, we adopt a deep learning-based approach to identify cluster lenses from the DESI Legacy Imaging Surveys, utilizing the catalog of galaxy cluster candidates identified by Zou et al. (2021). Our lens-finder employs a ResNet-18 architecture, trained with mock images of cluster lenses as positives and observational images of cluster scale non-lenses as negatives. We do an iterative operation to increase the completeness of our work, namely adding the found true positive samples back to the training set and training again for several times. Human inspection is conducted to further refine the candidates, categorizing them into grades (A, B, C) according to the significance of the strongly lensed arcs. Reviewing all 540,432 objects in Zou's catalog, we discover 485 high-confidence cluster lens candidates with a cluster $M_{500}$ range of $10^{13.67\sim14.97}M_{\odot}$ and a Brightest Central Galaxy (BCG) redshift range of $0.04\sim0.89$. After excluding the lens candidates listed in previous studies, we identify 247 newly discovered cluster lens candidates, including 16 grade A, 90 grade B, and 141 grade C. This catalog of cluster lens candidates is publicly available online, and follow-up observations are encouraged to confirm and conduct thorough investigations of these systems.

Abstract Translation:
星系团尺度的强引力透镜系统是稀有但宝贵的工具，可用于研究暗物质和暗能量的性质，并提供以其他方式无法获得的通量水平和空间分辨率来研究遥远宇宙的机会。大规模成像巡天为扩大星系团透镜样本提供了前所未有的机遇。在本研究中，我们采用基于深度学习的方法，利用Zou等人（2021）识别的星系团候选体目录，从DESI传统成像巡天中识别星系团透镜。我们的透镜查找器采用ResNet-18架构，以星系团透镜的模拟图像为正样本，以星系团尺度非透镜的观测图像为负样本进行训练。我们进行迭代操作以提高工作的完整性，即将找到的真阳性样本添加回训练集并再次训练多次。通过人工检查进一步筛选候选体，根据强透镜弧的显著性将其分为A、B、C三个等级。在审查Zou目录中的所有540,432个天体后，我们发现了485个高置信度的星系团透镜候选体，其星系团$M_{500}$范围为$10^{13.67\sim14.97}M_{\odot}$，最亮中心星系（BCG）红移范围为$0.04\sim0.89$。在排除先前研究中列出的透镜候选体后，我们识别出247个新发现的星系团透镜候选体，包括16个A级、90个B级和141个C级。该星系团透镜候选体目录已在线公开，鼓励进行后续观测以确认并深入研究这些系统。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，成功建立了星系团引力透镜候选体目录并公开，鼓励后续观测确认并深入研究这些系统。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/x1.png)

图1：我们的模拟程序的一个示例，边长为\(100^{\prime\prime}\)。左图：一个选定的非透镜星系团图像。中图：将要添加到星系团图像中的模拟弧图像，以及临界曲线（红色曲线）和焦散线（绿色曲线）。橙色十字表示星系团内成员星系的位置，青色十字表示源位置。右图：最终的模拟透镜图像。

<small>Figure 1: One example for our mock program, with side length of \(100^{\prime\prime}\) . Left: One selected non-lensed cluster image. Middle: The mock arc image to be added to the cluster image, together with the critical curves (red curve) and the caustics (green curve). The orange crosses indicate the positions of the member galaxies within the galaxy cluster, while the cyan cross indicate the source position. Right: The final mock lensing images.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/x3.png)

图3：从训练集中随机选取的800个模拟透镜的UMAP投影，包括我们手稿中定义的红（蓝星）、绿（蓝叉）和蓝（蓝菱形）源系统（见第II.2节）。红点表示来自COOL-LAMPS项目（Mork等人，2025）的177个星系团尺度强透镜的UMAP。

<small>Figure 3: UMAP projection of randomly selected 800 mock lenses from the training set, including the systems with red (blue star), green (blue cross), and blue (blue diamond) sources defined in our manuscript (See Section II.2 ). Red dots present the UMAP of 177 cluster-scale strong lenses from the COOL-LAMPS project (Mork et al. , 2025 ) .</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/x4.png)

图4：左图：在训练的最后一次迭代中，两种情况下训练集和验证集在200个训练周期上的交叉熵损失。在情况1中，我们采用Adam优化器，批大小为32，学习率为\(3\times 10^{-6}\)，权重衰减为\(1\times 10^{-1}\)。此外，在情况2中，我们使用初始学习率\(1\times 10^{-4}\)，最终学习率\(1\times 10^{-5}\)，权重衰减\(1\times 10^{-2}\)，并采用余弦退火。在周期20和90处的垂直虚线表示我们在两种情况下选择的早停点，即AUC的最高点（情况2），或训练损失变得异常之前的最高AUC（情况1）。中图：同一训练过程中ROC曲线下面积随周期的变化。右图：同一训练过程中AUC的导数随周期的变化。

<small>Figure 4: Left: The cross-entropy loss on the training and validation sets over 200 training epochs with two cases in the final iteration of our training. In Case 1, we adopt Adam optimizer, configured with a batch size of 32, a learning rate of \(3\times 10^{-6}\) , and a weight decay of \(1\times 10^{-1}\) . Moreover, in Case 2, We use a initial learning rate of \(1\times 10^{-4}\) , a final learning rate of \(1\times 10^{-5}\) , a weight decay of \(1\times 10^{-2}\) , with Cosine Annealing. The vertical dashed line at epoch 20 and 90 indicates the early stopping points we selected in the two cases, which is the highest point of the AUC (Case 2), or the highest AUC before the training loss become abnormal (Case 1). Middle: The Area Under the ROC curve as a function of epoch in the same training session. Right: The derivative of AUC as a function of epoch in the same training session.</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/x5.png)

图5：我们的分类器在验证集和测试集上分别评估的性能比较。左图显示我们的分类器在包含模拟图像的验证集上的ROC曲线（橙色线），曲线下面积（AUC=0.939）。以及我们的分类器在包含来自COOL-LAMPS项目（Mork等人，2025）的透镜候选体的测试集上的ROC曲线（蓝色线），曲线下面积（AUC=0.722）。右图显示上述两种情况的PR曲线。我们还用红色星号标记了最后一次迭代中采用的阈值（0.986）。

<small>Figure 5: Comparison of the performance of our classifier evaluated with validation and testing sets separately. The left panel shows the ROC curve (orange line) of our classifier on the validation set containing our mock images with the area under the curve (AUC=0.939). And the ROC curve (blue line) of our classifier on the testing set containing the lens candidates from the COOL-LAMPS project (Mork et al. , 2025 ) with the area under the curve (AUC=0.722). The right panel shows the PR curve for the above two cases. We also mark the threshold (0.986) adopted in last iteration with red stars.</small>

图6：我们的分类器在迭代过程中的性能。左图显示每次迭代的累积数量，包括所有候选体以及分别按三个等级显示。中图和右图显示将我们的分类器应用于包含来自COOL-LAMPS项目的透镜候选体的测试集时的纯度和完整性。

<small>Figure 6: Performance of our classifier along with the interations. Left Panel shows the cumulative number at each iteration, shown for all candidates and separately for the three grades. The middle and right panels shows the Purity and completeness when applying our classifier to the testing set containing the lens candidates from the COOL-LAMPS project.</small>

表2：迭代过程中发现的候选体统计，包括我们选择前4000个样本的阈值（Thresh.）；我们新发现候选体的最低分数（Thresh.TP）；我们新发现候选体的数量（New）和累积候选体数量（Cum.），以及A级到C级的累积候选体数量；在由COOL-LAMPS强透镜（Mork等人，2025）制作的测试集上的纯度（Purity）和完整性（Compl.）。

### [59] [Direct detection of cool molecular gas in a star-forming galaxy at $z=7.31$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13393)
*Karin Cescon,Jacqueline A. Hodge,Leindert A. Boogaard,Hiddo S. B. Algera,Lucie E. Rowland,Dominik A. Riechers,Renske Smit,Ilse De Looze,Rychard Bouwens,Paul van der Werf,Manuel Aravena,Elisabete da Cunha,Pratika Dayal,Andrea Ferrara,Rebecca Fisher,Hanae Inami,Pavel E. Mancera Piña,Pascal A. Oesch,Andrea Pallottini,Matus Rybak,Sander Schouws,Laura Sommovigo,Mauro Stefanon,Livia Vallini*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (90/100) - 该论文直接探测z=7.31星系REBELS-25的分子气体，与用户Zotero库中高权重的分子气体、星际介质、ALMA、尘埃、早期星系等主题高度吻合；作者包括a pallottini、manuel aravena、a ferrara等核心作者，且研究问题（早期星系气体含量、星际介质条件）与用户兴趣方向一致。

TL;DR: 该研究通过探测z=7.31星系REBELS-25的CO(3-2)和CO(7-6)发射线，确认了宇宙大爆炸后仅7亿年就存在一个极端巨大的分子气体库（约10¹¹ M☉），气体分数高达95%，并验证了[C II]作为早期宇宙分子气体示踪剂的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索早期宇宙（再电离时代）星系的分子气体含量和星际介质条件，以理解星系在宇宙最初十亿年内的快速质量积累过程。

Method: 利用VLA Q波段和ALMA Band 3观测CO(3-2)和CO(7-6)发射线，结合辐射传输代码TUNER自洽建模CO和尘埃连续谱发射，并考虑宇宙微波背景（CMB）的影响。

Result: 探测到CO(3-2)和CO(7-6)发射（均约3.5σ），获得分子气体质量约1.0×10¹¹ M☉（依赖α_CO假设）或1.8×10¹¹ M☉（通过TUNER建模），气体分数约0.95，气体尘埃比约600，消耗时标约1.2 Gyr，并推导出[C II]-H₂转换因子为60±25 M☉/L☉。

Conclusion: 该工作直接证实了z>7星系中低J CO发射的可探测性，为下一代观测设施铺平道路，并表明[C II]在再电离时代仍是可行的分子气体示踪剂，揭示了早期星系快速质量积累的关键信息。

Abstract: We investigate the molecular gas content and interstellar medium (ISM) conditions of REBELS-25, a massive, star-forming galaxy at $z=7.31$. Deep VLA Q-band and ALMA Band 3 observations reveal CO(3-2) and CO(7-6) emission (both at $\sim3.5σ$), and provide an upper limit on [C I](2-1). From the CMB-corrected CO(3-2) flux-representing the highest-redshift detection of a low-$J$ CO transition to date-we derive a molecular gas mass of $M_{\rm mol}=(1.0\pm0.4)\times10^{11}\,(α_{\rm CO}/(3\,$M$_{\odot}$(K$\,$\kms$\,$pc$^2)^{-1}))\,$M$_{\odot}$, directly confirming the presence of a very massive gas reservoir only $\simeq700\,$Myr after the Big Bang. This implies an extreme gas fraction of $f_{\rm gas}\simeq0.95$, a gas-to-dust ratio of $δ_{\rm GDR}\simeq6\times10^2$, and a depletion timescale of $τ_{\rm dep}\simeq1.2\,$Gyr, broadly consistent with extrapolated scaling relations for main-sequence galaxies at lower redshift. Using the radiative transfer code TUNER, we self-consistently model CO and dust continuum emission in the context of the significant CMB background, constraining ISM properties and recovering $M_{\rm mol}= (1.8^{+1.0}_{-0.9})\times10^{11}\,$M$_{\odot}$, independent of assumptions about $r_{31}$ and $α_{\rm CO}$. We further discuss the use of alternative molecular gas tracers at early epochs. Combining CO and [C II] measurements, we infer an empirical [C II]-to-H$_2$ conversion factor of $α_{\rm [C II]}=(60\pm25)\,$M$_{\odot}$/L$_{\odot}$, suggesting [C II] remains a viable molecular gas tracer in the Epoch of Reionization. These results demonstrate the detectability of low-$J$ CO emission even at $z>7$, paving the way for next-generation facilities, and provide critical insights into the rapid mass assembly of galaxies during the first billion years of cosmic history.

Abstract Translation:
我们研究了REBELS-25的分子气体含量和星际介质条件，这是一个红移z=7.31的大质量恒星形成星系。深度VLA Q波段和ALMA Band 3观测揭示了CO(3-2)和CO(7-6)发射（两者均为~3.5σ），并提供了[C I](2-1)的上限。根据经过宇宙微波背景修正的CO(3-2)通量——这是迄今为止对低J CO跃迁的最高红移探测——我们推导出分子气体质量为M_mol=(1.0±0.4)×10^11 (α_CO/(3 M_⊙ (K km s pc^2)^{-1})) M_⊙，直接证实了大爆炸后仅约700 Myr存在一个巨大的气体储库。这意味着极端的气体分数f_gas≈0.95、气尘比δ_GDR≈6×10^2以及消耗时标τ_dep≈1.2 Gyr，与较低红移主序星系的推断标度关系大致一致。利用辐射传输代码TUNER，我们在显著宇宙微波背景的背景下自洽地模拟了CO和尘埃连续谱发射，约束了星际介质性质，并恢复了M_mol=(1.8^{+1.0}_{-0.9})×10^11 M_⊙，独立于关于r_31和α_CO的假设。我们进一步讨论了早期宇宙中替代分子气体示踪剂的使用。结合CO和[C II]测量，我们推断出经验性的[C II]-H_2转换因子α_[C II]=(60±25) M_⊙/L_⊙，表明[C II]在再电离时代仍是可行的分子气体示踪剂。这些结果证明了即使在z>7时低J CO发射的可探测性，为下一代设施铺平了道路，并提供了对宇宙历史最初十亿年内星系快速质量积累的关键见解。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，该工作直接证实了z>7星系中低J CO发射的可探测性，为下一代观测设施铺平道路，并表明[C II]在再电离时代仍是可行的分子气体示踪剂，揭示了早期星系快速质量积累的关键信息。

( 2022 ) , the yellow hexagon represents HZ10 from Pavesi et al. ( 2019 ) , and green open triangles indicate SPT-selected DSFGs from Aravena et al. ( 2016 ) .</small>

<small>Figure 5: Evolution of the [C ii ]-to-H 2 conversion factor ( α [ C ​ ii ] \alpha_{\rm[C\,\textsc{ii}]} ) as a function of redshift. We include measurements drawn from the literature for main-sequence galaxies (MS), starburst galaxies (SB) and Lymann break analogues (LBA) (Stacey et al. , 1991 ; Ferkinhoff et al. , 2014 ; Huynh et al. , 2014 ; Magdis et al. , 2014 ; Capak et al. , 2015 ; Cormier et al. , 2015 ; Gullberg et al. , 2015 ; Schaerer et al. , 2015 ; Madden et al. , 2016 ; Accurso et al. , 2017 ; Contursi et al. , 2017 ; Hughes et al. , 2017 ; Zanella et al. , 2018 ; Rizzo et al. , 2020 , 2021 ) . The horizontal lines and shaded regions represent the mean and 1 σ \sigma scatter of the empirical α [ C ​ ii ] \alpha_{\rm[C\,\textsc{ii}]} calibrations from Zanella et al. ( 2018 ) (pink, solid line) and Zhao et al. ( 2024 ) (cyan, dashed line), and the median of the sample studied in Rizzo et al. ( 2021 ) (cornflower blue, dash-dotted line). The large star symbols indicate the α [ C ​ ii ] \alpha_{\rm[C\,\textsc{ii}]} values we derive for REBELS-25 using the CMB-corrected CO luminosity and assuming either α CO = 3 \alpha_{\rm CO}=3 (magenta) or α CO = 1 \alpha_{\rm CO}=1 (aqua). The yellow and orange hexagons both refer to HZ10 (see text; Pavesi et al. , 2019 ; Algera et al. , 2025a ) , the latter has been slightly offset in redshift to avoid overlapping error bars. The values derived for REBELS-25 are broadly consistent with most low- and intermediate-redshift studies, suggesting that the [C ii ] line remains an effective, though scattered, tracer of the molecular gas reservoir even at z > 7 z>7 .</small>

### [60] [The Early Maturity of High-Redshift Galaxies: Insights from sSFR, M/L and SFHs at z~7-14](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09139)
*P. Santini,M. Castellano,A. Calabrò,A. Fontana,E. Merlin,D. Bevacqua,P. Bergamini,S. Cantarella,L. Ciesla,A. Ferrara,S. L. Finkelstein,F. Fortuni,G. Gandolfi,T. Gasparetto,E. Giallongo,N. A. Grogin,S. T. Guida,A. M. Koekemoer,N. Menci,L. Napolitano,D. Paris,L. Pentericci,B. Perez-Diaz,B. Stoyanova,T. Treu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (90/100) - 论文聚焦JWST高红移星系（z~7-14）的恒星形成历史与sSFR演化，与用户Zotero库中JWST、高红移星系、恒星形成率等核心主题高度吻合；作者列表包含用户核心作者T. Treu、A. M. Koekemoer、A. Ferrara、S. L. Finkelstein，匹配度极高；方法上使用非参数SFH模型分析星系性质，与用户关注的恒星形成、尘埃、暗物质等方向紧密相关。

TL;DR: JWST观测发现z>10处存在意外多的UV亮星系，通过分析2420个z~7-14的星系样本，发现特定恒星形成率(sSFR)和质量-光度比(M/L)在红移范围内基本恒定，与多数理论模型存在矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST观测到z>10处存在超出预期的UV亮星系，理解这些高红移系统的物理特性和恒星形成历史对于区分不同理论模型至关重要。

Method: 从ASTRODEEP-JWST数据集中选取2420个z~7-14的可靠候选星系，使用非参数恒星形成历史模型分析其特定恒星形成率(sSFR)和恒星种群特性。

Result: 发现sSFR和M/L中值在探测的红移范围内基本恒定；样本显示广泛的物理条件和星系类型，包括z~10处已演化的星系；最高M/L星系在观测前至少500Myr形成大部分恒星；z>11星系通过随机恒星形成历史形成，早期保持UV暗，近期经历主要增长。

Conclusion: 观测到的sSFR演化与多数理论模型存在矛盾，成为区分竞争模型的关键参数；缺乏观测到的高sSFR系统表明任何无尘埃星暴阶段必须是短暂的；星系形成历史呈现多样性，包括早期演化和近期增长两种模式。

Abstract: The James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) has revealed an unexpected excess of UV-bright galaxies at z>10, unaccounted for by extrapolations from pre-JWST observations and theoretical models. Understanding the physical properties and star formation histories (SFH) of high redshift systems is key to distinguish between the different proposed scenarios. We identify and analyse a sample of 2420 robust candidates at z~7-14 drawn from the ASTRODEEP-JWST dataset over ~0.2 deg^2 and model their properties with non-parametric SFHs to derive their specific star formation rate (sSFR) and stellar population properties. We find that the median sSFR and M/L remain roughly constant across the probed redshift range. We show that this result is robust against potential systematics unless a hidden population of dust-enshrouded starbursts, undetectable in current data, exists at these redshifts. In any case, the absence of observed high-sSFR systems at the highest redshifts suggests that any dust-free starburst phase must be short-lived. The observed sSFR evolution is in tension with most (though not all) theoretical models, making it a key quantity for discriminating among competing scenarios. The sample shows a wide range of physical conditions and galaxy classes, including systems with low sSFR and high mass-to-light ratios (M/L) up to z~10, indicative of already evolved galaxies only a few hundred Myr after the Big Bang, and different degrees of dust attenuation. We finally attempt to reconstruct the assembly histories of two sub-samples: a) the highest-M/L galaxies at z~7-8, which appear to have formed the bulk of their stars at least 500 Myr before observation, implying progenitors observable as UV-bright sources at z>20, and b) z>11 galaxies, which formed through stochastic SFH, remaining UV-faint for most of their early evolution, before undergoing recent (~50 Myr old) episodes of major growth.

Abstract Translation:
詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（JWST）在红移z>10处发现了出乎意料的大量紫外明亮星系，这是基于JWST之前的观测外推和理论模型所未能预见的。理解高红移系统的物理性质和恒星形成历史（SFH）是区分不同提出方案的关键。我们从ASTRODEEP-JWST数据集中识别并分析了约0.2平方度范围内z~7-14的2420个稳健候选体，并使用非参数化SFH对其性质进行建模，以推导其比恒星形成率（sSFR）和星族性质。我们发现，中位sSFR和质光比（M/L）在探测的红移范围内大致保持恒定。我们表明，除非在这些红移处存在当前数据无法探测的隐藏尘埃包裹星暴群，否则这一结果对潜在系统误差是稳健的。无论如何，在最高红移处缺乏观测到的高sSFR系统表明，任何无尘埃星暴阶段都必须是短暂的。观测到的sSFR演化与大多数（尽管并非全部）理论模型存在矛盾，使其成为区分竞争方案的关键量。该样本展示了广泛的物理条件和星系类别，包括在z~10处具有低sSFR和高质光比（M/L）的系统，表明这些星系在大爆炸后仅几亿年就已演化，以及不同程度的尘埃消光。我们最终尝试重建两个子样本的组装历史：a) z~7-8处最高M/L的星系，它们似乎在观测前至少5亿年就形成了大部分恒星，这意味着其前体在z>20处可作为紫外明亮源被观测到；b) z>11的星系，它们通过随机SFH形成，在大部分早期演化中保持紫外暗淡，直到经历近期（约5千万年历史）的主要增长阶段。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要的结论：观测到的sSFR演化与多数理论模型存在矛盾，成为区分竞争模型的关键参数；缺乏观测到的高sSFR系统表明任何无尘埃星暴阶段必须是短暂的；星系形成历史呈现多样性，包括早期演化和近期增长两种模式。

### [61] [Probing Infrared eXcess to Investigate Early-Universe Dust (PIXIEDust)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.07964)
*Tom J. L. C. Bakx,Hiddo S. B. Algera,Jean-Baptiste Jolly,Clarke Esmerian,Kirsten Knudsen,Laura Sommovigo,Joris Witstok,Stefano Carniani,Jianhang Chen,Stephen Eales,Andrea Ferrara,Yoshinobu Fudamoto,Masato Hagimoto,Takuya Hashimoto,Hanae Inami,Akio K. Inoue,Theo Khouri,Ikki Mitsuhashi,Gunnar Nyman,Gustav Olander,Stephen Serjeant,Renske Smit,Ilsang Yoon,Jorge Zavala,Susanne Aalto,Caitlin M. Casey,Yoichi Tamura,Wouter Vlemmings*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (90/100) - 论文主题与用户Zotero库高度吻合，聚焦高红移星系尘埃、ALMA观测、早期宇宙尘埃形成等核心兴趣；多位作者（如A. Ferrara, Y. Fudamoto, S. Carniani, J. Chen, S. Serjeant）直接出现在用户核心作者列表中；方法（ALMA/NOEMA深度观测）与用户常用手段一致；结果对尘埃质量上限的约束与用户关注的尘埃、星际介质、恒星形成等主题紧密相关。

TL;DR: 对10个z>8高红移星系进行ALMA和NOEMA观测，未探测到显著尘埃发射，约束了尘埃质量和尘埃-恒星质量比的上限，表明早期宇宙尘埃积累效率低下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管高红移星系中通过红化的紫外发射暗示存在尘埃，但在z>8.3以上的（亚）毫米波段从未探测到尘埃发射。本研究旨在通过深度观测探索早期宇宙中尘埃的存在和性质。

Method: 结合约200小时的ALMA和NOEMA观测数据，对10个z>8星系进行分析。观测深度达到1σ灵敏度：158μm和88μm处2.0μJy，所有数据综合1.5μJy。按红移(8<z<9.5和9.5<z<15)、紫外连续谱斜率(βUV≶-2)和恒星质量(log10M*/M⊙≶9)进行分箱分析。

Result: 未探测到显著尘埃发射，约束平均尘埃质量在3σ置信度下低于10^5 M⊙，尘埃-恒星质量比低于3.7×10^-4（假设Tdust=50K，βdust=2.0）。分箱分析得到类似严格约束。

Conclusion: 结合其他研究，结果表明z>8宇宙中尘埃积累效率低下，可能原因包括超新星产生效率低、星际尘埃生长受限和/或外流导致的尘埃抛射。研究提供了在线数据和工具以促进高红移尘埃搜索。

Abstract: Despite the implied presence of dust through reddened UV emission in high-redshift galaxies, no dust emission has been detected in the (sub)millimetre regime beyond $z > 8.3$. This study combines around two hundred hours of Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA) and Northern Extended Millimeter Array (NOEMA) observations on ten $z > 8$ galaxies, revealing no significant dust emission down to a $1 σ$ depth of $2.0$, $2.0$, and $1.5 \,μ$Jy at rest-frame 158, 88 $μ$m, and across all the data, respectively. This constrains average dust masses to be below $< 10^{5}$ M$_{\odot}$ at $3 σ$ and dust-to-stellar mass ratios to be below $3.7 \times{} 10^{-4}$ (assuming $T_{\rm dust} = 50$ K and $β_{\rm dust} = 2.0$). Binning by redshift ($8 < z < 9.5$ and $9.5 < z < 15$), UV-continuum slope ($β_{\rm UV} \lessgtr -2$) and stellar mass ($\log_{10} M_{\ast}/{\rm M_{\odot}} \lessgtr 9$) yields similarly stringent constraints. Combined with other studies, these results are consistent with inefficient dust build-up in the $z > 8$ Universe, likely due to inefficient supernova production, limited interstellar grain growth and/or ejection by outflows. We provide data and tools online to facilitate community-wide high-redshift dust searches.

Abstract Translation:
尽管高红移星系中紫外发射的变红暗示了尘埃的存在，但在红移z > 8.3以上的（亚）毫米波段尚未探测到尘埃发射。本研究结合了阿塔卡马大型毫米/亚毫米阵列（ALMA）和北方扩展毫米阵列（NOEMA）对十个z > 8星系的约两百小时观测，在静止框架158微米、88微米以及所有数据中，分别未探测到显著的尘埃发射，1σ深度分别为2.0、2.0和1.5微央斯基。这限制了平均尘埃质量在3σ水平上低于10^5太阳质量，尘埃与恒星质量比低于3.7×10^{-4}（假设尘埃温度T_dust = 50 K，尘埃发射率指数β_dust = 2.0）。按红移（8 < z < 9.5和9.5 < z < 15）、紫外连续谱斜率（β_UV ≶ -2）和恒星质量（log10 M_*/M_⊙ ≶ 9）进行分箱分析，也得出了同样严格的限制。结合其他研究，这些结果与z > 8宇宙中尘埃积累效率低下的情况一致，可能原因包括超新星产生效率低、星际尘埃生长受限和/或外流导致的尘埃抛射。我们在线提供数据和工具，以促进社区范围内的高红移尘埃搜索。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要的总结：结合其他研究，结果表明z>8宇宙中尘埃积累效率低下，可能原因包括超新星产生效率低、星际尘埃生长受限和/或外流导致的尘埃抛射。研究提供了在线数据和工具以促进高红移尘埃搜索。

### [62] [Spatially Resolved Physical Properties of Young Star Clusters and Star-forming Clumps in the Brightest z>6 Galaxy, the Strongly Lensed Cosmic Spear at z=6.2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08054)
*Abdurro'uf,Dan Coe,Tom Resseguier,Calla Murphy,Xinfeng Xu,Angela Adamo,Namrata Roy,Alaina Henry,Vasily Kokorev,Gabriel Brammer,Seiji Fujimoto,Henry C. Ferguson,Amanda Pagul,Rogier A. Windhorst,Timothy Heckman,Jose M. Diego,Hollis B. Akins,Joseph Allingham,Ricardo O. Amorín,Danielle A. Berg,Maruša Bradač,Larry D. Bradley,Wenlei Chen,John Chisholm,Christopher J. Conselice,Pratika Dayal,Miroslava Dessauges-Zavadsky,Andreas L. Faisst,Steven L. Finkelstein,Yoshinobu Fudamoto,Lukas J. Furtak,Yuichi Harikane,Tiger Yu-Yang Hsiao,Yolanda Jimenez-Teja,Anton M. Koekemoer,Rebecca L. Larson,Ray A. Lucas,Matteo Messa,Lamiya Mowla,Minami Nakane,Gaël Noirot,Richard Pan,Massimo Pascale,Johan Richard,Massimo Ricotti,Luke Robbins,Daniel Schaerer,Fengwu Sun,Eros Vanzella,Brian Welch,Chris Willott,Adi Zitrin*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (89/100) - 论文聚焦于强引力透镜星系中极端致密星团的空间分辨研究，与用户Zotero库中强引力透镜、JWST、高红移星团、恒星形成等核心主题高度吻合。多位核心作者（Seiji Fujimoto, Yoshinobu Fudamoto, Christopher J. Conselice, Gabriel Brammer, Miroslava Dessauges-Zavadsky, Anton M. Koekemoer）直接参与，方法（JWST NIRCam/NIRSpec IFU空间分辨分析）和科学问题（早期宇宙恒星形成、星团形成机制）与用户兴趣高度一致。

TL;DR: JWST观测揭示了一个z=6.2的强引力透镜星系MACS0308-zD1（"宇宙之矛"）中的极端致密星团，这些星团半径约5pc，质量10^6-10^7太阳质量，表面密度超过10^4太阳质量/平方pc，年龄仅5-9百万年，但已形成引力束缚系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究早期宇宙（z>6）中星系的恒星形成过程，特别是通过JWST的高分辨率观测来探索高红移星系中的极端致密星团形成机制，这些星团比本地星团更致密、质量更大。

Method: 使用JWST的NIRCam成像和NIRSpec IFU光谱仪进行观测，覆盖了从紫外到光学波段的静止框架。利用引力透镜效应放大和解析星系结构，对星团进行空间分辨分析，测量其有效半径、恒星质量、表面密度和年龄等参数。

Result: 发现了三个极端致密的年轻星团（Reff~5pc，M*~10^6-10^7太阳质量，Σ*>10^4太阳质量/平方pc），年龄仅5-9百万年但已形成引力束缚系统。最亮星团的核心区域显示出被抑制的电离光子产生效率，可能表明存在反馈驱动的LyC逃逸通道。

Conclusion: 早期宇宙中存在比本地星团更致密、质量更大的极端致密星团，这些星团在很年轻时就能形成引力束缚系统。中心区域的电离光子产生效率抑制可能暗示着反馈机制促进了LyC光子的逃逸，这对理解早期宇宙的再电离过程具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present spatially resolved analysis of stellar populations in the brightest $z>6$ galaxy known to date (AB mag 23), the strongly lensed MACS0308$-$zD1 (dubbed the ``Cosmic Spear'') at $z_{\rm spec}=6.2$. New JWST NIRCam imaging and high-resolution NIRSpec IFU spectroscopy span the rest-frame ultraviolet to optical. The NIRCam imaging reveals bright star-forming clumps and a tail consisting of three distinct, extremely compact star clusters that are multiply-imaged by gravitational lensing. The star clusters have effective radii of $R_{\rm{eff}} \sim 5$ pc, stellar masses of $M_{*} \sim 10^{6}-10^{7}\,M_{\odot}$, and high stellar mass surface densities of $Σ_{*} > 10^{4}\,M_{\odot}~\rm{pc}^{-2}$. While their stellar populations are very young ($\sim 5-9$ Myr), their dynamical ages exceed unity, consistent with the clusters being gravitationally bound systems. Placing the star clusters in the size vs.~stellar mass density plane, we find they occupy a region similar to other high-redshift star clusters within galaxies observed recently with JWST, being significantly more massive and denser than local star clusters. Spatially resolved analysis of the brightest clump reveals a compact, intensely star-forming core. The ionizing photon production efficiency ($ξ_{\rm{ion}}$) is slightly suppressed in this central region, potentially indicating a locally elevated Lyman continuum escape fraction facilitated by feedback-driven channels.

Abstract Translation:
我们展示了已知最亮的z>6星系（AB星等23），即强引力透镜星系MACS0308-zD1（称为“宇宙之矛”，光谱红移z=6.2）中恒星族群的 spatially resolved 分析。新的JWST NIRCam成像和高分辨率NIRSpec IFU光谱覆盖了从紫外到光学的静止系波段。NIRCam成像揭示了明亮的恒星形成团块和一个由三个截然不同、极其致密的星团组成的尾状结构，这些星团因引力透镜效应而成像。这些星团的有效半径约为5秒差距，恒星质量约为10^6至10^7太阳质量，恒星质量面密度超过10^4太阳质量每平方秒差距。尽管它们的恒星族群非常年轻（约5-9百万年），但它们的动力学年龄超过1，这与星团是引力束缚系统一致。将这些星团置于大小与恒星质量面密度的平面中，我们发现它们占据了与最近JWST观测到的其他高红移星系中星团相似的区域，比本地星团显著更大质量和更致密。对最亮团块的 spatially resolved 分析揭示了一个致密、强烈恒星形成的核心。该中心区域的电离光子产生效率略有抑制，可能表明由反馈驱动的通道促进了局部莱曼连续谱逃逸分数。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，早期宇宙中存在比本地星团更致密、质量更大的极端致密星团，这些星团在很年轻时就能形成引力束缚系统。中心区域的电离光子产生效率抑制可能暗示着反馈机制促进了LyC光子的逃逸，这对理解早期宇宙的再电离过程具有重要意义。
