#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/macs0308-zD1_img_new.png)

图1：宇宙之矛（红移z=6.2）的NIRCam彩色图像（红色：F277W+F356W，绿色：F150W+F200W，蓝色：F090W+F115W），背景为红移z=0.356的星系团MACS J0308+2645。强透镜星系（右侧两图所示）分解为两个主要成分：一对大而明亮的恒星形成团块（1和2），以及一个包含三个不同星团（3、4和5）的弧，这些星团被多重成像为七个源（3a、3b、3c、4a、4b、5a和5b）。左上角插图为透镜模型识别出的对应像，显示团块形态，具有三个不同的子结构（下限）。红线表示红移z=6.2的透镜临界曲线，白线显示恒定放大率等高线。

<small>Figure 1: NIRCam color image (red: F277W+F356W, green: F150W+F200W, and blue: F090W+F115W) of the Cosmic Spear, at z = 6.2 z=6.2 , in the background of galaxy cluster MACS J0308+2645 at z = 0.356 z=0.356 . The strongly-lensed galaxy (shown in the two right panels) is resolved into two main components: a pair of large, bright star-forming clumps (1 and 2), and an arc containing three distinct star clusters (3, 4, and 5) which are multiply imaged into seven sources (3a, 3b, 3c, 4a, 4b, 5a, and 5b). The top-left corner inset shows a counter-image identified from the lens model. It reveals a clumpy morphology, with three distinct substructures (lower limit). The red line represents a lensing critical curve at z = 6.2 z=6.2 , while the white lines show contours of constant magnifications.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/galfit_result_venusimg_new_1.png)

图2：使用GALFIT对十一个NIRCam滤光片进行形态建模的结果。在建模中，星系被分解为十个成分：弧下宿主星系的弥散光（即尾状结构）、两个明亮团块，以及与星团多重像相关的七个致密源。在残差图像中，红色、白色和蓝色分别表示正值、零值和负值。约化卡方值显示在残差图的右下角。

<small>Figure 2: Results of morphological modeling using GALFIT applied to eleven NIRCam filters. In the modeling, the galaxy is decomposed into ten components: the diffuse light of the host galaxy underlying the arc (i.e., tail), two bright clumps, and seven compact sources associated with the multiple images of the star clusters. In the residual images, red, white, and blue colors are for positive, zero, and negative values, respectively. The reduced chi-square ( χ ν 2 \chi_{\nu}^{2} ) values are shown in the bottom-right corner of the residual maps.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/plot_datacube_nirspec_nircam.png)

图3：使用piXedfit结合NIRCam成像和NIRSpec IFU数据构建的光谱光度数据立方体。该数据立方体用于团块的 spatially resolved SED拟合。为创建数据立方体，数据集通过PSF匹配在空间和光谱上对齐至NIRSpec G395H/F290LP数据最长波长网格的空间分辨率，重采样至0.1角秒的像素尺度，并调整光谱与测光之间的归一化以确保一致性。左上图显示[OIII] λ5007图，由NIRSpec IFU数据在发射线波长中心窄波段（100埃）上积分光谱得到。其余图显示空间对齐和PSF匹配至NIRSpec IFU分辨率后的NIRCam图像。IFU的视场在左上图中可见，并在其他图中由白色方框标出。

<small>Figure 3: Spectrophotometric data cube constructed by combining NIRCam imaging and NIRSpec IFU data using piXedfit . This data cube is used for spatially resolved SED fitting of the clumps. To create the data cube, the datasets were spatially and spectrally aligned through PSF matching to the spatial resolution of the longest-wavelength grid of the NIRSpec G395H/F290LP data, resampling to a pixel scale of 0 ​ . ′ ′ ​ 1 0\farcs 1 , and aligning normalization between the spectra and the photometry for consistency. ### [63] [ALMA CO-CAVITY I. Resolved Molecular Gas in Void Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23399)
*D. Espada,S. B. De Daniloff,S. Duarte Puertas,M. Argudo-Fernández,U. Lisenfeld,S. Verley,I. Pérez,M. I. Rodríguez,T. Ruiz-Lara,R. García-Benito,L. Sánchez-Menguiano,M. Sánchez-Portal,A. Bongiovanni,S. F. Sánchez,A. Jiménez,R. E. Miura,G. Torres-Ríos,P. Villalba-González,Y. K. González-Koda,B. Bidaran,M. Alcázar-Laynez,A. Zurita,E. Florido,P. Vásquez-Bustos*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 与 Zotero 兴趣画像中的 alma, molecular, molecular gas 等主题/作者匹配。

TL;DR: 本文介绍了ALMA CO-CAVITY项目，利用ALMA望远镜对41个空洞星系（VGs）进行CO(1-0)巡天观测，结合CAVITY项目的光学IFU数据，实现了分子气体、恒星形成和恒星性质在像素级别的直接比较，并给出了数据产品、表面密度图和全局标度关系。研究发现空洞星系的标度关系与稠密环境中的星系兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环境在星系演化中起着关键作用，但大尺度环境和局部环境如何影响分子气体性质及其与恒星形成、恒星含量的关系仍不清楚。现有研究多集中在致密环境中的星系，对空洞星系（低密度环境）的详细分子气体性质研究匮乏。

Method: 采用ALMA干涉仪对41个空洞星系进行CO(1-0)分子气体观测，结合CAVITY项目的光学积分场单元（IFU）数据，构建像素级对比。生成数据立方体、矩图、位置-速度图，以及共同分辨率2.5角秒的表面密度图，并与已有巡天数据进行比较。

Result: 提供了ALMA数据产品（数据立方体、矩图、PV图等）和分辨率统一的表面密度图。发现样本很好地代表了空洞星系群体，但已有文献中的解析研究样本更偏大质量、更不孤立、位于更稠密的大尺度环境。分子气体主序散度最小（0.21 dex），其次是Schmidt-Kennicutt关系和恒星形成主序。空洞星系的标度关系与致密环境中的星系兼容。

Conclusion: ALMA CO-CAVITY项目为后续详细研究空洞星系分子气体性质及其与恒星形成关系奠定了基础，填补了低密度环境下分子气体高分辨研究的空白。从整体性质来看，空洞星系的标度关系与致密环境中的星系没有显著差异。

Abstract: The environment plays a key role in galaxy evolution, yet it remains unclear how detailed molecular gas properties and their connection to star formation and stellar content are influenced by both large-scale and local environments. Here we introduce the ALMA CO-CAVITY project, the first interferometric CO(1-0) survey of a large sample of 41 void galaxies (VGs) to characterise in detail their molecular gas properties. It is built over the CAVITY project, offering optical integral field unit (IFU) data, enabling a direct, pixel-to-pixel comparison between molecular gas (from ALMA), star formation, and stellar properties, as well as the derivation of their scaling relations. In this work we present ALMA data products for our sample, containing data cubes, moment maps and position-velocity diagrams at angular resolutions of 1 arcsec. We also present molecular gas, stellar mass, and star formation rate surface density maps at a common resolution of 2.5 arcsec. We contextualise our sample against representative unresolved and resolved surveys. While our sample provides a good representation of the VG population and follows the distribution of key properties seen in star-forming galaxy samples, galaxies included in resolved studies from the literature tend to be more massive, less isolated, and located in denser large-scale environments. We present global scaling relations for the ALMA CO-CAVITY sample and find that the molecular gas main sequence exhibits the smallest scatter (0.21 dex), followed by the Schmidt-Kennicutt relation and the star-forming main sequence. From integrated properties alone, we find that these scaling relations for VGs are compatible with those for denser environments. This paper lays the foundation for forthcoming studies exploiting this unique dataset.

### [64] [Massive Galaxies Form Early and Gray: Stellar Assembly and Dust Attenuation at $\mathbf{z>3.5}$ from CAPERS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13966)
*Katherine Chworowsky,Steven L. Finkelstein,Anthony J. Taylor,Alexa M. Morales,Mark Dickinson,L. Y. Aaron Yung,Pablo Arrabal Haro,Bren E. Backhaus,Davide Bevacqua,Óscar Chávez Ortiz,Adam C. Carnall,Callum T. Donnan,Mauro Giavalisco,Michaela Hirschmann,Kartheik G. Iyer,Anton M. Koekemoer,Rebecca L. Larson,Ray A. Lucas,Jed McKinney,Derek J. McLeod,Casey Papovich,Pablo G. Pérez-González,Lu Shen,Rachel S. Somerville,Laura Sommovigo,Thomas M. Stanton,Xin Wang,Stephen M. Wilkins,Jorge A. Zavala,the CAPERS Collaboration*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文利用JWST/NIRSpec光谱研究z>3.5大质量星系的恒星质量组装和尘埃消光，与用户画像中的高红移星系、尘埃、恒星形成历史等核心主题高度吻合。多位核心作者（如Koekemoer、Sommovigo、McKinney、Zavala）匹配，且论文聚焦于用户优先关注的星系形成与尘埃性质，而非纯宇宙学或恒星物理。

TL;DR: 利用JWST/NIRSpec光谱数据对148个高红移(z>3.5)大质量星系进行联合光谱-测光SED拟合，发现最质量星系（log M>10.5）呈现浅灰尘埃消光曲线，且其形成时间尺度比理论模型预测的更早，表明早期宇宙中大质量星系的增长比理论预期更快速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期宇宙（z≳4）中大质量星系（M⋆≳10¹⁰M⊙）的恒星质量组装过程是星系形成领域的核心挑战，其恒星形成历史由于测光数据固有的简并性而难以约束。

Method: 利用JWST/NIRSpec棱镜光谱数据（来自CAPERS巡天），对148个z>3.5、log(M⋆/M⊙)>9.5的星系进行联合光谱-测光SED拟合，采用灵活的恒星形成历史模型和尘埃模型。

Result: 最质量星系（log M>10.5）偏好浅灰尘埃消光曲线（高尘埃光学深度、大颗粒尺寸）；星系形成25%恒星质量的时间呈现显著多样性，但低sSFR星系形成更早；整体形成时间尺度比理论模型预测更早。

Conclusion: 早期大质量星系的增长比当前理论模型所捕捉到的更快，光谱约束与灵活的SFH和尘埃模型对重建高红移大质量星系形成历史至关重要。

Abstract: The stellar mass assembly of massive galaxies in the first few billion years of cosmic history remains a central challenge in galaxy formation. Galaxies with $M_\star \gtrsim 10^{10}M_\odot$ observed at $z \gtrsim 4$ must grow rapidly under conditions of intense gas accretion, feedback, and dust production. Observationally, their star-formation histories (SFHs) have been poorly constrained due to degeneracies inherent to broadband photometry. The advent of JWST enables direct spectroscopic access to detailed continuum shapes and rest-frame optical diagnostics at high redshift, providing a critical opportunity to reconstruct formation timescales of massive early galaxies. Here, we investigate massive galaxies using joint spectro-photometric SED fitting of JWST/NIRSpec prism spectroscopy from the CANDELS-Area Prism Epoch of Reionization Survey (CAPERS). Our sample comprises 148 galaxies selected photometrically with log $(M_\star/M_\odot) > 9.5$ at $z > 3.5$. We find that the most massive galaxies (log $(M_\star/M_\odot) > 10.5$) preferentially exhibit shallow, gray dust attenuation curves, consistent with higher dust optical depths and large grain sizes. We also find significant diversity in the time at which galaxies form 25% of their stellar mass. While formation timescales converge toward later cosmic times, galaxies with lower sSFR ($\lesssim -9$) at the observation epoch formed significantly earlier than systems with higher sSFRs. Across the full mass range, inferred assembly times are systematically earlier than model predictions, suggesting more rapid early growth than currently captured theoretically. These results underscore the importance of spectroscopic constraints and flexible SFH and dust models for reconstructing high-redshift massive galaxy formation histories.

Abstract Translation:
在宇宙历史的最初几十亿年里，大质量星系的恒星质量组装仍然是星系形成中的一个核心挑战。在红移 $z \gtrsim 4$ 处观测到的恒星质量 $M_\star \gtrsim 10^{10}M_\odot$ 的星系必须在强烈的气体吸积、反馈和尘埃产生条件下快速成长。观测上，由于宽带测光固有的简并性，它们的恒星形成历史（SFHs）一直难以被精确约束。JWST的出现使得直接光谱探测高红移处详细的连续谱形状和静止系光学诊断成为可能，为重建早期大质量星系的形成时标提供了关键机会。在此，我们利用来自CANDELS棱镜再电离时期巡天（CAPERS）的JWST/NIRSpec棱镜光谱，通过联合光谱-测光SED拟合来研究大质量星系。我们的样本包括148个通过测光选择的星系，其对数 $(M_\star/M_\odot) > 9.5$ 且 $z > 3.5$。我们发现，最庞大的星系（对数 $(M_\star/M_\odot) > 10.5$）倾向于表现出浅而灰的尘埃消光曲线，这与更高的尘埃光学深度和较大的尘埃颗粒尺寸一致。我们还发现星系形成其25%恒星质量的时间存在显著多样性。虽然形成时标趋向于更晚的宇宙时间，但在观测时刻具有较低比恒星形成率（$\lesssim -9$）的星系比具有较高比恒星形成率的系统形成得更早。在整个质量范围内，推断的组装时间系统性地早于模型预测，表明早期增长比当前理论捕捉到的更快。这些结果强调了光谱约束以及灵活的恒星形成历史和尘埃模型对于重建高红移大质量星系形成历史的重要性。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，早期大质量星系的增长比当前理论模型所捕捉到的更快，光谱约束与灵活的恒星形成历史和尘埃模型对重建高红移大质量星系形成历史至关重要。

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2605.13966v1/z_comp_DR0p4.png)

图2：CAPERS样本中星系测光红移与确认光谱红移的比较，颜色由 \(A_{V}\) 表示。星系被选择为具有测光红移 \(z_{{phot}}>3.5\)。虚线表示一对一关系，阴影区域具有 \(\Delta z=\) 0.5。虽然大多数源在测光和光谱红移之间显示出良好的一致性，但存在少量异常值，包括四个具有 \(z_{{phot}}>12\) 但 \(z_{{spec}}<7\) 的星系，这与高红移和尘埃红化的低红移测光解之间的已知简并性一致，并且它们作为可能的 \(z\sim 4-6\) 尘埃星暴星系（DSFGs）被包含在目标选择中。

<small>Figure 2: Comparison of photometric redshifts and confirmed spectroscopic redshifts for galaxies in the CAPERS sample, colored by \(A_{V}\) . Galaxies are selected to have photometric redshifts \(z_{{phot}}>3.5\) . The dashed line denotes the one-to-one relation with the shaded region having \(\Delta z=\) 0.5. While the majority of sources show good agreement between photometric and spectroscopic redshifts, a small number of outliers are present, including four galaxies with \(z_{{phot}}>12\) but \(z_{{spec}}<7\) , consistent with known degeneracies between high-redshift and dust-reddened lower-redshift photometric solutions, and were included in the target selection as likely \(z\sim 4-6\) DSFGs.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2605.13966v1/SED+SFH_panel_1.png)

图3：从Bagpipes拟合我们样本中四个星系的联合光谱和测光中恢复的SED。数据以灰褐色显示（测光显示为带有1 \(\sigma\) 误差棒的空心圆），模型拟合以黑色显示。阴影区域显示数据（恢复的拟合）的1 \(\sigma\) 误差（散布）。每个图中的插图显示了使用不同恒星形成历史参数化恢复的恒星形成历史：我们的基准Iyer等人（2019）恒星形成历史以黑色显示，Leja等人（2019）连续性恒星形成历史以蓝色显示，以及恒定恒星形成历史以红色显示（见§4.6）。Iyer等人（2019）恒星形成历史是本工作分析中使用的基准恒星形成历史。关于恒星形成历史的讨论见§ IV.6。插图中的垂直线显示了形成25%、50%和75%恒星质量的时间。面板（a）显示了我们样本中最庞大的星系，面板（b）是我们样本中红移最高的星系，面板（c）和（d）分别显示了具有中值恒星质量和红移的星系。包含所有分析星系（37张图像）的完整图集可在在线期刊中找到。

<small>Figure 3: Recovered SEDs from Bagpipes fitting of joint spectroscopy and photometry of four galaxies in our sample. The data is shown in taupe (photometry shown as open circles with 1 \(\sigma\) errorbars) and the model fit in black. The shaded region shows the 1 \(\sigma\) error (spread) in the data (recovered fit). The inset in each figure shows the recovered SFHs using different SFH parameterizations: our fiducial Iyer et al. ( 2019 ) SFH in black, Leja et al. ( 2019 ) Continuity SFH in blue, and a constant SFH in red (see §4.6). The Iyer et al. ( 2019 ) SFH is the fiducial SFH used in the analysis of this work. Discussion of the SFHs can be found in § IV.6 . The vertical lines in the inset show time at which 25%, 50%, and 75% of the stellar mass formed. Panel (a) shows the most massive galaxy in our sample, Panel (b) is the highest redshift galaxy in our sample, and Panels (c) and (d) show the galaxy with the median stellar mass and redshift, respectively. The complete figure set with all the galaxies analyzed (37 images) is available in the online journal.</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2605.13966v1/Mstar_comp_DR0p4.png)

图4：从联合光谱和测光SED拟合以及仅测光SED拟合得出的恒星质量估计的比较，颜色由红移表示。我们样本中的星系被选择为具有测光恒星质量 \(\log M_{\star}>9.5\)。开放的青色点表示由联合光谱-测光SED拟合推断的恒星质量定义的两个区间中的中值恒星质量：\(\log M_{\star}<9.5\) 和 \(\log M_{\star}\geq 9.5\)。虚线是一对一关系，而阴影区域显示 \(\pm\) 1 dex的范围。虽然总体一致性良好，但测光质量略高的微小偏差可能是由于宽带滤光片中星云发射被误认为恒星连续谱发射，而通过包含光谱可以更好地解耦。此外，由于测光质量选择，样本在对数 \((M_{\star}/M_{\odot})\) \(=9.5\) 以下是不完整的，这使低质量区间中的中值产生偏差，并导致其偏离一对一关系。

<small>Figure 4: Comparison of stellar mass estimates derived from joint spectroscopic and photometric SED fitting and from photometry-only SED fitting, colored by redshift. Galaxies in our sample were selected to have photometric stellar masses of \(\log M_{\star}>9.5\) . The open cyan points indicate the median stellar masses in two bins defined by the stellar mass inferred from joint spectro-photometric SED fitting: \(\log M_{\star}<9.5\) and \(\log M_{\star}\geq 9.5\) . The dashed line is a 1-to-1 relation while the shaded region shows a \(\pm\) 1 dex range. While overall agreement is good, a small deviation towards higher photometric masses is likely due to the misrepresentation of nebular emission as stellar continuum emission in broad band filters, which can be better decoupled with the inclusion of spectroscopy. Additionally, owing to the photometric mass selection, the sample is incomplete below log \((M_{\star}/M_{\odot})\) \(=9.5\) , which biases the median in the lower-mass bin and causes it to deviate from the one-to-one relation.</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/2605.13966v1/SFMS_sample_zbins_DR0p4.png)

图5：我们星系样本的恒星质量与恒星形成率（100 Myr平均）的关系，以跨越 \(3<z<9\) 的红移区间显示。Speagle等人（2014）的主序星系（SFMS）在 \(z=3\) –6的面板中以蓝色显示，而Cole等人（2025）的SFMS在 \(z=4.5\) –9的面板中以红色显示。阴影区域显示了这些关系的1 \(\sigma\) 散布。大多数星系位于或接近其各自红移处的SFMS，与这些时期典型的恒星形成系统一致。我们发现一个宁静星系（红色圆圈），其恒星形成率比其质量和红移处的SFMS低超过 \(3\sigma\)。Weibel等人（2025）的大质量宁静星系以绿色方块显示。我们没有将这个星系分类为宁静，因为恒星形成历史恢复显示在观测时间之前 \(\sim 20\) Myr有一次显著的恒星形成爆发，随后快速熄灭，这未被我们的100 Myr平均恒星形成率测量所捕捉。

<small>Figure 5: Stellar mass versus star-formation rate (averaged over 100 Myr) for our galaxy sample, shown in redshift bins spanning \(3 Speagle et al. ( 2014 ) SFMS is shown in blue for panels at \(z=3\) –6, while the Cole et al. ( 2025 ) SFMS is shown in red for panels at \(z=4.5\) –9. The shaded region shows the 1 \(\sigma\) spread in these relations. The majority of galaxies lie on or near the SFMS at their respective redshifts, consistent with typical star-forming systems at these epochs. We find one quiescent galaxy (red circle), classified as having a SFR more than \(3\sigma\) below the SFMS at their masses and redshift. The Weibel et al. ( 2025 ) massive quiescent galaxy is shown as a green square. We did not classify this galaxy as quiescent as the SFH recovery showed a significant burst of star-formation \(\sim 20\) Myr before the time of observation, followed by rapid quenching, which is not captured by our 100 Myr averaged SFR measurement.</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/2605.13966v1/binned_Av_curves.png)

图6：我们大质量星系样本恢复的消光曲线，按恒星质量（上）和红移（下）分箱。上：线条显示中值消光曲线，阴影区域为1 \(\sigma\) 散布。我们看到更庞大的星系倾向于表现出更浅的消光曲线，而较低质量的星系倾向于具有更陡的消光曲线和更大的散布。下：我们将整个星系样本分为低红移（ \(z<5.5\) ）和高红移（ \(z>5.5\) ）子样本。在低红移子样本中，我们进一步按恒星质量分为低质量（ \(\log M_{\star}<10.5\) ）和高质量（ \(\log M_{\star}>10.5\) ）子样本。我们看到，在低红移下，更庞大的星系具有更浅的消光曲线（ \(\delta>0\) ），而在高红移下，所有星系都表现出浅消光曲线，与低红移高质量子样本一致。

<small>Figure 6: Recovered attenuation curves of our sample of massive galaxies, binned by stellar mass (Top) and redshift (bottom). Top: The lines show median attenuation curves and the shaded region in the 1 \(\sigma\) spread. We see that more massive galaxies tend to exhibit shallower attenuation curves, while lower mass galaxies tend to have stepper attenuation curves with larger scatter. Bottom : We separate our full galaxy sample into a low- ( \(z 1 ), and there exists minimal evolution in slope for these galaxies, however, at \(z>5.5\) we see an evolution towards shallower attenuation curves.</small>

#### Figure 7
![Figure 7](https://arxiv.org/html/2605.13966v1/delta_stacked_horizontal_DR0p4.png)

图7：左：尘埃消光斜率参数 \(\delta\) 作为恒星质量函数的分布。更庞大的星系优先表现出比Calzetti消光曲线更浅的曲线（ \(\delta>0\) ），几乎所有质量超过 \(M_{\star}\sim 10^{10}M_{\odot}\) 的星系都具有比SMC定律更平坦的消光曲线。较低质量的星系涵盖更广的 \(\delta\) 范围，包括更陡的、类似SMC的消光。右：尘埃消光斜率 \(\delta\) 作为总消光 \(A_{V}\) 的函数。橙色圆圈是来自较低红移（ \(1.7<z<3.5\) ）JWST Blue Jay巡天（Maheson等人，2025）的结果。青色三角形是 \(z\sim 7\) 大质量（ \(9<\log M_{\star}<10\) ）星系（Fisher等人，2026），绿色方块显示了来自ALPINE-ALMA [C ii]巡天在 \(z\sim 5\) 处确定的尘埃性质（Boquien等人，2022）。粉色阴影曲线显示了根据JWST NIRCam对 \(\sim 3,800\) 个星系的观测确定的 \(\delta\) 从 \(z=1-9\) 的演化（Shivaei等人，2025）。存在对红移的弱依赖性，与总体相比，更高红移的星系具有更浅的消光曲线。

<small>Figure 7: Left: Distribution of the dust attenuation slope parameter \(\delta\) as a function of stellar mass. More massive galaxies preferentially exhibit shallower than Calzetti attenuation curves ( \(\delta>0\) ), with nearly all galaxies above \(M_{\star}\sim 10^{10}M_{\odot}\) having attenuation curves flatter than the SMC law. Lower-mass galaxies span a broader range of \(\delta\) , including steeper, SMC-like attenuation. Right: Dust attenuation slope \(\delta\) as a function of total attenuation \(A_{V}\) . The orange circles are results from lower redshift ( \(1.7 JWST Blue Jay survey (Maheson et al. , 2025 ) . The cyan triangles are \(z\sim 7\) massive ( \(9 (Fisher et al. , 2026 ) , and the green squares show dust properties as determined from the ALPINE-ALMA [C ii ] survey at \(z\sim 5\) (Boquien et al. , 2022 ) . The shaded pink curve shows evolution of \(\delta\) from \(z=1-9\) as determined from JWST NIRCam observations of \(\sim 3,800\) galaxies (Shivaei et al. , 2025 ) . There is a weak dependence on redshift, with higher redshift galaxies having shallower attentuation curves compared to the bulk of the population.</small>

### [65] [The galaxy-halo connection and the dynamical evolution of a giant disc in a massive node of the Cosmic Web at z~3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04144)
*G. Quadri,S. Cantalupo,C. Bacchini,A. Pensabene,A. Lupi,G. Pezzulli,W. Wang,M. Galbiati,T. Lazeyras,N. Ledos,H. Mao,A. Travascio*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文直接研究高红移(z~3)大质量盘状星系的暗物质晕性质、恒星形成效率及动力学演化，与用户画像中的强引力透镜、高红移星系动力学、宇宙正午等核心主题高度吻合。论文使用ALMA运动学数据和动力学建模，方法上与用户关注的星系动力学和气体研究一致。作者列表中虽无直接匹配的核心作者，但研究主题和方法与用户兴趣高度一致，且论文涉及高红移星系的多相气体和暗物质分布，属于用户优先关注的领域。

TL;DR: JWST发现了一个红移~3的巨型盘状星系"Big Wheel"，其尺寸是同类星系的近三倍。通过ALMA动力学数据和建模，研究者推断其暗物质晕质量约10^12.11 M☉，恒星质量约10^11.00 M☉，恒星-晕质量比显著高于预期，表明其恒星形成效率异常高，且近期演化平静，无大并合或强烈反馈事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST在红移~3的宇宙网节点中发现了一个异常巨大的盘状星系"Big Wheel"，其尺寸远超同期典型盘状星系，但其暗物质晕性质难以从JWST观测直接获取，因此需要结合动力学建模来理解其起源和形成历史。

Method: 结合基于物理的动力学模型与ALMA高分辨率运动学数据，利用JWST测光数据和CO运动学作为先验，推断暗物质晕质量和恒星质量。同时进行理想化星系的数值模拟，绝热演化25亿年以检验引力不稳定性。

Result: 暗物质晕质量log(Mh/M☉)=12.11^{+0.29}_{-0.17}，恒星质量log(M*/M☉)=11.00^{+0.11}_{-0.12}，恒星-晕质量比M*/Mh=0.06^{+0.04}_{-0.03}，显著高于已知的恒星-晕质量关系。数值模拟显示该星系在演化中未发展出引力不稳定性。

Conclusion: Big Wheel的恒星形成效率异常高，近期形成历史平静，可能没有经历大并合、剧烈盘不稳定性或强反馈事件。尽管此类星系罕见，但为高红移宇宙网节点中大质量盘星系的吸积和反馈贡献提供了新约束。

Abstract: Recent JWST observations revealed the surprising presence of a giant and massive disc galaxy in a Cosmic Web node at z$\sim3$. This galaxy, named the Big Wheel, has a size almost three times larger than expected for typical disc galaxies at the same redshift and similar stellar masses. Constraining the origin and formation history of the Big Wheel requires knowledge of its dark matter halo properties, which are difficult to derive from JWST observations alone. Here, we investigate the dark matter halo of the Big Wheel and provide further constraints on the galaxy baryonic content, combining a physically motivated dynamical model with deep ALMA kinematical data. By using priors based on JWST photometric data and CO kinematics, we infer a dark matter halo mass of $\log (M_{h}/M_{\odot})= 12.11^{+0.29}_{-0.17}$ and a stellar mass of $\log(M_{\star}/M_{\odot})=11.00^{+0.11}_{-0.12}$, leading to a stellar-to-halo mass (SHM) ratio of $M_\star/M_h=0.06^{+0.04}_{-0.03}$. This value is significantly higher than expected from state-of-the-art empirical SHM relations. This implies that the Big Wheel may have assembled its stellar content in a much more efficient way with respect to the general galaxy population at z$\sim3$. Combined with its morphological properties, our results suggest that the Big Wheel had a tranquil recent formation history, with probably no major mergers, violent disc instabilities, or strong ejective feedback. We perform a numerical simulation of an idealised galaxy and let it evolve adiabatically for $2.5$ Gyr to demonstrate that it does not develop gravitational instabilities during its evolution that could alter its resemblance to the observed one. Although systems alike the Big Wheel are arguably rare, our results offer new constraints on the contribution of accretion and feedback to the formation history of the most massive discs within high-redshift Cosmic Web nodes.

Abstract Translation:
最近的JWST观测揭示了一个令人惊讶的现象：在红移z~3的宇宙网节点中存在一个巨大且质量巨大的盘状星系。这个名为Big Wheel的星系，其大小几乎是相同红移和相似恒星质量的典型盘状星系的三倍。要限制Big Wheel的起源和形成历史，需要了解其暗物质晕的性质，而这很难仅从JWST观测中推导出来。在这里，我们结合基于物理的动力学模型和深ALMA运动学数据，研究了Big Wheel的暗物质晕，并进一步限制了星系的重子物质含量。通过使用基于JWST测光数据和CO运动学的前验信息，我们推断出暗物质晕质量为log(M_h/M_⊙)=12.11^{+0.29}_{-0.17}，恒星质量为log(M_⋆/M_⊙)=11.00^{+0.11}_{-0.12}，从而得到恒星-晕质量(SHM)比为M_⋆/M_h=0.06^{+0.04}_{-0.03}。这个值显著高于最先进的经验SHM关系的预期。这意味着Big Wheel可能以比z~3时一般星系群体更高效的方式组装了其恒星成分。结合其形态学特性，我们的结果表明Big Wheel近期形成历史平静，可能没有经历重大并合、剧烈的盘不稳定性或强烈的反馈喷流。我们进行了一个理想化星系的数值模拟，并让其绝热演化2.5 Gyr，以证明它在演化过程中不会发展出可能改变其与观测星系相似性的引力不稳定性。尽管像Big Wheel这样的系统可能很罕见，但我们的结果为高红移宇宙网节点中最巨大盘状星系的吸积和反馈对形成历史的贡献提供了新的限制。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，Big Wheel的恒星形成效率异常高，近期形成历史平静，可能没有经历大并合、剧烈盘不稳定性或强反馈事件。尽管此类星系罕见，但为高红移宇宙网节点中大质量盘星系的吸积和反馈贡献提供了新约束。

<small>Figure 1 : Best-fit parameters derived from the dynamical model of the Big Wheel galaxy obtained with dynesty , including, from left to right: the baryon fraction \(f_{bar}\) , the the stellar mass \(\log(M_{\star})\) , the bulge fraction \(f_{bulge}\) , the ratio between \(\alpha_{CO}\) and \(r_{41}\) , expressed as \(\beta\) , the scale radii of both the stellar and gaseous disc, \(R_{d,\star}\) and \(R_{d,gas}\) respectively, and the scale radius associated with the bulge \(R_{s,bulge}\) . Given the observational limitations discussed in Section 2 , the values and the distributions obtained for the scale radii of the gaseous disc and the stellar bulge are mostly driven by the choice of the priors.</small>

<small>Figure 3 : Derived stellar-to-halo mass (SHM) ratio for the Big Wheel (red diamond with \(1\sigma\) uncertainties along both axes), compared with the expected stellar-to-halo-mass relation (SHMR) from Moster et al. ( 2013 ) at \(z=3\) (solid blue line) and Shuntov et al. ( 2022 ) (dash-dotted green line; including only central halos). The errorbars on the Big Wheel point are obtained from the analysis presented in Figure 1 , while, the blue and green shaded areas represent the \(16^{th}\) to \(84^{th}\) percentiles obtained as discussed in Sec 3.2 . This figure shows that the SHM ratio of the Big Wheel is more than \(1\sigma\) away from the expected relations. The implication of this result are discussed in Section 5.1 .</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2605.04144v1/x4.png)

图4：基于为Big Wheel推导的最佳拟合参数（如图1所示）构建的理想化星系的数值模拟。顶部和底部面板分别显示了在模拟的五个不同时间（\(t=0.5\)、\(1\)、\(1.5\)、\(2\)和\(2.5\) Gyr）星系的正面气体和恒星表面密度图。在整个时间演化过程中，气体和恒星分布均未表现出任何全局引力不稳定性的出现。特别是，旋臂不断形成和瓦解，在演化过程中产生了如棒和伪核球等子结构。然而，全局盘结构得以保持。

<small>Figure 4 : Numerical simulation of an idealized galaxy built from the best-fit parameters derived for the Big Wheel and presented in Figure 1 . The top and the bottom panels, show, respectively, the gaseous and the stellar surface density maps of the galaxy, shown face-on, at five different times during the simulation ( \(t=0.5\) , \(1\) , \(1.5\) , \(2\) , and \(2.5\) Gyr). Throughout the entire time evolution, both the gas and the stellar distributions do not exhibit the onset of any global gravitational instabilities. In particular, spiral arms are continuously formed and disrupted, giving rise to substructures like a bar and a pseudo-bulge during the evolution. However, the global disc structure remains preserved.</small>

### [66] [Resolved Maps of Gas and Dust in a Massive Quiescent Galaxy at z=2 from INQUEST-JWST: Evidence of Accretion and Rejuvenation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.26195)
*Sai Gangula,Andrew B. Newman,Meng Gu,Sirio Belli,Katherine E. Whitaker,Tania M. Barone,Aliza Beverage,Andrea Bolamperti,Letizia Bugiani,Richard S. Ellis,Mariska Kriek,Allison Matthews,Themiya Nanayakkara*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文直接研究了一个强引力透镜星系（MRG-M0138）在z~2的高红移宁静星系中的气体和尘埃分布，使用了JWST/NIRSpec IFU高空间分辨率观测，核心科学问题（气体吸积、再活跃、AGN反馈）与用户兴趣高度吻合。论文涉及尘埃、气体运动学、恒星形成历史等用户高频关键词，且方法（IFU、吸收线）和主题（高红移星系、引力透镜）均与用户画像强匹配。

TL;DR: 利用JWST/NIRSpec IFU对红移约2的引力透镜现象星系MRG-M0138进行观测，通过Na I D吸收线追踪中性气体的分布与运动学，发现气体与恒星盘共转、存在非平衡结构（如离核团块、尘埃带），结合恒星形成历史揭示500 Myr前的再活跃事件，表明气体来自潮汐吸积，并解释了早期宁静星系气体含量差异的原因及AGN反馈燃料机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遥远宇宙中的宁静星系具有不同的气体含量，暗示多种熄灭机制在起作用，但此前对气体分布和运动学的观测几乎都是未分辨的，因此需要高空间分辨率的观测来追溯气体起源。

Method: 使用JWST/NIRSpec IFU对引力透镜星系MRG-M0138进行观测，在219个空间分块中利用Na I D吸收线（扣除恒星吸收后）追踪中性气体的运动学和空间分布。

Result: 气体呈现清晰的旋转运动，且与恒星盘运动学对齐；气体和尘埃具有复杂的空间结构，包括离核团块、尘埃带和外盘斑块；非平衡分布表明气体是吸积而来的；恒星形成历史分析显示500 Myr前存在再活跃事件；识别出两个可能相关的伴星系；在距离已知超大质量黑洞约90 pc处探测到气体团块。

Conclusion: 早期宁静星系的气体含量差异并非完全由气体消耗时标不同导致；潮汐相互作用是气体吸积的可能来源；探测到靠近超大质量黑洞的气体团块为间歇性AGN反馈提供燃料机制，有助于维持星系的宁静状态。

Abstract: Quiescent galaxies in the distant universe exhibit a range of gas content that may indicate a variety of quenching processes are at play. Mapping the distribution and kinematics of the gas can illuminate its origins, but nearly all such observations have been unresolved. We present JWST/NIRSpec IFU observations of MRG-M0138, a gravitationally lensed, massive quiescent galaxy at $z\sim2$ observed as part of the INQUEST-JWST survey. We use Na I D absorption, which we detect in excess of the stellar absorption over most of the galaxy, to trace the kinematics and spatial distribution of the neutral gas in 219 spatial bins. The gas exhibits clear rotation that is kinematically aligned with the stellar disk. Both the gas and dust have a complex spatial structure, including an off-nuclear clump, a dust lane, and patches in the outer disk. The non-equilibrium distribution suggests that the gas was accreted. Analysis of the galaxy's star formation history supports this interpretation by indicating a rejuvenation event 500 Myrs ago. We identify two plausibly associated galaxies and suggest that tidal interactions are a likely source of the accreted gas. Our results indicate that some of the variation in gas content among early quiescent galaxies is not related to differences in gas consumption timescales. The detection of a gas clump at a projected distance of $\sim90$ pc from the known supermassive black hole illustrates a mechanism to fuel the episodic AGN feedback that may maintain quiescence.

Abstract Translation:
遥远宇宙中的宁静星系表现出多种气体含量，这可能表明多种淬灭过程在起作用。绘制气体的分布和运动学可以揭示其起源，但几乎所有此类观测都未得到空间分辨。我们展示了作为INQUEST-JWST巡天一部分的JWST/NIRSpec IFU对MRG-M0138的观测，这是一个引力透镜化的、大质量宁静星系，红移$z\sim2$。我们利用Na I D吸收线（我们在大部分星系中探测到其超出恒星吸收的部分）来追踪219个空间分 bin 中中性气体的运动学和空间分布。气体表现出清晰的旋转，且运动学上与恒星盘对齐。气体和尘埃都具有复杂的空间结构，包括一个离核团块、一条尘埃带以及外盘中的斑块。这种非平衡分布表明气体是被吸积的。对星系恒星形成历史的分析支持了这一解释，表明在500 Myr前发生了一次复苏事件。我们识别出两个可能相关的星系，并认为潮汐相互作用是吸积气体的可能来源。我们的结果表明，早期宁静星系中气体含量的一些差异与气体消耗时标的差异无关。在距离已知超大质量黑洞投影距离约$\sim90$ pc处探测到一个气体团块，说明了一种为可能维持宁静状态的间歇性AGN反馈提供燃料的机制。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要：早期宁静星系的气体含量差异并非完全由气体消耗时标不同导致；潮汐相互作用是气体吸积的可能来源；探测到靠近超大质量黑洞的气体团块为间歇性AGN反馈提供燃料机制，有助于维持星系的宁静状态。

图1：红移\(z=1.948\)的透镜化宁静星系MRG-M0138的JWST/NIRSpec观测。左上：使用F115W、F150W和F356W滤光片获得的透镜星系团MACS J0138.0–2155的JWST/NIRCam图像。MRG-M0138呈现为一个明亮、红色、多重成像的源。黄色方框表示NIRSpec IFU视场。右上：以IFU视场为中心的放大视图。叠加的黑色网格描绘了空间分 bin（共219个）。底部：从一个示例空间分 bin（黑色）提取的光谱，\(1\sigma\)不确定度显示为灰色阴影区域。红色曲线代表使用pPXF得出的最佳拟合恒星连续谱和星云发射模型。标出了显著的光谱特征，包括Na I D和Ca II H \(\&\) K。

<small>Figure 1: JWST/NIRSpec observations of the lensed quiescent galaxy MRG-M0138 at \(z=1.948\) . Top left: JWST/NIRCam image of the lensing galaxy cluster MACS J0138.0–2155 obtained with the F115W, F150W, and F356W filters. MRG-M0138 appears as a bright, red, multiply imaged source. The yellow box indicates the NIRSpec IFU field of view. Top right: Zoomed-in view centered on the IFU field of view. The overlaid black grid delineates the spatial bins (219 in total). Bottom: The spectrum extracted from one example spatial bin (black), with the \(1\sigma\) uncertainty shown as the grey shaded region. The red curve represents the bestfit stellar continuum and nebular emission model derived using pPXF . Prominent spectral features, including Na I D and Ca II H \(\&\) K, are indicated.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2604.26195v1/x2.png)

图2：在G140M光谱中一个示例空间分 bin（与图1中使用的分 bin相同）中观测到的Na I D吸收线。左图：将观测光谱\(F\)（黑色）与最佳拟合pPXF恒星模型（橙色）进行比较，上图中[Na/Fe]* = 0，下图中[Na/Fe]* = +0.6。波长已转换到星系的系统静止参考系。右图：相应的气体吸收光谱\(F_{gas}=F/F_{*}\)（黑色）和最佳拟合Voigt模型（橙色），上图中[Na/Fe]* = 0，下图中[Na/Fe]* = +0.6。在所有图中，绿色虚线显示Na I D双线在静止参考系中的波长。

<small>Figure 2: Na I D absorption lines observed in an example spatial bin (same bin used in Figure 1 ) in the G140M spectra. Left panels: The observed spectrum \(F\) (black) is compared to the best-fit pPXF stellar model (orange) with [Na/Fe]* = 0 in the top panel and [Na/Fe]* = +0.6 in the bottom panel. Wavelengths are shifted to the systemic rest-frame of the galaxy. Right panels: The corresponding gas absorption spectra \(F_{gas}=F/F_{*}\) (black) and the best-fit Voigt model (orange) with [Na/Fe]* = 0 in the top panel and [Na/Fe]* = +0.6 in the bottom panel. In all panels, the green dashed lines show the rest-frame wavelengths of the Na I D doublet lines.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2604.26195v1/x3.png)

图3：表征过量Na I D吸收的部分覆盖分数Voigt轮廓参数的后验分布角图，这些参数是在将观测光谱除以最佳拟合恒星连续谱pPXF模型后，在与图1和图2相同的空间分 bin中获得的。对于每个参数，橙色线标记中位数，黑色虚线表示\(16^{\text{th}}\)和\(84^{\text{th}}\)百分位数。除了模型参数外，我们还为导出量\(\log(N\times C_{f})\)增加了一行和一列。虽然这不是拟合中的自由参数，但该组合比单独的\(\log N_{Na~I}\)或\(C_{f}\)受到更严格的约束，突出了模型中的一个关键简并性。

<small>Figure 3: Corner plot of the posterior distributions for the Partial Covering fraction Voigt profile parameters characterizing excess Na I D absorption, obtained after dividing the observed spectrum by the best-fit stellar continuum pPXF model, in the same spatial bin used in the Figure 1 and 2 . For each parameter, the orange line marks the median, and the black dashed lines indicate the \(16^{\text{th}}\) and \(84^{\text{th}}\) percentiles. In addition to the model parameters, we include an extra row and column for the derived quantity \(\log(N\times C_{f})\) . Although not a free parameter in the fit, this combination is more tightly constrained than either \(\log N_{Na~I}\) or \(C_{f}\) individually, highlighting a key degeneracy in the model.</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2604.26195v1/x4.png)

图4：气态Na I D等值宽度（\(EW_{gas}\)）的径向轮廓，通过将观测光谱除以最佳拟合恒星连续谱模型后的残余吸收测量得到。椭圆半径定义为\((x^{2}+(y/q)^{2})^{1/2}\)，其中\(x\)和\(y\)分别是分 bin在星系长轴和短轴上的投影，\(q=0.28\)是F200W滤光片中星光平均轴比。显示了两种假设恒星钠丰度下的径向轮廓：[Na/Fe]* \(=0.0\)（左图）和[Na/Fe]* \(=+0.6\)（右图）。我们平均了来自G140M和G235M观测的\(EW_{gas}\)测量值。在两幅图中，红色虚线表示核球有效半径\((R_{e,bulge})\)，绿色点划线表示整个星系的有效半径\((R_{e})\)。

<small>Figure 4: Radial profiles of the gaseous Na I D equivalent width ( \(EW_{gas}\) ), measured from the residual absorption after dividing the observed spectrum by the best-fit stellar continuum model. The elliptical radius is defined as \((x^{2}+(y/q)^{2})^{1/2}\) , where \(x\) and \(y\) are projections of a bin onto the major and minor axes of the galaxy, respectively, and \(q=0.28\) is the mean axial ratio of the starlight in the F200W filter. Radial profiles are shown for two assumed stellar sodium abundances: [Na/Fe]* \(=0.0\) ( left panel ) and [Na/Fe]* \(=+0.6\) ( right panel ). We averaged the \(EW_{gas}\) measurements from the G140M and G235M observations. In both plots, the dashed red line denotes the bulge effective radius \((R_{e,bulge})\) , and the dot dashed green line denotes the effective radius of the entire galaxy \((R_{e})\) .</small>

![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/2604.26195v1/x5.png)

图5：在空间积分光谱中探测到星际Ca II H、K吸收。左图：将观测到的叠加光谱（黑色）与最佳拟合pPXF恒星模型（橙色）进行比较。中图：观测光谱与最佳拟合恒星模型之比（黑色）显示出在Ca II H、K处有过量吸收的证据，如第III.4节所述，该吸收被建模（橙色）。右图：与中图相同，但波长区域围绕Na I D。钠吸收要强得多，这解释了为什么它可以在单个空间分 bin中被探测到。

Left panel : The observed stacked spectrum (black) is compared to the best-fit pPXF stellar model (orange). Right panel : As in the middle panel, but in the wavelength region around Na I D. The sodium absorption is much stronger, explaining why it is detectable in individual spatial bins.</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/2604.26195v1/x6.png)

图6：从Na I D测量的气体运动学稳健性测试。左列和右列分别关注速度（\(V_{gas}\)）和速度弥散（\(\sigma_{gas}\)）。第一行：假设\({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=0\)时，从两次观测（G140M和G235M）提取的气体运动学比较。第二行：使用G140M观测，假设[Na/Fe]* = 0或+0.6时推断的气体运动学比较。第三行：说明覆盖分数\(C_{f}\)对气体运动学的影响。我们计算了当\(C_{f}\)值处于前10百分位数（\(V_{gas,\uparrow C_{f}},~\sigma_{gas,\uparrow C_{f}}\)）和后10百分位数（\(V_{gas,\downarrow C_{f}},~\sigma_{gas,\downarrow C_{f}}\)）时后验样本的中位速度和速度弥散。在前两行中，红色虚线是1:1线，而绿色线和\(1\sigma\)误差带显示线性拟合。在所有图中，速度和速度弥散的单位是\(km~s^{-1}\)。

<small>Figure 6: Tests of the robustness of the gas kinematics measured from Na I D. The left and right columns focus on the velocities ( \(V_{gas}\) ) and velocity dispersions ( \(\sigma_{gas}\) ), respectively. Top row: Comparisons of the gas kinematics extracted from the two observations (G140M and G235M), assuming \({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=0\) . Middle row: Comparisons of the gas kinematics inferred when assuming [Na/Fe]* = 0 or +0.6 in the analysis, using the G140M observations. Bottom row: Illustration of the influence of the covering fraction \(C_{f}\) on the gas kinematics. We calculated the median velocity and velocity dispersion of the posterior samples when the \(C_{f}\) value is in top 10th percentile ( \(V_{gas,\uparrow C_{f}},~\sigma_{gas,\uparrow C_{f}}\) ) and bottom 10th percentile ( \(V_{gas,\downarrow C_{f}},~\sigma_{gas,\downarrow C_{f}}\) ). In the top two rows, the red dashed line is the 1:1 line, while the green line and \(1\sigma\) error band shows a linear fit. In all the plots, the units of velocity and velocity dispersion are \(km~s^{-1}\) .</small>

![Figure 7](https://arxiv.org/html/2604.26195v1/x7.png)

图7：气体和尘埃分布与运动学图。（A）使用NIRCam F115W、F150W和F356W滤光片在源平面重建的星系图像，如Newman等人（2025）所述。（B）恒星速度场。（C）假设\({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=0\)时Na I D的速度。（D）假设\({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=0\)时的\(C_{f}\times N_{Na~I}\)图。该乘积代表空间分 bin上的平均柱密度。（E）假设\({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=+0.6\)时的\(C_{f}\times N_{Na~I}\)图。（F）F115W–F200W颜色。（G）从我们的SPS建模导出的\(A_{V}\)图。虚线分 bin标记未达到稳健气体运动学\(\Delta AIC\)阈值的区域。中心右下方的白色叉号因SN Encore（Pierel等人，2024）的污染而被排除。所有空间图中坐标系的原点设置在星系中心，由Newman等人（2025）报告的表面亮度峰值确定。所有气体量代表G140M和G235M测量值的平均值。轴的单位是角秒（\(1^{\prime\prime}=8.6\) kpc）。

<small>Figure 7: Maps of the distribution and kinematics of gas and dust. (A) Reconstructed image of the galaxy in the source plane using the NIRCam F115W, F150W, and F356W filters as in Newman et al. ( 2025 ) . (B) The stellar velocity field. (C) The velocity of Na I D, assuming \({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=0\) . (D) The \(C_{f}\times N_{Na~I}\) map, assuming \({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=0\) . This product represents the average column density over the spatial bin. (E) The \(C_{f}\times N_{Na~I}\) map assuming \({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=+0.6\) . (F) The F115W–F200W color. (G) The \(A_{V}\) map derived from our SPS modeling. Dotted bins mark regions that did not meet the \(\Delta AIC\) threshold for robust gas kinematics. The white cross to the lower-right of the center was excluded due to contamination from SN Encore (Pierel et al. , 2024 ) . The origin of the coordinate system in all spatial maps is set at the galaxy’s center, as determined from the surface brightness peak reported by Newman et al. ( 2025 ) . All gas quantities represent the average of the G140M and G235M measurements. The axis units are arcsec ( \(1^{\prime\prime}=8.6\) kpc).</small>

#### Figure 8
![Figure 8](https://arxiv.org/html/2604.26195v1/x8.png)

图8：气体和恒星速度场的比较。左图和右图分别显示分析中假设\({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=0\)和+0.6的结果。恒星和气体速度明显相关，气体滞后于恒星旋转速度的量取决于假设的[Na/Fe]*。绘制了通过显著性阈值（第III.3节）的每个空间分 bin，使用了G140M和G235M数据集的平均值。红色虚线表示\(V_{star}=V_{gas}\)，绿色实线及其\(1\sigma\)误差带显示线性拟合。紫色菱形表示沿尘埃带的区域，橙色方块表示靠近星系中心的气体。这些气体和尘埃增强的区域在运动学上似乎没有不规则性。

<small>Figure 8: A comparison of the gas and stellar velocity fields. The left and right panels show results assuming \({[Na/Fe]^{*}}=0\) and +0.6, respectively, in the analysis. The stellar and gas velocities are clearly correlated, with the gas lagging the stellar rotation speed by an amount that depends on the assumed [Na/Fe]*. Each spatial bin that passes our significance threshold (Section III.3 ) is plotted, using the average of the G140M and G235M data sets. The red dashed lines represent \(V_{star}=V_{gas}\) , and the green solid lines with \(1\sigma\) error bands show linear fits. The purple diamonds indicate the region along the dust lane, while the orange squares mark the gas close to the galaxy center. These regions of enhanced gas and dust do not appear to be kinematically irregular.</small>

### [67] [Metal Mayhem at $\rm z \sim 7-10$: Diversity and Evolution of Gas-Phase Metallicity Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07076)
*Maria Koller,Roberto Maiolino,Hannah Übler,Qiao Duan,Jan Scholtz,Santiago Arribas,William M. Baker,Stefano Carniani,Stephane Charlot,Mirko Curti,Luca Graziani,Gareth Jones,William McClymont,Michele Perna,Bruno Rodríguez Del Pino,Sandro Tacchella,Alessandra Venditti,Giacomo Venturi,Joris Witstok*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文使用JWST/NIRSpec-IFU研究z~7-10星系的金属丰度梯度，核心关注高红移星系动力学、星际介质混合及气体吸积过程，与用户对高红移星系动力学和强引力透镜研究的兴趣高度契合。作者中包含用户核心作者Hannah Übler，且论文涉及低金属丰度、卫星星系相互作用等前沿主题，与用户Zotero库中的'cosmic noon'、'dense gas'、'lens'等关键词及高红移星系演化方向一致。

TL;DR: JWST观测发现早期宇宙（z=7.2-9.5）低金属丰度星系存在多样化的金属丰度梯度，卫星星系偏离本地基本金属丰度关系，表明存在原始气体吸积和相互作用驱动的星际介质混合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究早期宇宙（红移z=7.2-9.5）星系的金属丰度梯度分布，探索星系在宇宙最初十亿年内的演化机制，特别是低金属丰度系统中的气体吸积、相互作用和反馈过程。

Method: 使用JWST/NIRSpec-IFU观测7个低金属丰度星系系统，测量其金属丰度梯度。样本包括主星系（log(M*/M⊙)∼7.8-9.5）和3个卫星星系，分析其金属丰度、恒星形成率等参数，并与本地基本金属丰度关系进行比较。

Result: 1. 星系金属丰度梯度变化范围大（从正到负），平均梯度为-0.02±0.04 dex kpc⁻¹；2. 卫星星系金属丰度极低（3%-4% Z⊙），显著偏离本地基本金属丰度关系（ΔFMR≈-0.9 dex）；3. 有卫星星系的系统呈现平坦梯度，表明潮汐相互作用驱动星际介质混合；4. 两个源可能存在AGN，反馈可能导致平坦梯度；5. 一个源检测到正梯度，表明金属贫乏气体直接流入星系中心。

Conclusion: 早期宇宙星系通过多样化的、间歇性的过程生长，包括原始气体吸积、潮汐相互作用、合并事件和反馈机制。这些结果表明早期演化具有结构多样性，而非单一可预测的路径。

Abstract: We present a JWST/NIRSpec-IFU study of metallicity gradients in seven low-metallicity systems at $z=7.2-9.5$. The main sample spans stellar masses of $\rm \log(M_*/M_{\odot}) \sim 7.8-9.5$, star formation rates (SFRs) of $\rm \log(\text{SFR} / M_{\odot} \text{yr}^{-1}) \sim 0.5-2.5$, and gas-phase metallicities of $4\%-15 \%~Z_\odot$. Within our sample, we also identify three low-metallicity satellite galaxies associated with two of our sources, providing a rare view of early-epoch interactions. The three satellites exhibit even more primordial properties, with metallicity $3\% -4\% ~Z_\odot$ and low star-formation activity ($\rm \log(\text{SFR} / M_{\odot} \text{yr}^{-1}) \sim -0.5$ to $-0.9$). We find that our galaxies, and especially the satellites, are significantly offset from the local Fundamental Metallicity Relation (FMR), with deviations reaching $Δ\text{FMR} \approx -0.9$ dex. This indicates that these galaxies are likely experiencing strong accretion of pristine gas. Overall, we observe a large scatter in radial metallicity gradients, ranging from positive to negative with an average metallicity gradient of $\rm -0.02 \pm 0.04 \ dex \ kpc^{-1}$. Flat gradients are found in systems with confirmed satellites, suggesting that tidal interactions and mergers drive the radial mixing necessary to homogenise the interstellar medium. The (tentative) presence of an AGN in two of our sources suggests that strong feedback may also be responsible for the observed flat gradients. Conversely, the detection of a positive gradient in one source points toward a direct funnelling of metal-poor gas inflow into the central region of the galaxy. These results show that galaxies in the first billion years grow through diverse, episodic processes, suggesting that early evolution is characterised by structural variety rather than a single, predictable path.

Abstract Translation:
我们利用JWST/NIRSpec-IFU对七个低金属丰度系统（红移z=7.2-9.5）的金属丰度梯度进行了研究。主样本的恒星质量范围为log(M_*/M_⊙) ~ 7.8-9.5，恒星形成率（SFR）为log(SFR / M_⊙ yr^{-1}) ~ 0.5-2.5，气相金属丰度为4%-15% Z_⊙。在样本中，我们还识别出与两个源相关的三个低金属丰度卫星星系，提供了早期宇宙相互作用的罕见视角。这三个卫星星系表现出更原始的性质，金属丰度为3%-4% Z_⊙，恒星形成活动较低（log(SFR / M_⊙ yr^{-1}) ~ -0.5至-0.9）。我们发现，我们的星系，尤其是卫星星系，显著偏离了局部基本金属丰度关系（FMR），偏差达到ΔFMR ≈ -0.9 dex。这表明这些星系可能正在经历强烈的原始气体吸积。总体而言，我们观测到径向金属丰度梯度存在较大离散，范围从正梯度到负梯度，平均金属丰度梯度为-0.02 ± 0.04 dex kpc^{-1}。在确认存在卫星星系的系统中发现了平坦梯度，表明潮汐相互作用和并合驱动了星际介质均匀化所需的径向混合。两个源中（初步）存在的活动星系核（AGN）表明，强烈的反馈也可能导致观测到的平坦梯度。相反，在一个源中检测到的正梯度指向金属贫乏气体流入直接汇聚到星系中心区域。这些结果表明，第一批十亿年内的星系通过多样化的、间歇性的过程生长，表明早期演化的特征在于结构多样性，而非单一可预测的路径。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要，早期宇宙星系通过多样化的、间歇性的过程生长，包括原始气体吸积、潮汐相互作用、合并事件和反馈机制。这些结果表明早期演化具有结构多样性，而非单一可预测的路径。

### [68] [Survival of the most compact: the life and death of satellite halos in self-interacting dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19362)
*David Klemmer,Moritz S. Fischer,Kimberly K. Boddy,Manoj Kaplinghat,Laura Sagunski*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文聚焦于自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）子晕的演化，并明确指出其密度剖面多样性会在强引力透镜系统中留下可观测印记，与用户对暗物质、强引力透镜及子晕结构的核心兴趣高度吻合。论文开发的高效模拟框架直接服务于强透镜观测预言，属于用户首要兴趣领域。

TL;DR: 开发了模拟自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）子晕演化的计算框架，重点关注速度/角度依赖的散射截面，通过虚拟宿主粒子模拟子晕-晕相互作用，比全分辨率模拟更高效，揭示了SIDM子晕密度分布的更大多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）模型通过暗物质粒子间的短程相互作用，可能产生独特的星系旋转曲线内区多样性和引力透镜特征。卫星星系和暗物质子晕为测试这些模型提供了重要场所，但需要开发高效模拟框架来研究子晕演化。

Method: 开发了N体模拟框架，将主晕解析处理，使用虚拟宿主粒子模拟散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用过程。采用Eddington反演方法精确建模晕中的局部速度分布。该方法比全分辨率宿主模拟计算成本显著降低，同时包含潮汐剥离和潮汐加热效应。测试了各向同性和前向主导的自散射两种极限情况。

Result: 环境效应（特别是散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用）对子晕演化有强烈影响，驱动复杂的结构演化。SIDM子晕相比无碰撞暗物质具有更大的中心密度范围和密度剖面斜率多样性。计算高效的模拟框架能够建模真实环境中的SIDM子晕。

Conclusion: 准确建模散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用对于预测SIDM子晕密度剖面至关重要。研究的SIDM模型中，子晕质量剖面增强的多样性将在强透镜系统和卫星星系中留下可观测印记。

Abstract: Self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) models feature short-range interactions between dark matter (DM) particles that lead to larger diversity in the inner parts of galactic rotation curves and potentially unique gravitational lensing signatures. Satellite galaxies and dark subhalos provide a valuable testing ground for such models. We develop a simulation framework to explore subhalo evolution and its gravothermal collapse for velocity- and angle-dependent self-interacting cross section in these SIDM models. Our results are essential for testing these models. We perform N-body simulations, treating the host halo analytically and modelling the scattering-induced subhalo-halo interaction process using virtual host particles, a central innovation of our work. We use the Eddington inversion method to accurately model the local velocity distribution in the halo. Our approach is significantly less computationally expensive than simulations with a fully resolved host, while incorporating tidal stripping and tidal heating. We test both isotropic and forward-dominated self-scattering, which represent limiting cases for the angular dependence of the self-interaction cross section. Environmental effects, especially the scattering-induced subhalo-halo interaction, have a strong impact on the subhalo evolution and drive a complex structural evolution. As a result, SIDM subhalos have a larger range of central densities and density profile slopes compared to collisionless DM. Our cost-efficient simulation framework enables modelling of SIDM subhalos in realistic environments. Our results highlight the necessity of accurately modelling the scattering-induced subhalo-halo interaction to predict SIDM subhalo density profiles. For the SIDM models we investigate, the enhanced diversity in the mass profiles of subhalos would leave an observable imprint on strong lensing systems and satellite galaxies.

Abstract Translation:
自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）模型具有暗物质（DM）粒子之间的短程相互作用，这导致星系旋转曲线内部部分具有更大的多样性，并可能产生独特的引力透镜信号。卫星星系和暗子晕为检验此类模型提供了宝贵的试验场。我们开发了一个模拟框架，用于探索这些SIDM模型中速度依赖和角度依赖的自相互作用截面下的子晕演化及其引力热坍缩。我们的结果对于检验这些模型至关重要。我们进行了N体模拟，解析地处理主晕，并使用虚拟主晕粒子模拟散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用过程，这是我们工作的核心创新。我们使用爱丁顿反演方法精确模拟晕中的局部速度分布。我们的方法在计算上比完全解析主晕的模拟要经济得多，同时包含了潮汐剥离和潮汐加热。我们测试了各向同性和前向主导的自散射，它们代表了自相互作用截面角度依赖性的极限情况。环境效应，特别是散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用，对子晕演化有强烈影响，并驱动了复杂的结构演化。因此，与无碰撞暗物质相比，SIDM子晕具有更大范围的中心密度和密度轮廓斜率。我们经济高效的模拟框架能够在现实环境中对SIDM子晕进行建模。我们的结果强调了精确模拟散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用以预测SIDM子晕密度轮廓的必要性。对于我们研究的SIDM模型，子晕质量轮廓增强的多样性将在强透镜系统和卫星星系中留下可观测的印记。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，准确建模散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用对于预测SIDM子晕密度剖面至关重要。研究的SIDM模型中，子晕质量剖面增强的多样性将在强透镜系统和卫星星系中留下可观测印记。

The notation \({eo}={A}\) – \({B}\) denotes the apocentre (A) and pericentre (B) distances, given in units of the host’s scale radius, \(r_{{s,\,host}}\) . ### [69] [JWST's PEARLS: A clumpy ring galaxy at $z = 4.0148$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11575)
*David Vizgan,Ming-Yang Zhuang,Ian Smail,Rogier Windhorst,Gibson Bowling,Cheng Cheng,Seth Cohen,Christopher Conselice,Jose Diego,Brenda Frye,Norman Grogin,Rolf Jansen,Patrick Kamieneski,Anton Koekemoer,Rafael Ortiz,Massimo Ricotti,Bangzheng Sun,Hayley Williams,S. P. Willner,Aadya Agrawal,Manuel Solimano,Zachary Stone,Joaquin Vieira,Chentao Yang*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 论文研究了一个红移z=4.0148的候选环星系，其形态可能与强引力透镜效应混淆，直接涉及用户核心兴趣领域（强引力透镜、星系-星系强透镜）。论文使用JWST和HST进行高红移星系观测，与用户画像中的JWST、高红移星系、尘埃、恒星形成等关键词高度匹配。虽然论文主要结论倾向于碰撞环星系，但明确讨论了引力透镜作为可能的解释，并建议透镜巡天考虑此类污染源，这对用户的研究有直接参考价值。

TL;DR: 这篇论文研究了一个红移z=4.0148的候选环星系，通过HST和JWST观测发现其具有复杂的环状结构，可能是碰撞形成的环星系，但也不能完全排除引力透镜效应的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环星系是研究星系演化动力学过程的重要对象，特别是碰撞形成的环星系。随着JWST时代的到来，高红移碰撞环星系的发现和研究变得可能，这有助于理解早期宇宙中的星系形成和演化过程。

Method: 使用HST/ACS、JWST/NIRCam和JWST/NIRSpec对红移z=4.0148的候选环星系进行多波段观测，分析其形态、恒星形成率和恒星质量等物理性质。

Result: 观测显示该星系具有复杂的环状形态，包含三个明亮团块，环半径约1.8千秒差距。恒星形成率为140 M☉/年，恒星质量为log(M*/M☉)=10.41，与其他高红移碰撞环星系相似。

Conclusion: 该星系很可能是碰撞形成的环星系，但不能完全排除引力透镜效应的可能性。需要高分辨率光谱观测来确认其性质。建议当前和未来的引力透镜巡天应考虑高红移环星系作为可能的污染源。

Abstract: Ring galaxies are an uncommon class of galaxies whose morphology is closely related to dynamical processes that govern galaxy evolution. Some ring galaxies, known as "collisional ring galaxies", are thought to form as a consequence of head-on collisions between galaxies, and a number of high-redshift collisional ring galaxies have been discovered and/or studied in the era of the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST). In this paper, we present HST/ACS, JWST/NIRCam, and JWST/NIRSpec observations of a candidate ring galaxy at $z_{\rm spec} = 4.0148$, previously identified as a potential gravitational lens. The galaxy exhibits a complex morphology, including three bright clumps along an apparent ring with radius $\approx 0.25$" $\simeq 1.8$ kpc. It has a total SFR $= 140^{+20}_{-30}$ ${\rm M}_{\rm \odot}$ yr$^{-1}$ and $\log(M_\ast/{\rm M}_\odot) = 10.41^{+0.11}_{-0.13}$, making it similar to other high-redshift collisional ring galaxies. Although we argue strongly in favor of the collisional ring explanation, we cannot entirely rule out a galaxy-galaxy strong lensing explanation for the system's morphology, in which a foreground galaxy at $z \simeq 1.7$ lenses a galaxy at $z \simeq 4.0$ into an Einstein ring-like configuration; to confirm the nature of this source, we require kinematic information via high spectral resolution observations. We suggest that current and future gravitational lens surveys should consider high-redshift ring galaxies as possible but significant contaminants.

Abstract Translation:
环星系是一类不常见的星系，其形态与支配星系演化的动力学过程密切相关。一些环星系，被称为“碰撞环星系”，被认为是由星系之间的正面碰撞形成的。在詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜时代，已经发现和/或研究了一些高红移碰撞环星系。本文介绍了哈勃空间望远镜ACS、JWST/NIRCam和JWST/NIRSpec对一个候选环星系的观测结果，该星系位于$z_{\rm spec} = 4.0148$，先前被识别为一个潜在的引力透镜。该星系呈现出复杂的形态，包括沿一个半径约为$0.25"$ $\simeq 1.8$ kpc的环状结构上的三个明亮团块。其总恒星形成率SFR $= 140^{+20}_{-30}$ ${\rm M}_{\rm \odot}$ yr$^{-1}$，$\log(M_\ast/{\rm M}_\odot) = 10.41^{+0.11}_{-0.13}$，使其与其他高红移碰撞环星系相似。尽管我们强烈支持碰撞环的解释，但我们不能完全排除星系-星系强透镜效应对该系统形态的解释，即一个红移$z \simeq 1.7$的前景星系将一个红移$z \simeq 4.0$的背景星系透镜成类似爱因斯坦环的构型；为了确认该天体的性质，我们需要通过高光谱分辨率观测获得运动学信息。我们建议当前和未来的引力透镜巡天应将高红移环星系视为可能但重要的污染源。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，该星系很可能是碰撞形成的环星系，但不能完全排除引力透镜效应的可能性。需要高分辨率光谱观测来确认其性质。建议当前和未来的引力透镜巡天应考虑高红移环星系作为可能的污染源。

图1：左：MACS0416星团的4角分2伪RGB图像，使用JWST NIRCam F115W + F150W作为蓝色，F200W + F277W作为绿色，F356W + F444W作为红色。环星系的位置用洋红色方框标出。右：候选环星系在JWST F150W成像中的\(2\arcsec\)局部放大图（上）和CRG的\(2\arcsec\)重新缩放RGB局部放大图（下），使用了F150W、F200W和F356W滤光片（分别对应\(z=4.0148\)处的静止波长0.30、0.40和0.71 \(\mu\) m）。在上图中，我们以红色等高线显示了来自ALCS巡天（Fujimoto et al. , 2024 ）的\(\sim 3\sigma\) ALMA探测。CRG的JWST成像清晰地揭示了环状形态；我们已缩放RGB局部放大图的通道以突出环绕系统红色中心的团块状蓝色环。

<small>Figure 1: Left: 4 arcmin 2 pseudo-RGB image of the MACS0416 cluster, using JWST NIRCam F115W + F150W as blue, F200W + F277W as green, and F356W + F444W as red. The location of the ring galaxy is indicated in a magenta box. Right: \(2\arcsec\) cutout of the candidate ring galaxy in JWST F150W imaging (top) and \(2\arcsec\) re-scaled RGB cutout of the CRG (bottom), using the F150W, F200W, and F356W filters (corresponding to rest-frame wavelengths of 0.30, 0.40, and 0.71 \(\mu\) m respectively at \(z=4.0148\) ). In the top panel, we show the \(\sim 3\sigma\) ALMA detection from the ALCS survey (Fujimoto et al. , 2024 ) as a red contour. The JWST imaging of the CRG clearly reveals a ring morphology; we have scaled the channels of the RGB cutout to emphasize the clumpy blue ring surrounding the red center of the system.</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.11575v2/Figure2.png)

<small>Figure 2: 2 \(\arcsec\) cutouts of the ring galaxy as observed by HST ACS (F606W and F814W) and JWST NIRCam (F090W, F115W, F150W, F200W, F277W, F356W, and F444W) at their native resolutions. The bottom-right cutout panel shows a rescaled RGB image from the NIRCam data using F277W (red), F150W (green), and F090W (blue) to further highlight the red center vs. blue ring. The magenta box shows the region from which the NIRSpec PRISM data were taken. These data products (2D spectrum and integrated 1D spectrum) are shown in the bottom half of the figure. We have scaled the contrast in the cutouts and 2D spectra to highlight important features, showing a red continuum exhibiting strong emission lines from a source at \(z=4.0148\) , with emission lines that appear to encompass the spatial extent of the continuum source. The vertical dashed lines indicate the location of expected emission lines at \(z=4.0148\) , and are included with annotations to demonstrate a match with the spectroscopic redshift of the galaxy.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.11575v2/Figure3.png)

图3：上：在将空间分辨率匹配到F444W后，HST ACS和JWST NIRCam成像的2 \(\arcsec\)局部放大图。右下角局部放大图是图1中原始NIRCam分辨率的RGB图像。RGB局部放大图中的比例尺适用于所有面板。RGB面板中的圆圈标记了用于多波段测光和SED建模的五个孔径：团块A（红色）、B（蓝色）和C（绿色）、中心（橙色）和总流量（白色虚线）。洋红色矩形表示图2中光谱的狭缝。下：每个孔径内的流量密度与观测波长的关系，颜色编码与上方面板相同。在SED拟合之前，每个测光点都乘以了5%的流量不确定度（以二次方形式相加）。来自bagpipes的最佳拟合SED模型，假设所有孔径的\(z=4.0148\)，以实线显示，证明了测光结果与来自CANUCS（Sarrouh et al. , 2026 ）的光谱红移之间极好的一致性。

<small>Figure 3: Top: 2 \(\arcsec\) cutouts of HST ACS and JWST NIRCam imaging, after matching the spatial resolution to F444W. The bottom-right cutout is the RGB image from Figure 1 at native NIRCam resolution. The scale bar in the RGB cutout applies to all panels. Circles in the RGB panel mark the five apertures used for the multi-band photometry and SED modeling: clumps A (red), B (blue), and C (green), the center (orange) and the total flux (white, dashed line). The magenta rectangle indicates the slit for the spectra in Figure 2 . Bottom: Flux density versus observed wavelength within each aperture, as color coded in the top panel. A 5% flux uncertainty was multiplied in quadrature to each photometric point before SED fitting. The best-fit SED models from bagpipes , assuming \(z=4.0148\) for all apertures, are shown as solid lines, demonstrating excellent agreement between the photometry and the spectroscopic redshift from CANUCS (Sarrouh et al. , 2026 ) .</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.11575v2/Figure4.png)

图4：左：来自CRG外围两个伴星测光的最佳拟合SED模型（中位数和1 \(\sigma\)误差），其测光红移与CRG的光谱红移相似。右：F277W图像的模型减除后2″局部放大图。减除的发射被建模为二维Sérsic轮廓。图像缩放旨在突出附近的伴星和从环边缘延伸出的臂状潮汐特征。可能的伴星系的位置和孔径大小由虚线圆圈指示。具有\(z_{phot}\sim 4\)的两个团块以红色着色，如右图所示，而其他以蓝色着色的团块具有\(z_{phot}\sim 1.0-1.5\)，很可能是前景源。

<small>Figure 4: Left: Best-fit SED models (median and 1 \(\sigma\) error) from photometry of two companions on the outskirts of the CRG with photometric redshifts that are similar to the spectroscopic redshift of the CRG. Right: Model-subtracted, 2″ cutout of the F277W image. The subtracted emission is modeled as a 2D Sérsic profile. The image scaling is tuned to highlight the nearby companions and the arm-like tidal feature extending from the edge of the ring. The locations and aperture sizes used for possible companion galaxies are indicated by the dashed circles. The two clumps with \(z_{phot}\sim 4\) are colored red, as in the right panels, while the other clumps, colored in blue, have \(z_{phot}\sim 1.0-1.5\) , and are most likely foreground sources.</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.11575v2/Figure5.png)

图5：左：流量密度与观测波长的关系，绘制了来自两个HST和七个JWST宽滤光片图像的测光点（绿色方块）。这些数据取自对应于图3中所示“中心”（以及右图中的绿色圆圈）的孔径。橙色和蓝色光谱分别代表红移\(z=4.0148\)的星系团块与最佳拟合红移为\(z=1.66\)的前景引力透镜的bagpipes模型。\(z\simeq 4\)的解更好地描述了测光结果，并且预测的\(z\simeq 1.7\)源SED在\(3.2-5.0\) \(\mu\) m之间显示出若干条在NIRSpec数据中未发现的谱线（见图2）。右：从F200W成像中减除F182M成像的缩放版本；我们计算了一个“校正因子”，考虑了星系“中心”附近的弥散星光，该因子来自洋红色孔径内包围的流量。

<small>Figure 5: Left: Flux density versus observed wavelength, plotting photometric points from the two HST and seven JWST wide-filter images in the green squares. These data are taken from an aperture corresponding to the “center” shown in Figure 3 (and the green circle in the right panel). The orange and blue spectra represent bagpipes models of a galaxy clump at \(z=4.0148\) versus a foreground gravitational lens with a best-fit redshift of \(z=1.66\) . The \(z\simeq 4\) solution better describes the photometry, and the predicted source SED at \(z\simeq 1.7\) exhibits a number of lines between \(3.2-5.0\) \(\mu\) m that are not found in the NIRSpec data (see Figure 2 ). Right: A scaled version of F182M imaging subtracted from the F200W imaging; we calculate a “corrective factor”, accounting for diffuse starlight near the “center” of the galaxy, from the flux enclosed within the magenta aperture.</small>

#### Figure 6
![Figure 6](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.11575v2/Figure6.png)

图6：低红移环星系比较样本（Shimakawa et al. , 2024 ）和选定的高红移环星系样本（Yuan et al. , 2020 ; Liu et al. , 2023 ; Nestor Shachar et al. , 2025 ; Perna et al. , 2025 ）（包括本工作研究的星系）的恒星形成主序。我们使用Popesso et al. ( 2023 )的参数化主序进行进一步比较。我们发现，迄今为止观测到的高红移环星系比其低红移对应物具有高得多的恒星形成率，并且位于\(z=2-4\)的恒星形成主序之上或之上。

<small>Figure 6: The star-forming main-sequence (SFMS) for a comparison sample of low-redshift ring galaxies (Shimakawa et al. , 2024 ) and a selected sample of high-redshift ring galaxies (Yuan et al. , 2020 ; Liu et al. , 2023 ; Nestor Shachar et al. , 2025 ; Perna et al. , 2025 ) , including the galaxy studied in this work. We use the parametrized main sequences from Popesso et al. ( 2023 ) for further comparison. We find that observed high-redshift ring galaxies to date have much higher SFR than their lower-redshift analogs, and lie on or above the SFMS at \(z=2-4\) .</small>

#### Figure 7
![Figure 7](https://arxiv.org/html/2603.11575v2/Figure7.png)

图7：左：一个经过充分表征的光学选择强透镜系统样本（SLACS、BELLS、SL2S；Bolton et al. , 2008 ; Brownstein et al. , 2012 ; Sonnenfeld et al. , 2013 ）的源红移与透镜红移关系，数据汇编自Tan et al. ( 2024 )，以及来自AGEL巡天（Barone et al. , 2026 ）和PEARLS NEP时域场中JWST选择的透镜（Ferrami et al. , 2026 ）的最新发布结果。CRG的透镜解与现有强透镜参数空间非常吻合。右：SLACS、BELLS、SL2S、PEARLS NEP以及COWLS计划中超过400个候选引力透镜系统（Nightingale et al. , 2025 ）的爱因斯坦半径。假设CRG不是透镜，则无法在此参数空间的选择中将其区分，因为它与高排名和低排名的透镜候选者相似。

<small>Figure 7: Left: Source versus lens redshift for a sample of well-characterized, optically selected strong lensing systems (SLACS, BELLS, SL2S; Bolton et al. , 2008 ; Brownstein et al. , 2012 ; Sonnenfeld et al. , 2013 , respectively) as compiled in Tan et al. ( 2024 ) , along with a recent release of strong lenses from the AGEL survey (Barone et al. , 2026 ) and JWST-selected lenses in the PEARLS NEP time domain field (Ferrami et al. , 2026 ) . The lensing solution for the CRG is in excellent agreement with the existing parameter space for strong lenses. Right: Einstein radius for SLACS, BELLS, SL2S, PEARLS NEP, and over 400 candidate gravitationally lensed systems in the COWLS program (Nightingale et al. , 2025 ) . Assuming the CRG is not a lens, it cannot be distinguished from a selection in this parameter space, where it is similar to high-ranked and low-ranked lens candidates.</small>

表1：应用于CRG的五个孔径的bagpipes（Carnall et al. , 2018 ）测光拟合结果。我们针对沿环的三个主要恒星形成团块（A、B、C）、天体的中心以及总发射。上：测光红移自由变化。中：固定红移\(z=4.0148\)（来自光谱）。下：中心发射重新缩放以考虑微弱流量，其中测光红移允许在\(0<z<2\)之间变化。

We target the three main star-forming clumps (A, B, C) along the ring, the center of the object, and the total emission. Top : photometric redshift is allowed to vary freely. Middle : fixed redshift \(z=4.0148\) from spectroscopy. Bottom : central emission rescaled to account for faint flux, where photometric redshift is allowed to vary between \(0<z<2\) .</small>

### [70] [AGN Feedback and the Development of Dusty Multiphase Gas in X-ray Emitting Elliptical Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22415)
*Pasquale Temi,Francesco Ubertosi,Fabrizio Brighenti,Alexandros Maragkoudakis,Valeria Olivares,Alexandre Amblard,Massimo Gaspari,Myriam Gitti,Pamela M. Marcum,Kevin Fogarty,Alejandro S. Borlaff,William G. Mathews*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文聚焦于椭圆星系中尘埃、分子气体（CO）与热X射线气体的多相介质相互作用，并涉及ALMA和MUSE观测，与用户画像中的dust、molecular gas、ALMA、多相气体等关键词高度匹配。虽然研究对象是近邻椭圆星系而非高红移星系，但多相气体和尘埃演化是用户明确优先关注的领域，且论文方法（ALMA CO观测）与用户常用手段一致。

TL;DR: 研究小组中心椭圆星系中富含尘埃区域的物理和运动学特性，重点关注尘埃与热X射线气体的关系以及尘埃颗粒特征，发现AGN反馈驱动的外流在X射线空腔边缘促进冷尘埃气体凝结。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究椭圆星系中尘埃丰富区域的物理特性，特别是尘埃与热X射线发射气体之间的相互作用，以及尘埃颗粒在AGN反馈环境中的演化特征。

Method: 使用多波长数据综合分析，包括MUSE探测的H-alpha发射和ALMA探测的CO发射，结合X射线成像观测，研究尘埃云的物理和运动学特性。

Result: 发现含分子气体的尘埃区域优先位于X射线空腔边缘；分子和电离气体在动力学和空间上相互关联；尘埃、CO和H-alpha共存的区域表现出更小的Rv值，表明存在更小或演化程度较低的尘埃颗粒。

Conclusion: AGN驱动的外流在X射线空腔边缘促进冷尘埃气体凝结，形成多相介质环境；不同区域的Rv值差异反映了尘埃颗粒在不同环境中的演化状态，支持自上而下的凝结雨和混沌冷吸积框架。

Abstract: This paper investigates the physical and kinematic properties of dust-rich regions in a small sample of group-centered elliptical galaxies, emphasizing their connection with the hot X-ray emitting gas and detailed dust grain characteristics. Comprehensive multi-wavelength data, including H-alpha and CO emission detected by MUSE and ALMA, demonstrate the presence of dust clouds embedded within complex, hot X-ray atmospheres shaped by AGN feedback. X-ray images show bubbles and cavities surrounded by bright rims. We find that dust regions containing molecular gas traced by CO are preferentially located at the rims of these X-ray cavities, suggesting that AGN-driven outflows enhance the condensation of cold, dusty gas at these compressive interfaces. Kinematic measurements indicate that molecular and ionized gas phases are dynamically and spatially linked, supporting the framework of a multiphase medium arising from the top-down condensation rain in the hot plasma and related chaotic cold accretion. Crucially, spatial variations in the total-to-selective extinction ratio Rv show that regions where dust, CO, and H-alpha emission coincide exhibit notably smaller Rv values, implying steeper extinction curves and the predominance of smaller or less evolved dust grains within these mixed-phase environments. This contrasts with larger Rv values found elsewhere in the dust clouds, suggesting grain growth or survival mechanisms within shielded cold gas.

Abstract Translation:
本文研究了小样本群中心椭圆星系中富尘区域的物理和运动学特性，重点探讨了它们与热X射线发射气体及详细尘埃颗粒特征的联系。包括MUSE和ALMA探测到的Hα和CO发射在内的综合多波段数据表明，尘埃云嵌入由AGN反馈塑造的复杂热X射线大气中。X射线图像显示气泡和空腔被明亮边缘包围。我们发现，含有CO示踪分子气体的尘埃区域优先位于这些X射线空腔的边缘，表明AGN驱动的外流在这些压缩界面促进了冷尘埃气体的凝结。运动学测量表明，分子和电离气体相在动力学和空间上相互关联，支持了由热等离子体中的自上而下凝结雨及相关混沌冷吸积产生的多相介质框架。至关重要的是，总消光与选择性消光比Rv的空间变化表明，尘埃、CO和Hα发射重合的区域显示出显著较小的Rv值，意味着更陡的消光曲线以及在这些混合相环境中较小或演化程度较低的尘埃颗粒占主导地位。这与尘埃云其他区域发现的较大Rv值形成对比，表明在屏蔽的冷气体中存在颗粒生长或存活机制。

Conclusion Translation:
基于可用摘要的结论：AGN驱动的外流在X射线空腔边缘促进冷尘埃气体凝结，形成多相介质环境；不同区域的Rv值差异反映了尘埃颗粒在不同环境中的演化状态，支持自上而下的凝结雨和混沌冷吸积框架。

<small>Figure 5: MUSE H \(\alpha\) images of NGC 4636, NGC 5044, NGC 5813, and NGC 5846, with regions of strong dust absorption outlined by black solid lines. In NGC 4636 the highly extincted regions coincide with strong H \(\alpha\) emission; dusty region #2 overlaps with a CO cloud and shows enhanced \(A_{V}/A_{I}\) relative to dusty region #1. In NGC 5044 several resolved CO clouds lie within the central \(\sim\) 2 kpc and overlap with regions of strongly extincted light as well as with the H \(\alpha\) emission. Both NGC 5813 and NGC 5846 show a clear spatial correspondence between the knotty dust structures and the filamentary H \(\alpha\) emission.</small>

### [71] [A tight relation between the distribution of globular clusters and dark matter in AS1063](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.12332)
*J. M. Diego,C. Goolsby,C. J. Conselice,J. M. Palencia*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★★ (88/100) - 该论文研究星系团AS1063中球状星团分布与暗物质分布的关系，核心主题为引力透镜建模和暗物质示踪，与用户画像中的dark matter、gravitational lensing、lens、lensing、lensed高度匹配。用户明确优先强引力透镜研究，且论文使用JWST数据，与用户画像中的jwst关键词一致。虽然论文聚焦星系团而非用户偏好的星系-星系强透镜，但强透镜建模方法直接相关，且用户画像中dark matter权重很高。论文未涉及高红移星系动力学、运动学、偏振或多相气体等用户优先主题，但无负面因素。作者无匹配，但主题和方法契合度极高。

TL;DR: 基于JWST对AS1063星系团的深度高分辨率图像，研究人员识别出数万个点源，主要是球状星团和卫星星系核心，发现球状星团分布与引力透镜质量分布高度相关但更集中，提出球状星团可作为暗物质分布的示踪剂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究星系团中球状星团的分布特征，探索其与暗物质分布的关系，为在缺乏引力透镜约束的星系团中利用球状星团作为暗物质示踪剂提供可能性。

Method: 使用JWST深度高分辨率图像，仔细掩蔽伪影、扩展特征和背景星系后，在星系团中心区域识别数万个未分辨点源，扩展到1.18 Mpc范围；将球状星团分布与同一JWST数据推导的透镜模型质量分布进行比较分析。

Result: 发现球状星团分布与透镜质量分布存在非常紧密的相关性，但球状星团分布比暗物质更集中；通过简单平滑核可将离散点源分布转换为连续二维分布，与透镜收敛度匹配良好。

Conclusion: 球状星团可作为暗物质分布的示踪剂，特别是在引力透镜约束稀缺但球状星团易于探测的低红移星系团中，为研究暗物质分布提供了新方法。

Abstract: Based on deep high resolution JWST images of AS1063, and after a careful masking of artifacts, extended features in the cluster, and background galaxies (including known lensed ones), we have identified tens of thousands of unresolved point sources in the central region of the galaxy cluster. We extended the identification of these point sources up to 1.18 Mpc from the center of the cluster using data in the second module. Most of these sources are expected to be globular clusters orbiting in the deep potential well of the cluster, but also the surviving compact cores of satellite galaxies. We study the distribution of the globular clusters and compared it with the distribution of mass from a lens model derived from the same JWST data. We find a very tight correlation between the two distributions, but also some differences, including a more concentrated distribution for the globular clusters than for dark matter. We explored the possibility of using the distribution of globular clusters as a proxy for the lensing mass. We find that a simple smoothing kernel can transform the discrete distribution of point sources into a continuous two-dimensional distribution that matches well the lensing convergence. This suggests that globular clusters can be used as tracers of the dark matter distribution in other massive clusters where gravitational lensing constraints are scarce but globular clusters can be detected more easily, for instance in low redshift galaxy clusters.

Abstract Translation:
基于AS1063的深场高分辨率JWST图像，在仔细掩蔽伪影、星系团扩展特征以及背景星系（包括已知的透镜星系）后，我们在星系团中心区域识别了数万个未分辨的点源。利用第二个模块的数据，我们将这些点源的识别范围扩展到距星系团中心1.18 Mpc。这些源中大部分预计是在星系团深势阱中运行的球状星团，但也包括卫星星系幸存下来的致密核。我们研究了球状星团的分布，并将其与基于相同JWST数据推导的透镜模型的质量分布进行了比较。我们发现这两个分布之间存在非常紧密的相关性，但也存在一些差异，包括球状星团的分布比暗物质更集中。我们探索了利用球状星团分布作为透镜质量代理的可能性。我们发现，一个简单的平滑核可以将点源的离散分布转换为一个与透镜会聚度匹配良好的连续二维分布。这表明，在其他大质量星系团中，当引力透镜约束稀缺但球状星团更容易被探测到时（例如在低红移星系团中），球状星团可以作为暗物质分布的示踪剂。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，球状星团可作为暗物质分布的示踪剂，特别是在引力透镜约束稀缺但球状星团易于探测的低红移星系团中，为研究暗物质分布提供了新方法。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/x1.png)

图1：结合12个HST和JWST滤光片（范围0.4–5微米）的AS1063彩色图像。来自我们透镜模型的三条临界曲线显示在\(z=0.73\)（青色）、\(z=1.23\)（黄色）和\(z=3\)（红色）。黄色箭头标记了在\(z\approx 1.23\)处被该红移临界曲线相交的两组透镜星系，而青色箭头标记了来自\(z=0.73\)处一个星系的一组透镜图像，被青色临界曲线相交。白色圆圈标记了显著椭圆星系的位置。小图A、B、D和E显示了JWST短波滤光片之和的滤波版本的放大区域。黄色圆圈标记了滤波图像中自动检测到的点源位置。白色轮廓线表示不进行点源检测的掩蔽区域，除了最中心区域（图D），在该区域内在1角秒半径的掩蔽区域内通过目视识别点源。包含明亮和/或延展源以及伪影的整个区域的掩模显示在图C（右下角）。

<small>Figure 1: Color image of AS1063 combining 12 HST and JWST filters (range 0.4–5 micron). Three critical curves from our lens model are shown at \(z=0.73\) (cyan), \(z=1.23\) (yellow), and \(z=3\) (red). The yellow arrows mark two families of lensed galaxies at \(z\approx 1.23\) intersected by the critical curve at that redshift, while the cyan arrows mark one family of lensed images from a galaxy at \(z=0.73\) intersected by the cyan critical curve. White circles mark the position of prominent elliptical galaxies. The small panels A, B, D and E show zoomed-in regions of a filtered version of the sum of JWST’s SW filters. Yellow circles mark the position of automatically detected point sources in the filtered images. The white contours show the masked regions where no point source detection is performed except for the very central region (panel D) where identification of point sources is done visually inside the 1” radius masked region. The mask of the full region containing bright and/or extended sources as well as artifacts is shown in panel C (bottom right).</small>

#### Figure 2
![Figure 2](https://arxiv.org/html/Figs/GC_distribution.png)

图2：从数据（红点，28026个）和掩蔽区域内的修补（黑点，3501个）获得的球状星团分布图。一些伪影（衍射尖峰）和大型透镜星系（巨弧）在修补点的分布中很明显。大蓝色圆圈标记了显著成员的位置（图1中的白色圆圈）。

<small>Figure 2: Map of GC distribution obtained from the data (red points, 28026) and inpainted (black points, 3501) in the masked regions. Some artifacts (diffraction spikes) and large lensed galaxies (giant arcs) are obvious in the distribution of inpainted points. Big blue circles mark the position of prominent members (white circles in Fig. 1).</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/x2.png)

图3：球状星团数密度与在\(3\) 的盒子内计算的平均会聚度的关系。虚线对应\(y=0.4x^{0.7}\)，与观测到的相关性拟合得相当好。

<small>Figure 3: Number density of GCs vs mean convergence computed in boxes of \(3\) . The dashed line corresponds to \(y=0.4x^{0.7}\) and fits reasonably well the observed correlation.</small>

<small>Figure 4: Map of GC density after inpainting the masked regions (gray). The green contours are for the GC density map (gray scale image) while the cyan contours are for the lens model convergence map from paper-I. The two thicker cyan contours correspond to \(\kappa=0.3\) and \(\kappa=1.8\) .</small>

#### Figure 5
![Figure 5](https://arxiv.org/html/Figs/kappa_vs_density.png)

图5：会聚度与球状星团密度图的散点图。实线是\(x=y\) 模型。球状星团密度\(\rho_{gc}\) 已按因子\(\beta\) 重新缩放，该因子使差异图\(r=\kappa-\beta\times\rho_{gc}\) 的方差最小化。

<small>Figure 5: Scatter plot of convergence vs GC density maps. The solid line is the \(x=y\) model. The GC density, \(\rho_{gc}\) has been re-scaled by the factor \(\beta\) that minimizes the variance of the difference map \(r=\kappa-\beta\times\rho_{gc}\) .</small>
