#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.17766v2/x3.png)

图3：九个SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E PSB的CO SLED和激发比分布。左图显示由CO(2–1)和CO(5–4)跃迁（以及可用时的CO(4–3)）构建的CO SLED。SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E PSB以橙色圆圈显示（非探测以橙色阴影三角形显示），AGN J1448+1010以蓝色标出。我们与\(z\sim 1.25\)主序星系（黑色方块）和星暴星系（灰色方块）（Valentino et al., 2020）、银河系内盘（黑色虚线；Fixsen et al. 1999）、热化\(S_{CO}\propto J^{2}\)关系（灰色虚线）、来自Narayanan and Krumholz (2014)的覆盖\(\Sigma_{SFR}=0.1-10\,{M_{\odot}\,yr^{-1}\,kpc^{-2}}\)的模型激发序列（灰色曲线；虚线和点划线分别表示下界和上界），以及邻近的激波PSB系统NGC 1266（红色菱形；Alatalo et al. 2011；Pellegrini et al. 2013）进行比较。中图显示SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E PSB（J1448+1010以蓝色标出）和\(z\sim 1.25\)比较星系的\(L^{\prime}_{{CO(5-4)}}/L^{\prime}_{{CO(2-1)}}\)分布，右图显示相同样本的累积分布。单个非探测包含在直方图（橙色阴影条）和\(3\sigma\)极限的累积分布中；然而，AGN J1448+1010未包含在后者的累积分布中。总体而言，该样本主要由中等激发的CO SLED组成，在AGN宿主J1448+1010中有一个高激发异常值。

<small>Figure 3: CO SLEDs and excitation ratio distributions for the nine SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E PSBs. The left panel shows the CO SLEDs constructed from the CO(2–1) and CO(5–4) transitions (and CO(4–3) where available). The SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E PSBs are shown as orange circles (with the nondetection shown as an orange hatched triangle), with the AGN J1448+1010 outlined in blue. We compare to \(z\sim 1.25\) MS (black squares) and SB (gray squares) galaxies (Valentino et al. , 2020 ) , the Milky Way inner disk (black dashed line; Fixsen et al. 1999 ), the thermalized \(S_{CO}\propto J^{2}\) relation (dotted gray line), the model excitation sequence from Narayanan and Krumholz ( 2014 ) spanning \(\Sigma_{SFR}=0.1-10\,{M_{\odot}\,yr^{-1}\,kpc^{-2}}\) (gray curve; dashed and dashed-dotted lines represent lower and upper bounds, respectively), and the nearby shocked PSB system NGC 1266 (red diamonds; Alatalo et al. 2011 ; Pellegrini et al. 2013 ). The middle panel shows the distribution of \(L^{\prime}_{{CO(5-4)}}/L^{\prime}_{{CO(2-1)}}\) for the SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E PSBs (with J1448+1010 outlined in blue) and the \(z\sim 1.25\) comparison galaxies, while the right panel shows the cumulative distributions for the same samples. The single nondetection is included in the histogram (orange hatched bin) and the cumulative distribution at the \(3\sigma\) limit; however, the AGN J1448+1010 is not included in the latter. Overall, the sample is comprised of mostly moderate excitation CO SLEDs, with a single high excitation outlier in the AGN host J1448+1010.</small>

#### Figure 4
![Figure 4](https://arxiv.org/html/2602.17766v2/x4.png)

图4：左图显示\(L^{\prime}_{{CO(5-4)}}/L^{\prime}_{{CO(2-1)}}\)与总SFR的关系，显示了非被掩埋（白色圆圈）和被掩埋（橙色圆圈）的SFR估计值（Setton et al., 2025）。右图显示激发比与使用CO(5–4)源大小计算的\(\Sigma_{SFR}\)的关系（见表1）。如图3所示，AGN J1448+1010以蓝色标出。两个面板均包括来自Valentino et al. (2020)的\(z\sim 1.25\)主序星系（灰色方块）和星暴星系（黑色方块）以及激波PSB NGC 1266（红色菱形；Alatalo et al. 2011；Pellegrini et al. 2013；Alatalo 2015）作为参考。右图还显示了来自Valentino et al. (2020)的观测趋势和来自Narayanan and Krumholz (2014)的激发模型。黑色十字表示SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E天体的中位不确定度；对于SFR和\(\Sigma_{SFR}\)轴，实线和虚线分别表示被掩埋和非被掩埋值的不确定度。总之，在SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E PSB中，CO激发与总SFR或SFR面密度之间未观察到明显趋势，相反，所有系统均与少量到适度的恒星形成活动一致。

<small>Figure 4: The left panel shows \(L^{\prime}_{{CO(5-4)}}/L^{\prime}_{{CO(2-1)}}\) against total SFR, showing both the non-buried (white circles) and buried (orange circles) SFR estimates (Setton et al. , 2025 ) . In the right panel we show the excitation ratio versus \(\Sigma_{SFR}\) computed using CO(5–4) source sizes (see Table 1 ). As in Figure 3 , the AGN J1448+1010 is outlined in blue. Both panels include \(z\sim 1.25\) MS (gray squares) and SB (black squares) comparison galaxies from Valentino et al. ( 2020 ) and the shocked PSB NGC 1266 (red diamond; Alatalo et al. 2011 ; Pellegrini et al. 2013 ; Alatalo 2015 ) for reference. The right panel additionally shows the observed trend from Valentino et al. ( 2020 ) and the excitation model from Narayanan and Krumholz ( 2014 ) . Black crosses indicate median uncertainties for the SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E objects; for the SFR and \(\Sigma_{SFR}\) axes, solid and dashed bars indicate those for the buried and non-buried values, respectively. Together, no clear trend is observed between the CO excitation and both total or surface-density SFR for SQuIGG \(\vec{L}\) E PSBs, where instead all systems are consistent with little to modest star-forming activity.</small>

</details>


### [98] [The Little Blue and Red Dots Rosetta Stones: Non-Gaussian broad lines, hot dust, and X-ray weakness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22214)
*M. Brazzini,F. D'Eugenio,R. Maiolino,J. Lyu,C. DeCoursey,H. Übler,X. Ji,I. Juodžbalis,J. Scholtz,G. C. Jones,K. Hainline,E. Dalla Bontà,P. G. P érez-González,S. Geris,A. Harshan,C. Feruglio,M. Bischetti,G. Mazzolari,G. Rieke,S. Alberts,B. Trefoloni,S. Carniani,E. Parlanti,A. Marconi,G. Risaliti,C. Ramos Almeida,P. Rinaldi,M. Perna,S. Zamora,I. Lamperti,G. Venturi,G. Cresci,Andrew J. Bunker,L. R. Ivey*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★☆ (85/100) - 该论文研究JWST发现的AGN（红点和蓝点），涉及尘埃、稠密气体、宽线轮廓等，与用户Zotero画像中的dust、dense gas、JWST等关键词高度匹配。作者中包含用户核心作者hannah übler和g c jones，且论文主题属于高红移活动星系核研究，与用户对高红移星系动力学和气体的兴趣有较强关联。虽然论文主要聚焦AGN而非强引力透镜，但用户画像中明确包含AGN相关关键词，且论文涉及的高红移气体性质与用户兴趣方向一致。

TL;DR: JWST新发现的AGN分为红点和蓝点两类，它们具有独特的性质，不同于本地I型AGN和高红移类星体。两类天体共享标准I型AGN的核心引擎，但在周围稠密气体分布、几何结构和吸积特性上存在差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST新发现的AGN表现出特殊性质，需要理解这些"小点"天体（红点和蓝点）的本质特征，以及它们与标准AGN的异同，从而揭示早期宇宙中AGN的物理机制。

Method: 通过比较两类原型的代表性天体（红罗塞塔石GN-28074和蓝罗塞塔石GS-3073），分析其光谱特征、X射线辐射、中红外发射、激发诊断和吸收特征等观测数据。

Result: 两类天体都显示指数型巴尔末线轮廓、极弱X射线辐射、强[OIII] 4363发射、弱热尘埃中红外发射且无时间变异性。主要差异在于：蓝罗塞塔石有强HeII 4686发射（窄线和宽线成分），而红罗塞塔石未检测到；红罗塞塔石有显著的巴尔末吸收线，表明视线方向存在极稠密气体。

Conclusion: LRDs和LBDs共享标准I型AGN的核心引擎，但在围绕吸积盘的稠密气体数量、几何结构以及吸积特性上存在差异。这些差异可能反映了不同的物理环境或演化阶段。

Abstract: The population of Active Galactic Nuclei (AGN) newly discovered by the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) exhibits peculiar properties that distinguish it from both local type I AGN and high-redshift quasars. Most of these sources are compact, appearing as 'little dots': among them, the sub-class (10-30% of the total) characterized by significantly red optical colors has been named 'Little Red Dots' (LRDs), while here we analogously introduce the term 'Little Blue Dots' (LBDs) for the remaining, bluer sources (70-90%). We then present a comparative analysis of the prototypical representatives ('Rosetta Stones') of the two classes: GN-28074 at z=2.26, the Red Rosetta Stone, and GS-3073 at z=5.55, the Blue Rosetta Stone. In both Rosetta Stones the broad Balmer lines are better described by exponential profiles rather than single Gaussians, similarly to normal low-redshift type I AGN, indicating that exponential profiles are not unique to LRDs. They are both extremely X-ray weak, show strong auroral [OIII] 4363 emission, weak hot dust mid-IR emission, and no time variability. However, they differ in terms of excitation diagnostics: the HeII 4686 line is undetected in the Red Rosetta but strongly detected in the Blue Rosetta in both narrow and broad components, with the latter much broader than hydrogen Balmer lines. This supports BLR stratification and disfavors the cocoon electron-scattering scenario. An additional difference is the presence of prominent Balmer absorption in the Red Rosetta -- indicative of extremely dense gas along the line of sight -- but absent in the Blue Rosetta. Taken together, these results suggest that LRDs and LBDs share the same central engine as standard type I AGN, while differing in the amount and geometry of dense gas surrounding the accretion disk, and/or in their accretion properties.

Abstract Translation:
詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（JWST）新发现的活动星系核（AGN）群体展现出与本地I型AGN和高红移类星体均不同的奇特性质。这些源大多致密，呈现为“小点”：其中，具有显著红色光学颜色的子类（占总数的10-30%）被命名为“小红点”（LRDs），而此处我们类比地引入术语“小蓝点”（LBDs）来指代其余更蓝的源（70-90%）。随后，我们对这两个类别的典型代表（“罗塞塔石碑”）进行了比较分析：红罗塞塔石碑——红移z=2.26的GN-28074，以及蓝罗塞塔石碑——红移z=5.55的GS-3073。在两个罗塞塔石碑中，宽巴尔默线用指数轮廓而非单一高斯轮廓描述得更好，这与正常的低红移I型AGN类似，表明指数轮廓并非LRDs所独有。它们都极其X射线弱，显示出强烈的极光[OIII] 4363发射、微弱的热尘埃中红外发射，并且没有时间变化。然而，它们在激发诊断方面存在差异：HeII 4686线在红罗塞塔中未被探测到，但在蓝罗塞塔的窄成分和宽成分中均被强烈探测到，且后者比氢巴尔默线宽得多。这支持了宽线区（BLR）的分层结构，并否定了茧状电子散射情景。另一个差异是红罗塞塔中存在显著的巴尔默吸收——表明沿视线方向存在极其致密的气体——而蓝罗塞塔中则没有。综合这些结果，表明LRDs和LBDs与标准I型AGN共享相同的中央引擎，但在围绕吸积盘的致密气体数量、几何结构以及/或它们的吸积特性上有所不同。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，LRDs和LBDs共享标准I型AGN的核心引擎，但在围绕吸积盘的稠密气体数量、几何结构以及吸积特性上存在差异。这些差异可能反映了不同的物理环境或演化阶段。

### [99] [Caught in Swallowtails: Discovery of Two Swallowtail Image Formations in MS 0451.6-0305](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.10097)
*Ashish K. Meena,Wenlei Chen,Lukas J. Furtak,Johan Richard,Adi Zitrin,Jose M. Diego,Mathilde Jauzac,Patrick L. Kelly,Rogier A. Windhorst*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★☆ (85/100) - 该论文直接涉及强引力透镜中的高阶焦散结构（swallowtail caustics），与用户的核心领域‘强引力透镜’高度吻合。论文利用JWST观测高红移星系（z=2.91和z=6.70）的亚结构，放大倍数极高，与用户对高红移星系动力学、亚结构及JWST的强烈兴趣一致。虽然无核心作者，但主题和方法匹配度极高。

TL;DR: JWST观测发现MS 0451.6-0305星系团后方存在两个燕子尾状引力透镜系统（z=2.91和z=6.70），首次在单个星系团中观测到多个高阶燕子尾透镜形态，能够将亚秒差距尺度的星系亚结构放大数百倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高阶引力透镜效应，特别是燕子尾状透镜形态，以探测高红移星系中的亚秒差距尺度结构，了解早期宇宙中星系的形成和演化过程。

Method: 使用JWST-NIRCam成像观测MS 0451.6-0305星系团，识别复杂的透镜图像形态，通过详细的透镜建模分析高阶燕子尾状透镜配置，计算放大倍数和有效半径。

Result: 发现两个燕子尾状透镜系统：z=2.91系统产生四重成像弧，点源放大倍数≥300，透镜校正有效半径≤0.8-1.5 pc；z=6.70系统放大倍数20-200，有效半径≤0.8-18.5 pc。这是首次在单个星系团中观测到多个燕子尾透镜形态。

Conclusion: 燕子尾状透镜能够将亚秒差距尺度的星系亚结构放大数百倍，为研究从中间红移到宇宙最初十亿年的星系形成提供了新的观测手段，展示了高阶引力透镜在探测早期宇宙精细结构中的强大能力。

Abstract: We report the discovery of two swallowtail image formations at $z=2.91$ and $z=6.70$ behind the galaxy cluster MS 0451.6-0305 in JWST-NIRCam imaging. We find that in both of the above lensed systems, the complex image morphology cannot be reproduced by simple fold/cusp caustics, and detailed lens modeling reveals higher-order swallowtail caustic configurations. In the $z=2.91$ lens system, a small part of the source galaxy (which itself is part of a galaxy group) containing atleast two compact knots sits inside the swallowtail caustic, producing a quadruply imaged arc. At two of the image positions of these knots, we infer point source magnifications of $\gtrsim 300$, implying lensing-corrected effective radii of $\lesssim 0.8-1.5$ pc. The $z=6.70$ system exhibits even more complex image formation. We therefore only use the most confidently identified counter-images of knots in this system as constraints in our lens modeling. The resulting model predicts magnifications $\sim20-200$ and lensing-corrected effective radii of $\lesssim 0.8-18.5$ pc for various knots. Together, these two systems represent the first example of observations of multiple swallowtail image formations in a single galaxy cluster and demonstrate the ability of swallowtail caustics to magnify individual substructures at sub-parsec scales, from intermediate redshifts to the first billion years of the Universe.

Abstract Translation:
我们报告在JWST-NIRCam成像中，于星系团MS 0451.6-0305后方红移$z=2.91$和$z=6.70$处发现两个燕子尾图像构型。我们发现，在上述两个透镜系统中，复杂的图像形态无法用简单的折叠/尖点焦散线重现，详细的透镜建模揭示了高阶燕子尾焦散线构型。在$z=2.91$透镜系统中，源星系（其本身是一个星系群的一部分）的一小部分包含至少两个致密节点，位于燕子尾焦散线内部，产生了一个四重成像的弧。在这些节点的两个图像位置，我们推断点源放大率$\gtrsim 300$，这意味着透镜校正的有效半径$\lesssim 0.8-1.5$ pc。$z=6.70$系统展现出更为复杂的图像构型。因此，我们仅使用该系统中最可靠识别的节点反像作为透镜建模的约束。所得模型预测各节点的放大率$\sim20-200$，透镜校正的有效半径$\lesssim 0.8-18.5$ pc。这两个系统共同代表了在单个星系团中观测到多个燕子尾图像构型的首个实例，并展示了燕子尾焦散线将亚秒差距尺度的单个子结构从中间红移放大到宇宙最初十亿年的能力。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要，燕子尾状透镜能够将亚秒差距尺度的星系亚结构放大数百倍，为研究从中间红移到宇宙最初十亿年的星系形成提供了新的观测手段，展示了高阶引力透镜在探测早期宇宙精细结构中的强大能力。

Key Figures:

#### Figure 1
![Figure 1](https://arxiv.org/html/MS0451_color_cc.jpeg)

图1: MS0451 ( \(z=0.55\) ) 星系团的JWST假彩色图像 ( \(R={F356W+F444W}\) , \(G={F200W+F277W}\) , \(B={F115W+F150W}\) )。黄色曲线显示了红移 \(z=6.70\) 源对应的临界曲线，对应于Zitrin-Analytic透镜模型。透镜图像用细的绿色虚线圆圈圈出，其位置进一步用绿色箭头突出显示。我们没有标记系统10.1至10.5，因为它们彼此非常接近。系统19中的节点也因相同原因未标记。系统10和19均对应燕子尾图像构型。有关这些弧的放大视图，请参阅下面的图3和图4。

The green and red points show the spectroscopic and photometric cluster members, respectively. The cluster red sequence is shown in the gray shaded region. The vertical dashed curve highlights the limiting magnitude for cluster members selected using the red sequence analysis.</small>

#### Figure 3
![Figure 3](https://arxiv.org/html/z2p9_image_rgb.jpeg)

图3: 红移 \(z=2.91\) 处的燕子尾图像构型。左图显示了星系团的假彩色图像，蓝色和黄色虚线分别代表 \(z=2.85\) 和 \(z_{s}=2.91\) 的临界曲线。四重成像的节点用彩色箭头标记。中图显示了相应的放大率图，不同颜色（与左图中箭头颜色相同）的星形标记了四重成像节点的观测位置。右图显示了源平面中相应的焦散线结构。蓝色和黑色的实线和虚线分别显示了 \(z=2.85\) 和 \(z=2.91\) 处的切向和径向临界焦散线，展示了靠近源位置的焦散线演化。三颗星形显示了左图和中间图中多像系统的质心源位置。三个内嵌面板显示了每个源位置附近区域的放大视图。请注意，右图中的比例尺显示了源平面中的本征距离。

<small>Figure 3: Swallowtail image formation at \(z=2.91\) . Left panel shows the false color image of the cluster with blue and yellow dashed curves representing the critical curve for \(z=2.85\) and \(z_{s}=2.91\) , respectively. The quadruply imaged knots are marked by colored arrows. Middle panel represents the corresponding magnification map with different colored (same as the arrow colors in the left panel) stars marking the observed positions of the quadruply imaged knots. Right panel shows the corresponding caustic structure in the source plane. The solid and dashed curves in blue and black show tangential and radial critical caustics at \(z=2.85\) and \(z=2.91\) , respectively, showing the evolution of caustics close to the source position(s). The three stars show the barycenter source position for the multiple image systems shown in the left and middle panels. The three inset panels display a zoomed-in view of the regions near each source position. Note that the scale in the right panel shows the proper distance in the source plane.</small>

<small>Figure 4: Swallowtail image formation at \(z=6.70\) . Left panel shows the false color image of the cluster with yellow dashed curves representing the critical curve for \(z_{s}=6.70\) . Different systems and knots are shown in different colors. We note that 19.K1/K2/K3/K4/K5 are not counter-images of each other; instead, they are individual knots. See Sec. VI for more details. Middle panel shows the corresponding magnification map with different colored (same color scheme as the left panel) stars representing the observed positions of the different knots. Right panel shows the caustic structure in the source plane with solid and dashed curves representing the tangential and radial caustics, respectively. The stars indicate the barycenter position of different multiple-image systems shown in the left panel. Note that the scale in the right panel shows the proper distance in the source plane.</small>

### [100] [The early Universe with JWST and ALMA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.04314)
*Rodrigo Herrera-Camus,Natascha Förster Schreiber,Livia Vallini,Rychard Bouwens,John D. Silverman*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

Recommendation: ★★★★☆ (85/100) - 该论文是一篇关于JWST和ALMA在早期宇宙星系研究中的综述，主题与用户兴趣画像高度匹配，特别是JWST、ALMA、星际介质、尘埃等关键词。论文作者中包含用户核心作者列表中的Natascha Förster Schreiber和Rodrigo Herrera-Camus，作者匹配度高。论文内容涉及高红移星系的星际介质、运动学、形态等，与用户偏好的高红移星系动力学和运动学方向一致。虽然是一篇综述而非原创研究，但其综合性和前沿性仍具有较高参考价值。

TL;DR: ALMA和JWST联合观测正在革新我们对早期宇宙星系形成的理解，通过高分辨率研究星系的气体、尘埃、恒星、运动学等特性，揭示了宇宙最初十亿年星系的复杂演化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ALMA和JWST的协同观测能力为研究早期宇宙星系提供了前所未有的机会，能够从空间分辨尺度上探索高红移星系的星际介质、运动学、形态、活动星系核和恒星形成活动等复杂特性。

Method: 结合ALMA和JWST的观测能力，通过多波长观测获取高红移星系的气体、尘埃和恒星信息，同时整合理论模型和数值模拟来理解早期星系演化。

Result: 研究总结了宇宙最初十亿年星系研究的最新突破，包括关键发现、未解问题和当前限制，展示了这些观测如何改变我们对早期星系演化的理解。

Conclusion: 虽然现有设施和合作努力可以取得显著进展，但未来需要更高的角分辨率和灵敏度，这要求升级现有仪器并开发下一代天文台，以推动早期星系演化研究的进一步发展。

Abstract: The Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array and the James Webb Space Telescope are transforming our understanding of galaxy formation and evolution in the early Universe. By combining their capabilities, these observatories provide unprecedented insights into the gas, dust, and stars of high-redshift galaxies at spatially resolved scales, unveiling the complexities of their interstellar medium, kinematics, morphology, active galactic nuclei, and star formation activity. This review summarizes recent breakthroughs in the study of galaxies during the first billion years of cosmic history, highlighting key discoveries, open questions, and current limitations. We discuss how observations, theoretical models, and simulations are shaping our understanding of early galaxy evolution and identify promising directions for future research. While significant progress can be achieved through optimized use of existing facilities and collaborative efforts, further advances will require enhanced angular resolution and sensitivity, motivating upgrades to current instruments and the development of next-generation observatories.

Abstract Translation:
阿塔卡马大型毫米/亚毫米阵列和詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜正在改变我们对早期宇宙中星系形成和演化的理解。通过结合它们的能力，这些天文台在空间分辨尺度上提供了对高红移星系中气体、尘埃和恒星的前所未有的洞察，揭示了它们星际介质、运动学、形态、活动星系核和恒星形成活动的复杂性。本综述总结了宇宙历史最初十亿年星系研究的最新突破，突出了关键发现、未解问题和当前局限性。我们讨论了观测、理论模型和模拟如何塑造我们对早期星系演化的理解，并指出了未来研究的有前景方向。虽然通过优化利用现有设施和合作努力可以取得显著进展，但进一步的进展需要更高的角分辨率和灵敏度，这要求升级现有仪器并开发下一代天文台。

Conclusion Translation:
基于现有摘要：虽然现有设施和合作努力可以取得显著进展，但未来需要更高的角分辨率和灵敏度，这要求升级现有仪器并开发下一代天文台，以推动早期星系演化研究的进一步发展。
